# 2.5 Interactions with other Components

## 2.5.0-1 Interactions with other Components Management of requests towards 5G-L1-DL and 5G-L1-UL subcells (ID: 11177858)

**2.5.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11177868`)

Interactions with other Components 5G-L2-PS ensures that no requests (5G_UP_ALG_4665_replaced([11192609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvlyp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) are sent towards DL subcells with subcellId values that are not configured within PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Although the maximum value of subcellId for DL subcells is defined in 5G_UP_1854_replaced([11375881](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueQLJvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), it can happen that less than maximum number of subcells is configured.

5G-L2-PS also ensures that no requests (5G_UP_ALG_5135_replaced([11204062](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwi05vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) are sent towards UL subcells with subcellId values that are not configured within PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Although the maximum value of subcellId for UL subcells is defined in 5G_UP_1859_replaced([11375909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueQLKvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), it can happen that less than maximum number of subcells is configured.

[CB008985-A] When supercell mode is enabled (numOfSuperSubcells >= 2) L2 PS shall ensure that each request is sent to the respective 5G-L1 subcell with 5G-L1-DL subcellId or 5G-L1-UL subcellId value the SSB (beamId) is associated to. There is a mapping for supercell between beamId and pair of 5G-L1-DL subcellId and 5G-L1-UL subcellId of given 5G-L1 subcell, refer to 5G_UP_1851_replaced([11375846](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ueQLIfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB008985-A]

---

## 2.5.1 Interactions with L1-DL

### 2.5.1.0-2 Interactions with L1-DL L1-DL Message split between ABIL/FPGA and following HW Variant (ID: 11177882)

**2.5.1.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13400734`)

Interactions with L1-DL The following DlData_* messages:

  * DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq
  * DlData_PdschSendReq
  * DlData_CsiRsSendReq
  * DlData_PdcchSendReq
  * DlData_SsBlockSendReq



are separated between ABIL/FPGA and following HW variants (ABIO, ABIP [CB014419-SR-EB] , ABIR [End CB014419-SR-EB]).

The reason is that FPGA on ABIL has reached its hardware limits and cannot support any further adaptation of the L1-L2 Interface.

ABIL/FPGA messages will be renamed adding the suffix “Loner”:

  * DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReqLoner
  * DlData_PdschSendReqLoner
  * DlData_CsiRsSendReqLoner
  * DlData_PdcchSendReqLoner
  * DlData_SsBlockSendReqLoner



while ABIO/ABIP [CB014419-SR-EB] /ABIR [End CB014419-SR-EB] messages will be renamed adding the suffix “L1sw”:

  * DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReqL1sw
  * DlData_PdschSendReqL1sw
  * DlData_CsiRsSendReqL1sw
  * DlData_PdcchSendReqL1sw
  * DlData_SsBlockSendReqL1sw



Throughout this module these messages are referred by the name without suffix.

---

### 2.5.1.1 General Exceptions on the DlData Interface

#### 2.5.1.1.0-1 General Exceptions on the DlData Interface Expected Exceptions (ID: 11177896)

**2.5.1.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11177899`)

General Exceptions on the DlData Interface 5G-L2-PS may send out a limited amount of send request messages late, such that L1-DL receives them after the closure of the L1 receive window. The L1 receive window for send request messages is defined in 5G_L1_IF_123_replaced([11513234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRvTmfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In the sequel, message X is a placeholder for exactly 1 of the following message names:

  * DlData_SlotTypeReq (5G_L1_IF_43_replaced([11512351](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRol6_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * DlData_PatternConfigReq (5G_L1_IF_54_replaced([11512418](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRpM9_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * DlData_SsBlockSendReq (5G_L1_IF_63_replaced([11512469](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRpNAfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * DlData_PdcchSendReq (5G_L1_IF_70_replaced([11512527](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRqbEfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * DlData_PdschSendReq (5G_L1_IF_79_replaced([11512684](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpMfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * DlData_PdschPayloadTbSendReq (5G_L1_IF_79_replaced([11512684](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpMfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * DlData_CsiRsSendReq (5G_L1_IF_98_replaced([11513023](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRtecvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * DlData_RimRsSendReq (5G_L1_IF_14804_replaced([11513122](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRusgvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))



5G-L2-PS shall obey the following rules:

  * During a time span of 5 slots after processing a PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), a PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq (5G_L2_IF_220_replaced([10970911](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UlnW_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or a PsCell_CellDeleteReq (5G_L2_IF_179_replaced([10970510](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UjLHPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) 5G-L2-PS may send messages X late in any cell deployed on the same CPU core.



Rationale:

Cell procedures are not running in the background and take multiple slots to be completed. During the first slots after a cell procedure 5G-L2-PS has to process tasks which piled up during the procedure, thus message transmissions towards L1-DL can be delayed.

  * When the above time span has ended, the number of late messages X in a cell shall not exceed 1% of all messages X sent in the same cell within any given time interval of 1 second.



Rationale:

5G-L2-PS can send request messages to L1-DL only after UE scheduling. Since the processing time needed for UE scheduling in a certain slot can't be predicted, it is unavoidable that request messages are sent out late from time to time, in particular when the load on 5G-L2-PS is high.

Also, the message propagation delay on the L1-L2 interface is variable and not exactly known to 5G-L2-PS.

Note: L1-DL drops request messages which it receives after the message receive window and it doesn't perform the corresponding requests.

#### 2.5.1.5.2 Sending DlData_PdcchSendReq for UL DCI

##### 2.5.1.5.2.0-1 Sending DlData_PdcchSendReq for UL DCI UL DCI (ID: 11178031)

**2.5.1.5.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11178037`)

Sending DlData_PdcchSendReq for UL DCI UL DCI - Non specific setting

---

**2.5.1.5.2.0-1.0-1.0-6**  (ID: `11178122`)

Sending DlData_PdcchSendReq for UL DCI UL DCI Transmission Request to L1-DL

Each UL PDCCH Scheduler which allocates a UL DCI shall send a DlData_PdcchSendReq message to the L1-DL instance handling the corresponding subcell to request the transmission of the DCI.

For the details of DlData_PdcchSendReq message content and timing: see 5G_L1_5G21A_70 and 5G_L1_5G21A_121.

The IE rnti is filled according to the configured C-RNTI of the UE or to the temporary RNTI for Msg3 HARQ retransmission.

In case of DCI for CG Activation, CG deactivation or CG ReTransmission or CG Modification

  * the IE rnti = CS-RNTI
  * the IE dciScramblingRnti = C-RNTI



The IE startCce and aggregation level are filled according to the allocation (5G_UP_ALG_4426_replaced([11170801](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_4055_replaced([11170246](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt9a9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) respectively).

startSymbolNumber shall be set according to the UE specific search space configured in the PDCCH token allocated to the UL scheduler as per 5G_UP_ALG_2448_replaced([11170221](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt9a8fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) to be checked - see 5G_UP_ALG_4474_replaced([11171714](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuGk5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

The IE dmrsScramblingSequenceInt ([image-0][image_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_5613.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]in 38.211) shall be set to the physical cell ID (physCellId in PsCell_CellSetupReq).

The IE dmrsScramblingSequenceInt is set according to the coreset and search space used to send the DCI:

 If the CORESET(0) is used, the IE is set to the physCellId defined at the cell setup ([image-1][image_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_5613.002.png[/image_path][/image-1]in 38.211).

 For other CORESETs:

 If the search space is a common search space, the IE is set to the physCellId defined at the cell setup.

 If the search space is a UE-Specific search space, the IE is set to the ueSssDmrsScramblingId associated to the CORESET and received in the in the PsCell_CellSetupReq.

The Information Elements (IE) dmrsScramblingSequenceInt and dciScramblingSequenceInit are set according to the coreset and search space used to send the DCI:

 If the CORESET(0) is used, the IEs above are set to the physCellId defined at the cell setup ([image-2][image_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_5613.003.png[/image_path][/image-2]in 38.211).

 For other CORESETs:

 If the search space is a common search space, the dciScramblingSequenceInit is set to the physCellId and the dmrsScramblingSequenceInt is set to ueSssDmrsScramblingId.

 If the search space is a UE-Specific search space, the dmrsScramblingSequenceInt and dciScramblingSequenceInit are set to the ueSssDmrsScramblingId associated to the CORESET and received in the in the PsCell_CellSetupReq.

The IE dmrsScramblingSequenceInt and dciScramblingSequenceInit are set for CG Deactivation with same conditions for a CSS and coreset explained above since search space = type3

The IE dciPayload is set to the generated DCI.

The IE dciPayload for format 0_1:

'antennaPort' field value is calculated according to the UL rank during CG Activation or CG Modification and cdmGroupNoData which is 2 or a calculated value {1,2} in CG Modification

The IE dciSize is set according to the size of the DCI (see 5G_UP_ALG_4930_replaced([11198773](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwKaa_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_4935_replaced([11198812](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwLBc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The IEs nShiftModNumOfRegBundles, interleaverRows are not applicable when the cceRegMappingType is set to non-interleaved. Not applicable means that L1 will ignore these fields.

For DL DCI transmitted in the UE dedicated bandwidth part, the IE precoderGranularity shall be set to "regBundleSize".

For UL DCI transmitted on Coreset#0, whatever is the active bandwidth Part, the Coreset configuration is defined in 5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) using the commonControlResourceSet[0]. The IEs coresetFreqDomain, cceRegMappingType, interleaverRows, regBundleSize shall be set accordingly. The IE numOfSymbols shall be set to coresetDuration. In addition the dmrsReferencePoint shall be set to coresetStartPRB to be compliant with 5G_UP_IF_728_replaced([11504330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tSmnrvv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). UL DCI transmitted over Coreset#0 corresponds to grant for Msg3 retransmission.

For UL DCI transmitted on Coreset#0,coresetFreqDomainRbShift shall also be set according to coreset configuration defined in 5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) .

For UL DCI transmitted on Coreset#0, nShiftModNumOfRegBundles = nShift mod{ rrmNumOfPRBinCoreset * numOfSymbols / regBundleSize }

with:

nShift is included in commonControlResourceSet[0] in PsCell_CellSetupReq.

rrmNumOfPRBinCoreset is the number of ‘1’ bits in the bitmap coresetFreqDomain multiply by 6.

numOfSymbols is set according to 5G_UP_IF_636_replaced([11502317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tSfS6vv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (N_symb^CORESET parameter).

For UL DCI transmitted on Coreset different from Coreset#0, the IE coresetFreqDomain is set according to the value received in UE setup (5G_L2_IF_389_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The IEs cceRegMappingType, nterleaverRows, regBundleSize shall be set according to value received in 5G_L2_IF_389_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). In addition, the dmrsReferencePoint shall be set to pointA to be compliant with 5G_UP_IF_728_replaced([11504330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tSmnrvv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

{For UL DCI transmitted in the UE specific search space in the UE dedicated BWP, the IE coresetFreqDomain, cceRegMappingType, interleaverRows, regBundleSize shall be set according to the values configured for the BWP with cellBwpId that is associated with initialUeActiveBwpId, see 5G_UP_ALG_17939_replaced([11110885](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpIlUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).}

For UL DCI transmitted with a Coreset different from Coreset#0 ,coresetFreqDomainRbShift is set to 0.

[Before CNI-96927]

For UL DCI transmitted with a Coreset different from Coreset#0, nShiftModNumOfRegBundles = nShift mod{ rrmNumOfPRBinCoreset * numOfSymbols / regBundleSize }

with:

nShift is included in controlResourceSet in PsUser_UserSetupReq.

rrmNumOfPRBinCoreset is the number of ‘1’ bits in the bitmap coresetFreqDomain multiply by 6.

numOfSymbols is set according to 5G_UP_IF_638_replaced([11502627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tSfS7_v1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (N_symb^CORESET parameter).

[CNI-96927]

For UL DCI transmitted with a Coreset different from Coreset#0, nShiftModNumOfRegBundles is set to 0.

[End CNI-96927]

For analog beamforming for eCPRI RUs, L2 PS shall indicate beam of the corresponding UE through numCeAxCIndex and ceAxcIndex and patternId in DlData_PdcchSendReq according to 5G_L1_5G21A_73 as

numCeAxCIndex number of eAxC index for D2 subcell type according to 5G_L1_5G21A_868.

ceAxcIndex eAxC index of default data for D2 subcell type according to 5G_L1_5G21A_868 and 5G_UP_ALG_22399_replaced([11193226](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvqrJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

patternId map beam Id to pattern Id according to 5G_UP_ALG_1909_replaced([11111524](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOE7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

When supercell mode is enabled (numOfSuperSubcells >= 2) L2 PS shall set patternId to 0 in DlData_PdcchSendReq.

---

**2.5.1.5.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11178127`)

Sending DlData_PdcchSendReq for UL DCI UL DCI and Transport Block Receive Request with carrier aggregation

---

**2.5.1.5.2.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11178132`)

Sending DlData_PdcchSendReq for UL DCI 5G-L2-PS shall send DlData_PdcchSendReq to 5G-L1-DL for the subcells that are allocated to the UE in the FD scheduling (see 5G_UP_ALG_5055_replaced([11201947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwa5E_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). This message is not sent for the subcells that are not allocated.

---

**2.5.1.5.2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11178138`)

Sending DlData_PdcchSendReq for UL DCI UL DCI - FDD Specific setting

---

**2.5.1.5.2.0-1.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13392578`)

Sending DlData_PdcchSendReq for UL DCI [Before CB007372-A]

**Need to check remaining IEs**

**FDD-specific settings for UL DCI Transmission Request to L1-DL**

This requirement defines IEs of the DlData_PdcchSendReq that are specific for FDD. Parameters that are not mentioned here are assumed to be common with TDD, defined in 5G_L2_10888_replaced([11178037](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26-IjPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For a FDD carrier with 5MHz bandwidth, the IE startSymbolNumber shall be set to '0'.

For FDD on a carrier shared with LTE, IE startSymbolNumber shall be set to '2'.

For the initial UL BWP, CORESET#0 with 24PRB bandwidth on 5MHz and 48PRBs on 10, 15 and 20MHz is configured.

For UE dedicated DL BWP, CORESET configuration coresetFreqDomain, cceRegMappingType, interleaverRows, regBundleSize shall be set according to the values configured for cellBwpId that is associated with initialUeActiveBwpId, see 5G_UP_ALG_17939_replaced([11110885](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpIlUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The same settings for IE startSymbolNumber are used for 10MHz and 15MHz and for 20MHz bandwidths.

For UL DCI transmitted in the UE dedicated bandwidth;**numOfSymbols is set according to the coresetDuration (5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) )**

For FDD on a carrier shared with LTE, numOfSymbols is set to '1'.

For a FDD carrier with 5MHz bandwidth and aggregation level set to Agg4, the 64-bit IE coresetFreqDomain is set to "0xF000 0000 0000 0000".

Note: This bit-mapping results in RRC IE frequencyDomainResources set to "0x1E00 0000 0000" .

For FDD carrier with 10MHz or 15MHz and slot type B4 with 2 PDCCH symbols, the 64-bit IE coresetFreqDomain in 5G_L2_IF_93_replaced([10968323](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UXk5fu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is set to "0xFF00 0000 0000 0000".

Note: Those bitmaps result from a hardcoded allocation of the CORESET for L1/L2 FDD starting the allocation of 4 consecutive CCEs at PRB0. The logic is given by the comment in 36.331.v15.0.1:

_\-- Frequency domain resources for the CORESET. Each bit corresponds a group of 6 RBs, with grouping starting from PRB 0, which is fully_

_\-- contained in the bandwidth part within which the CORESET is configured._

_\-- The most significant bit corresponds to the group of lowest frequency which is fully contained in the bandwidth part within which the_

_\-- CORESET is configured, each next subsequent lower significance bit corresponds to the next lowest frequency group fully contained within_

_\-- the bandwidth part within which the CORESET is configured, if any._

_\-- Bits corresponding to a group not fully contained within the bandwidth part within which the CORESET is configured are set to zero._

_\-- Corresponds to L1 parameter 'CORESET-freq-dom'(see 38.211, section 7.3.2.2) frequencyDomainResources BIT STRING (SIZE (45))_

For FDD on a carrier shared with LTE with 10MHz**as well as with 15Mhz and 20MHz**

**As per 5G_UP_ALG_3935_replaced([11168314](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktvYg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), only CORESET#1 in dedicated BWP will be used by L2PS.**

  * the IE coresetFreqDomain for the common PDCCH shall be set according the parameter settings in 5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * the IE coresetFreqDomain for the dedicated PDCCH shall be set according the parameter settings in 5G_L2_IF_389_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_L2_IF_408_replaced([10975247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Dfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



For**NSA the requirements above introduced for 5GC000836-D continue to apply, also for 10MHz and 15MHz bandwidth. Only Msg2 and Msg3 are sent on CCCH and only one UE is scheduled per slot on a FDD carrier, so msg3 ReTxand UL user data are never scheduled in the same slot.**

The same settings for IE cceRegMappingType are used for 10MHz and 15MHz bandwidths.

For 5/10/15 MHz**as well as for 20MHz**

the Coreset configuration is defined in

  * 5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), structure IE commonControlResourceSet[numOfCommonControlResourceSets] for Common Search Space of both Initial BWP and dedicated BWP.
  * 5G_L2_IF_389_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) resp. 5G_L2_IF_408_replaced([10975247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Dfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UE Specific Search Space (UE SSS) of dedicated BWP.



(Note: UE SSS of initial BWP is not utilized.)

The same settings for the IEs cceRegMappingType, interleaverRows, regBundleSize, numOfSymbols and dmrsReferencePoint as defined for TDD in 5G_L2_10447_replaced([11178156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26-vm_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be used.

The IE coresetFreqDomain for the common and dedicated PDCCH shall be set according the references in 5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and in 5G_L2_IF_408_replaced([10975247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Dfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), respectively.

Background: in accordance with the approach explained in 5G_L2_10447_replaced([11178156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26-vm_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for DL, the UE is directed to the UE dedicated UL BWP even for the inital RA by proper setting of the  _firstActiveUplinkBWP-Id IE in 5G_CP_IF_RRC_5129._

[End CB007372-A]

#### 2.5.1.5.3 Sending DlData_PdcchSendReq for DL DCI

##### 2.5.1.5.3.1 DL DCI for UEs

###### 2.5.1.5.3.1.0-1 DL DCI for UEs DL DCI - parameters common to FDD and TDD (ID: 11178156)

**2.5.1.5.3.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11178161`)

DL DCI for UEs DL DCI Transmission Request to L1-DL (deprecated)

---

**2.5.1.5.3.1.0-1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11178166`)

DL DCI for UEs DL DCI Transmission Request to L1-DL (deprecated)

[CNI-59628] Need to check remaining IEs (see parent SFS requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4474_replaced([11171714](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuGk5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Each DL PDCCH Scheduler which allocates a DL DCI shall send a DlData_PdcchSendReq message to the L1-DL instance handling the corresponding subcell to request the transmission of the DCI.

For the details of DlData_PdcchSendReq message content and timing: see 5G_L1_5G21A_70 and 5G_L1_5G21A_121.

The IE rnti is set to:

  * RA-RNTI (calculated in 5G_UP_ALG_3383_replaced([11152335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksfbV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in case of RA msg2
  * C-RNTI of the UE, otherwise



The IE startCce and aggregationLevel are filled according to the allocation (5G_UP_ALG_4426_replaced([11170801](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_4055_replaced([11170246](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt9a9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) respectively) .

to be checked - see 5G_UP_ALG_4474_replaced([11171714](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuGk5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (same as UL DCI)

[Before PR484189]; The IE dmrsScramblingSequenceInt ( in 38.211) shall be set to the physical cell ID (physCellId in PsCell_CellSetupReq).[End PR484189]

[PR484189];

The Information Element (IE) dmrsScramblingSequenceInt is set according to the coreset and search space used to send the DCI:

 If the CORESET(0) is used, the Information Element is set to the physical cell identitity defined at the cell setup ( in 38.211).

 For other CORESETs:

 If the search space is a common search space, the Information Element is set to the physical cell identitity defined at the cell setup.

 If the search space is a UE-Specific search space, the Information Element is set to the ueSssDmrsScramblingId associated to the CORESET and received in the in the PsCell_CellSetupReq.

[End PR484189]

[End CNI-59628]

The IE pdcchDciTransmitPower is set according to 5G_UP_ALG_2552_replaced([11118347](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

The IE dciPayload is set to the generated DCI.

The IE dciSize is set according to the size of the DCI (DCI format 1_0 5G_UP_ALG_4440_replaced([11171492](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuEvuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ; DCI format 1_1 5G_UP_ALG_10502_replaced([11171547](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuFWwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The IEs nShiftModNumOfRegBundles, interleaverRows are not applicable when the cceRegMappingType is set to non-interleaved. Not applicable means that L1 will ignore these fields.

[CNI-59628] to be checked - see 5G_UP_ALG_4474_replaced([11171714](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuGk5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (same as UL DCI ?)

For DL DCI transmitted in the UE dedicated bandwidth part, the IE precoderGranularity shall be set to "regBundleSize".

[End CNI-59628]

For DL DCI transmitted on Coreset#0, whatever is the active Bandwidth Part, the Coreset configuration is defined in 5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) using the commonControlResourceSet[0]. The IEs coresetFreqDomain , cceRegMappingType, interleaverRows, regBundleSize shall be set accordingly. The IE numOfSymbols shall be set to coresetDuration. In addition the dmrsReferencePoint shall be set to coresetStartPRB to be compliant with 5G_UP_IF_728_replaced([11504330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tSmnrvv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For DL DCI transmitted on Coreset#0,coresetFreqDomainRbShift shall also be set accordingly shall also be set according to coreset configuration defined in 5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) .

[CNI-59628] to be checked - see 5G_UP_ALG_4474_replaced([11171714](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuGk5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (same as UL DCI ?)

For DL DCI transmitted on Coreset#0,

nShiftModNumOfRegBundles = nShift mod{ rrmNumOfPRBinCoreset * numOfSymbols / regBundleSize }

with:

nShift is included in commonControlResourceSet[0] in PsCell_CellSetupReq.

rrmNumOfPRBinCoreset is the number of ‘1’ bits in the bitmap coresetFreqDomain multiply by 6.

numOfSymbols is set according to 5G_UP_IF_636_replaced([11502317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tSfS6vv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (N_symb^CORESET parameter).

[End CNI-59628]

For DL DCI transmitted on Coreset different from Coreset#0, the IE coresetFreqDomain is set according to the value received in UE setup ( 5G_L2_IF_389_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The IEs cceRegMappingType, interleaverRows, regBundleSize shall be set according to the values received in 5G_L2_IF_389_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). In addition, the dmrsReferencePoint shall be set to pointA to be compliant with 5G_UP_IF_728_replaced([11504330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tSmnrvv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: requirement has been linked to 5GC001242-A to highlight correct setting of dmrsReferencePoint, see PR513333.

[5GC000723-I]

For DL DCI transmitted in the UE specific search space in the UE dedicated BWP, the IE coresetFreqDomain, cceRegMappingType, interleaverRows, regBundleSize shall be set according to the values configured for the BWP with cellBwpId that is associated with initialUeActiveBwpId, see 5G_UP_ALG_1847_replaced([11110888](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpIlUvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End 5GC000723-I]

For DL DCI transmitted with a Coreset different from Coreset#0 ,coresetFreqDomainRbShift is set to 0.

[CNI-59628] to be checked - see 5G_UP_ALG_4474_replaced([11171714](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuGk5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (same as UL DCI ?)

For DL DCI transmitted with a Coreset different from Coreset#0,

nShiftModNumOfRegBundles = nShift mod{ rrmNumOfPRBinCoreset * numOfSymbols / regBundleSize }

with:

nShift is included in controlResourceSet in PsUser_UserSetupReq.

rrmNumOfPRBinCoreset is the number of ‘1’ bits in the bitmap coresetFreqDomain multiply by 6.

numOfSymbols is set according to 5G_UP_IF_638_replaced([11502627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tSfS7_v1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (N_symb^CORESET parameter).

[End CNI-59628]

The beamID used for derivation of patternID (see 5G_UP_ALG_1939_replaced([11111782](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpQhIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be added to message DlData_PdcchSendReq.

[5GC000523-F]

Each DL PDCCH Scheduler which allocates a DL DCI and sends a DlData_PdcchSendReq message to the L1-DL instance handling the corresponding subcell to request the transmission of the DCI shall process related PM Counters of class 'NR Cell Utilization' according to 5G_L2_330_replaced([11192795](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28mgQvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End 5GC000523-F]

[CNI-59628] to be checked - see 5G_UP_ALG_4474_replaced([11171714](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuGk5fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) - not applicable to UL DCI ?

[5GC000605-L]

When dlMimoMode 'OL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO' or 'CL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO, the field PdcchOLPrecodingOption4X4 in DlData_PdcchSendReq is set to rdPdcchPrecodingOption4X4 (cf. 5G_L2_1100_replaced([11182094](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27Y_RPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[End 5GC000605-L]

[5GC000920-A][5GC000920-B]

If no beamforming is applied, i.e. ("actBeamforming = False" && "beamFormingType = None" received via PsCell_CellSetupReq), no antenna port selection is applied. Therefore, only value "0" or "1" are applied in the field PdcchOLPrecodingOption4X4, where the value is set from rdPdcchPrecodingOption4X4 in DlData_PdcchSendReq (cf. 5G_L2_1100_replaced([11182094](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27Y_RPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[PR475364] when rdPdcchPrecodingOption4X4=2, the field PdcchOLPrecodingOption4X4 shall be set to value 0.

[End 5GC000920-A][End 5GC000920-B]

[5GC001451-A]

If numOfSubSectors == 2 and rdNbXpolAntennasCommonChannel == 1 (two Xpol antennas used) no antenna port selection is applied. rdTwoXpolAntennasPdcchPrecodingOption (cf. 5G_L2_1227_replaced([11191943](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28gZnPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is used to select correct precoding matrix for PDCCH, therefore PdcchPrecodingOption4X4 IE in DlData_PdcchSendReq shall be equal to rdTwoXpolAntennasPdcchPrecodingOption.

[End 5GC001451-A]

[End CNI-59628]

[5GC000918-A]

For analog beamforming for eCPRI RUs, L2 PS shall indicate beam of the corresponding UE or braodcast beam through numCeAxCIndex and ceAxcIndex and patternId in DlData_PdcchSendReq according to 5G_L1_5G21A_73 as

numCeAxCIndex number of eAxC index for D2 subcell type according to 5G_L1_5G21A_868.

ceAxcIndex eAxC index of default data for D2 subcell type according to 5G_L1_5G21A_868 and 5G_UP_ALG_22399_replaced([11193226](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvqrJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

patternId map beam Id to pattern Id according to 5G_UP_ALG_1909_replaced([11111524](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOE7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End 5GC000918-A]

**2.5.1.5.3.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11178172`)

DL DCI for UEs DL DCI Transmission Request to L1-DL (Part 1)

---

**2.5.1.5.3.1.0-1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11178180`)

DL DCI for UEs DL DCI Transmission Request to L1-DL (Part 1)

Each DL PDCCH Scheduler which allocates a DL DCI shall send a DlData_PdcchSendReq message to the L1-DL instance handling the corresponding subcell to request the transmission of the DCI.

For the details of DlData_PdcchSendReq message content and timing: see 5G_L1_5G21A_70 and 5G_L1_5G21A_121.

The IE rnti is set to:

  * RA-RNTI (calculated in 5G_UP_ALG_3383_replaced([11152335](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksfbV_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in case of RA msg2
  * C-RNTI of the UE, otherwise



The beamID used for derivation of patternID (see 5G_UP_ALG_1939_replaced([11111782](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpQhIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be added to message DlData_PdcchSendReq.

\----------- pdcchDmrsConfig structure:

[Before PR559111],

The Information Element (IE) dmrsScramblingSequenceInt is set according to the coreset and search space used to send the DCI:

 If the CORESET(0) is used, the Information Element is set to the physical cell identitity defined at the cell setup ( in 38.211).

 For other CORESETs:

 If the search space is a common search space, the Information Element is set to the physical cell identitity defined at the cell setup.

 If the search space is a UE-Specific search space, the Information Element is set to the ueSssDmrsScramblingId associated to the CORESET and received in the in the PsCell_CellSetupReq.

[PR559111]

The IE dmrsScramblingSequenceInt is set according to the coreset and search space used to send the DCI:

 If the CORESET(0) is used, the Information Element is set to the physical cell identitity defined at the cell setup ([image-0][image_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_5624.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]in 38.211).

 For other CORESETs:

 If the search space is a common search space, the Information Element is set to the physical cell identitity defined at the cell setup.

 If the search space is a UE-Specific search space, the Information Element is set to the ueSssDmrsScramblingId associated to the CORESET and received in the in the PsCell_CellSetupReq.

[End PR559111]

\----------- dciConfig structure:

The IE pdcchDciTransmitPower is set according to 5G_UP_ALG_2552_replaced([11118347](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqCkQvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

The IE dciPayload is set to the generated DCI.

The IE dciSize is set according to the size of the DCI (DCI format 1_0 5G_UP_ALG_4440_replaced([11171492](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuEvuPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ; DCI format 1_1 5G_UP_ALG_10502_replaced([11171547](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuFWwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

\----------- CoresetConfig structure:

The IE startCce and aggregationLevel are filled according to the allocation (5G_UP_ALG_4426_replaced([11170801](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuAeQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_4055_replaced([11170246](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt9a9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) respectively) .

The IEs nShiftModNumOfRegBundles, interleaverRows are not applicable when the cceRegMappingType is set to non-interleaved. Not applicable means that L1 will ignore these fields.

For DL DCI transmitted in the UE dedicated bandwidth part, the IE precoderGranularity shall be set to "regBundleSize".

For DL DCI transmitted on Coreset#0, whatever is the active Bandwidth Part, the Coreset configuration is defined in 5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) using the commonControlResourceSet[0]. The IEs coresetFreqDomain , cceRegMappingType, interleaverRows, regBundleSize shall be set accordingly. The IE numOfSymbols shall be set to coresetDuration. In addition the dmrsReferencePoint shall be set to coresetStartPRB to be compliant with 5G_UP_IF_728_replaced([11504330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tSmnrvv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For DL DCI transmitted on Coreset#0,coresetFreqDomainRbShift shall also be set accordingly shall also be set according to coreset configuration defined in 5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) .

For DL DCI transmitted on Coreset#0,

nShiftModNumOfRegBundles = nShift mod{ rrmNumOfPRBinCoreset * numOfSymbols / regBundleSize }

with:

nShift is included in commonControlResourceSet[0] in PsCell_CellSetupReq.

rrmNumOfPRBinCoreset is the number of ‘1’ bits in the bitmap coresetFreqDomain multiply by 6.

numOfSymbols is set according to 5G_UP_IF_636_replaced([11502317](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tSfS6vv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (N_symb^CORESET parameter).

For DL DCI transmitted on Coreset different from Coreset#0, the IE coresetFreqDomain is set according to the value received in UE setup ( 5G_L2_IF_389_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The IEs cceRegMappingType, interleaverRows, regBundleSize shall be set according to the values received in 5G_L2_IF_389_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). In addition, the dmrsReferencePoint shall be set to pointA to be compliant with 5G_UP_IF_728_replaced([11504330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tSmnrvv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For DL DCI transmitted with a Coreset different from Coreset#0 ,coresetFreqDomainRbShift is set to 0.

For DL DCI transmitted with a Coreset different from Coreset#0,

nShiftModNumOfRegBundles = nShift mod{ rrmNumOfPRBinCoreset * numOfSymbols / regBundleSize }

with:

nShift is included in controlResourceSet in PsUser_UserSetupReq.

rrmNumOfPRBinCoreset is the number of ‘1’ bits in the bitmap coresetFreqDomain multiply by 6.

numOfSymbols is set according to 5G_UP_IF_638_replaced([11502627](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tSfS7_v1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (N_symb^CORESET parameter).

For DL DCI transmitted in the UE specific search space in the UE dedicated BWP, the IE coresetFreqDomain, cceRegMappingType, interleaverRows, regBundleSize shall be set according to the values configured for the BWP with cellBwpId that is associated with initialUeActiveBwpId, see 5G_UP_ALG_17939_replaced([11110885](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpIlUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In case of PRB blanking supported, offsetToCarrier shall be set according to the PRB blanking configurations. For DL DCI transmitted with a Coreset different from Coreset#0, coresetFreqDomainRbShift shall also be set accordingly shall also be set according to coreset configuration defined in 5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

refer to REQ 5G_L2_13048_replaced([11178185](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26-voPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the next part

---

**2.5.1.5.3.1.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11178185`)

DL DCI for UEs DL DCI Transmission Request to L1-DL (Part 2)

---

**2.5.1.5.3.1.0-1.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11178209`)

DL DCI for UEs DL DCI Transmission Request to L1-DL (Part 2)

refer to REQ 5G_L2_13044_replaced([11178172](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26-vnvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the previous part

\----- PdcchPrecodingConfig and eCpriConfig structure:

When dlMimoMode 'OL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO' or 'CL 4x4 or 4x2 MIMO, the field PdcchOLPrecodingOption4X4 in DlData_PdcchSendReq is set to rdPdcchPrecodingOption4X4 (cf. 5G_L2_3723_replaced([11182089](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27Y_Q_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If dlMimoMode is 'CL 8x4 MIMO', rdPdcchPrecodingOption4X4 is not used, the field pdcchPrecodingOption4X4 and related XPolBeam in DlData_PdcchSendReq shall be set to as 5G_L2_494_replaced([11156008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_248vSvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For the case FD beamforming is disabled, if L2-PS needs to send DCIs to users in two beam directions with C4 subcell, for each DCI transmission, the field pdcchPrecodingOption4X4 in DlData_PdcchSendReq shall be set to repetitionTwoXPol. The pattern ID of the first XPolBeam is one beam direction and pattern ID of the second XPolBeam is another beam direction (see 5G_L2_494_replaced([11156008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_248vSvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

For the case FD beamforming is enabled, the field pdcchPrecodingOption4x4 shall be set to repetitionOneXPol.

If dlMimoMode is 'CL 8x4 MIMO', to transmit DCI with C4 subcell, L2-RT shall follow below rules (see 5G_L2_497_replaced([11156027](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_248vT_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as well).

1) If user’s DCI is transmitted with the first XPolBeam of the subcell, patternId of the first XPolBeam shall be filled with user’s best beam and pdcchPrecodingOption4x4 shall be set to repetitionOneXPol.

2) If user’s DCI is transmitted with the second XPolBeam of the subcell, patternId of the second XPolBeam shall be filled with user’s best beam and pdcchPrecodingOption4x4 shall be set to repetition2ndXPol.

For eCPRI and dlMimoMode is CL 8x4, each stream can be set as different beams for frequency multiplexed PDCCH.

Each PDCCH need 2 streams,

The 2 stream index {0, 1} is used for all the FDM PDCCH with no "same beam for one stream" restriction as CPRI. So ECpriConfig structure in DlData_PdcchSendReq is set as below:

numCeAxCIndex set to 2;

ceAxcIndex set to {0, 1};

patternId set to the one patternID choosed for this PDCCH, which is the same as CPRI;

For eCPRI, if dlMimoMode is CL 8x4, pdcchPrecodingOption4X4 in DlData_PdcchSendReq shall be set to repetitionOneXPol for all the PDCCH.

If no beamforming is applied,

[CB013440-A] if enhCtrlChannelTransMode is different than 'disabled' (see PsCell_CellSetupReq, PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq) then follow 5G_L2_23660_replaced([11178739](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27By5PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), otherwise [End CB013440-A] see 5G_UP_ALG_2183_replaced([11112736](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZEBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_907_replaced([11353384](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ub-6UvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), no antenna port selection is applied. Therefore, only value "0" or "1" are applied in the field PdcchOLPrecodingOption4X4, where the value is set from rdPdcchPrecodingOption4X4 in DlData_PdcchSendReq (cf. 5G_L2_3723_replaced([11182089](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27Y_Q_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). when rdPdcchPrecodingOption4X4=2, the field PdcchOLPrecodingOption4X4 shall be set to value 0.

If numOfSubSectors == 2 and rdNbXpolAntennasCommonChannel == 1 (two Xpol antennas used) no antenna port selection is applied. rdTwoXpolAntennasPdcchPrecodingOption (cf. 5G_L2_1227_replaced([11191943](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28gZnPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is used to select correct precoding matrix for PDCCH, therefore PdcchPrecodingOption4X4 IE in DlData_PdcchSendReq shall be equal to rdTwoXpolAntennasPdcchPrecodingOption.

For analog beamforming for eCPRI RUs, L2 PS shall indicate beam of the corresponding UE or braodcast beam through numCeAxCIndex and ceAxcIndex and patternId in DlData_PdcchSendReq according to 5G_L1_5G21A_73 as

numCeAxCIndex number of eAxC index for D2 subcell type according to 5G_L1_5G21A_868.

ceAxcIndex eAxC index of default data for D2 subcell type according to 5G_L1_5G21A_868 and 5G_UP_ALG_22399_replaced([11193226](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvqrJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

patternId map beam Id to pattern Id according to 5G_UP_ALG_1909_replaced([11111524](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOE7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

When supercell mode is enabled (numOfSuperSubcells >= 2) L2 PS shall set patternId to 0 in DlData_PdcchSendReq.

Each DL PDCCH Scheduler which allocates a DL DCI and sends a DlData_PdcchSendReq message to the L1-DL instance handling the corresponding subcell to request the transmission of the DCI shall process related PM Counters of class 'NR Cell Utilization' according to 5G_L2_329_replaced([11192791](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28mgQfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

###### 2.5.1.5.3.1.0-2 DL DCI for UEs DL DCI - FDD specific parameters (ID: 11178215)

**2.5.1.5.3.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11178219`)

DL DCI for UEs [CNI-59628] No CP2 content - to be checked [End CNI-59628]

FDD-specific settings for DL DCI Transmission Request to L1-DL

This requirement defines IEs of the DlData_PdcchSendReq that are specific for FDD. Parameters that are not mentioned here are assumed to be common with TDD, defined in 5G_L2_880_replaced([11178166](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26-vnfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For FDD carrier with 5MHz and slot type B4 with 2 PDCCH symbols, the IE startSymbolNumber shall be set to '1'.

(5GC000723-H) {For FDD carrier with 5MHz BW, the DL DCI is transmitted in USS that is associated with Coreset#0. The IE startSymbolNumber shall be set to the OFDM symbol index that is corresponding to the one indicated in the first bit of monitoringSymbolsWithinSlot in search space configuration, see 5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and the IE startCce is set according to 5G_UP_ALG_3955_replaced([11169860](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6Xp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).}

For the initial DL BWP, CORESET#0 with 24PRB bandwidth on 5MHz and 48PRBs on 10, 15 and 20MHz is configured.

[Before 5GC000723-I][5GC000836-D] For UE dedicated DL BWP, CORESET#1 on full available bandwidth of the FDD carrier is configured.

[5GC000723-I] For UE dedicated DL BWP, CORESET configuration coresetFreqDomain, cceRegMappingType, interleaverRows, regBundleSize shall be set according to the values configured for the BWP with cellBwpId that is associated with initialUeActiveBwpId, see 5G_UP_ALG_1847_replaced([11110888](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpIlUvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

(5GC000723-H) For UE dedicated BWP, CORESET#4 on full available 5MHz BW of the FDD carrier is configured.

[5GC000836-G] The same settings for IE startSymbolNumber are used for 10MHz and 15MHz [5GC000836-J] and for 20MHz bandwidths.

[5GC000836-G] For DL DCI transmitted in the UE dedicated bandwidth; numOfSymbols is set according to the coresetDuration (5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ).

(5GC000723-H) For SA, for FDD carrier with 5MHz BW, the IE numOfSymbols shall be set to '2'.

For FDD carrier with 5MHz and slot type B4 with 2 PDCCH symbols, the 64-bit IE coresetFreqDomain in the DlData_PdcchSendReq message is set to "0xF000 0000 0000 0000".

Note: This bit-mapping results in RRC IE frequencyDomainResources set to "0x1E00 0000 0000".

[5GC000836-G] For FDD carrier with 10MHz or 15MHz and slot type B4 with 2 PDCCH symbols, the 64-bit IE coresetFreqDomain in the DlData_PdcchSendReq message is set to "0xFF00 0000 0000 0000".

Note: Those bitmaps result from a hardcoded allocation of the CORESET for L1/L2 FDD starting the allocation of 4 consecutive CCEs at PRB0. The logic is given by the comment in 36.331.v15.0.1:

\-- Frequency domain resources for the CORESET. Each bit corresponds a group of 6 RBs, with grouping starting from PRB 0, which is fully

\-- contained in the bandwidth part within which the CORESET is configured.

\-- The most significant bit corresponds to the group of lowest frequency which is fully contained in the bandwidth part within which the

\-- CORESET is configured, each next subsequent lower significance bit corresponds to the next lowest frequency group fully contained within

\-- the bandwidth part within which the CORESET is configured, if any.

\-- Bits corresponding to a group not fully contained within the bandwidth part within which the CORESET is configured are set to zero.

\-- Corresponds to L1 parameter 'CORESET-freq-dom'(see 38.211, section 7.3.2.2) frequencyDomainResources BIT STRING (SIZE (45))

[5GC001904-A] for FDD on a carrier shared with LTE with 10MHz [5GC001904-B] as well as with 15Mhz and 20MHz [End 5GC001904-B]

[PR504294]

As per 5G_UP_ALG_3935_replaced([11168314](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktvYg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), only CORESET#1 in dedicated BWP will be used by L2PS.

[End PR504294]

  * the IE coresetFreqDomain for the common PDCCH shall be set according the parameter settings in 5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * the IE coresetFreqDomain for the dedicated PDCCH shall be set according the parameter settings in 5G_L2_IF_389_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_L2_IF_408_replaced([10975247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Dfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



[End 5GC001904-A]

[5GC000836-L]

The Coreset configuration is defined in

  * 5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), structure IE commonControlResourceSet[numOfCommonControlResourceSets] for Common Search Space of both Initial BWP and dedicated BWP.
  * 5G_L2_IF_389_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) resp. 5G_L2_IF_408_replaced([10975247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Dfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UE Specific Search Space (UE SSS) of dedicated BWP.



(Note: UE SSS of initial BWP is not utilized.)

The same settings for the IEs cceRegMappingType, interleaverRows, regBundleSize, numOfSymbols and dmrsReferencePoint as defined for TDD in 5G_L2_880_replaced([11178166](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26-vnfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [tagged with 5GC000580-G] shall be used.

The IE coresetFreqDomain for the common and dedicated PDCCH shall be set according the references in 5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and in 5G_L2_IF_408_replaced([10975247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Dfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), respectively.

[5GC000836-J]

On 5MHz FDD with Agg8 (if configured so by the NIDD parameter aggregationLevel ), the Coreset#0 configured on 24PRB/2 OFDMA symbols is used for Agg8 and Coreset#1 on full Bw/1 OFDMA symbol for Agg4 the DL slot type B5 is used. For details cf. 5G_UP_ALG_4055_replaced([11170246](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt9a9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For all channel bandwidths including 20MHz

the same settings for the IEs cceRegMappingType, interleaverRows, regBundleSize, numOfSymbols and dmrsReferencePoint as defined for TDD in 5G_L2_880_replaced([11178166](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26-vnfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [tagged with 5GC000580-G] shall be used.

The IE coresetFreqDomain for the common and dedicated PDCCH shall be set according the references in 5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and in 5G_L2_IF_408_replaced([10975247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Dfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), respectively.

[5GC001242-A]

For FDD on a carrier shared with LTE, if PRB blanking function is enabled and nbrOfBlankedPRBsLowEdgeDL or nbrOfBlankedPRBsHighEdgeDL is greater than 0, CORESET#0 with blanked PRBs is not able to be used any more. CORESET#1 in dedicate BWP maps to raSearchSpace will be used.

the IE coresetFreqDomain for the common PDCCH shall be set according the parameter settings in 5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

the IE coresetFreqDomain for the dedicated PDCCH shall be set according the parameter settings in 5G_L2_IF_389_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_L2_IF_408_replaced([10975247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Dfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End 5GC001242-A]

[5GC001242-D]

For FDD NSA mode, if PRB blanking function is enabled, CORESET#0 may fall into the blanking area or not:

\- If the blanked PRBs overlapping with CORESET#0, that is, CORESET#0 is not able to be used any more. CORESET#1 in dedicate BWP maps to raSearchSpace will be used.

\- If the blanked PRBs not overlapping with CORESET#0, that is, CORESET#0 still is able to be used. CORESET#0 shall be used to map to raSearchSpace.

the IE coresetFreqDomain for the common PDCCH shall be set according the parameter settings in 5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_L2_IF_84_replaced([10968165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UW90_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

the IE coresetFreqDomain for the dedicated PDCCH shall be set according the parameter settings in 5G_L2_IF_389_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_L2_IF_408_replaced([10975247](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Dfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End 5GC001242-D]

##### 2.5.1.5.3.2 DL dummy DCI

###### 2.5.1.5.3.2.0-1 DL dummy DCI (ID: 11178232)

**2.5.1.5.3.2.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11178237`)

DL dummy DCI As specified by the feature CB010359, L2PS shall add dummy DCI on first symbol of DL PDCCH in some DL slots.

L2PS implementation is limited to DL scheduler, and UL scheduler does not send dummy DCI.

When CCE split is used, the first symbol contains UL DCI and DL DCI.

the requirement 5G_UP_ALG_3955_replaced([11169860](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kt6Xp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) defines two CCE areas to separate DL DCI and UL DCI.

DL Scheduler shall not add dummy DCI in the CCE area reserved to UL DCI.

[CB008940-L]

If slowPrbPoolingTddFr1DlAllowed = TRUE, in CCE split case and CCE non-split case, for each PDCCH symbol, the total number of PRB used by UL DCI, DL DCI and dummy DCI shall not exceed numAllocCellPrb, the number of PRB allocated by BBRM.

Specifically in CCE split case, if the numAllocCellPrb is equal or lower than the coresetMaxSize, dummy DCI can be added only in the DL CCE area. If the numAllocCellPrb is greater than the coresetMaxSize, dummy DCI can be added in the DL CCE area and beyond the coresetMaxSize.

coresetMaxSize is the maximum size of the coresets used in the slot.

[End CB008940-L]

---

#### 2.5.1.5.4 FDD BF Stream Distribution for DL PDCCH and UL PDCCH

##### 2.5.1.5.4.0-1 FDD BF Stream Distribution for DL PDCCH and UL PDCCH (ID: 13312711)

**2.5.1.5.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13018893`)

FDD BF Stream Distribution for DL PDCCH and UL PDCCH For FDD cell with actBeamforming = TRUE on A4 DL subcell, PDCCH for DL scheduling is assigned to first 2 streams for DL, and PDCCH for UL scheduling is assigned to the last 2 streams for DL according to [11384035: DL/UL subcell type A4: number of spatial streams and MIMO mode](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ue32MvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), [11353824: Beamforming of Control and Shared Channels](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucCkpvvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and [12783618: CSI feedback based beam management: 32 ports CSI_RS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_URtrsY7iEfCrqOdGJPoCRA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9). That is: for PDCCH for DL scheduling, DlData_PdcchSendReqL1sw->ceAxCIndex is set to {0,1,0,0}, and for PDCCH for UL scheduling, DlData_PdcchSendReqL1sw->ceAxCIndex is set to {2,3,0,0}.

#### 2.5.1.6.2 Sending DlData_PdschSendReq

##### 2.5.1.6.2.0-1 Sending DlData_PdschSendReq Setting numCsirsMappingRes (ID: 11178264)

**2.5.1.6.2.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `11178379`)

Sending DlData_PdschSendReq If the flag csirsTrackingEnable or actPdcchSharingWithPdsch or actSubTrsRateMatch or actTddCsiImRm set to True in PsCell_CellSetupReq message (5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), in FR1, 5G-L2-PS shall fill the numRateMatchingRes IE in all DlData_PdschSendReq messages (5G_L1_5G21A_86) scrambled by a C-RNTI in order to provide the number of CSI-RS for Tracking, resource elements for rate matching PDSCH around PDCCH DCI in the same symbol inside the PDSCH allocation, see 5G_UP_ALG_2987_replaced([11125029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqsEi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall fill numRateMatchingRes as a sum of following resource elements:

  * CSI-RS for Tracking resource elements.

  * resource elements for rate matching PDSCH around PDCCH DCI in the same symbol.




\- CSI-IM resource elements.

step 1: CSI-RS for Tracking periodicity and slot check:

SFN and slot are the one used for the DlData_PdschSendReq (5G_L1_5G21A_86).

5G_UP_ALG_2987_replaced([11125029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqsEi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) defines the frames which contain CSI-RS for tracking REs.

If the current frame contains no CSI-RS for tracking REs stop proceed with counting Res for rate matching PDSCH around PDCCH DCI in the same symbol due to the step 1.1. Otherwise, check if the current slot contains CSI-RS for tracking REs:

if [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is a summation. The summation symbol is followed by the index of summation, which is "ofdmIndex", with the lower limit being 0 and the upper limit being 5. The expression being summed is "numCsirsTrRes[slotIndex][ofdmIndex]".[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_5644.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] > 0 (see 5G_UP_ALG_10885_replaced([11124985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqsEg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

go on with step 2

else

stopproceed with step 1.1

numCsirsTrRes: Defined in 5G_L2_57_replaced([11141810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23q85PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Step 1.1:

If rateMatching option in DlData_PdschSendReq is set to 2: RATE_MATCHING_DCI or 3: RATE_MATCHING_CSIRS_AND_DCI or 6: RATE_MATCHING_SYMBOL_AND_DCI the number of PDSCH and PDCCH Res overlapping should be counted (numOfPdcchandPdschOverlapingRes):

1.1.1 Define the overlapping area of the PDCCH and PDSCH:

Case 1: 1 DCI, rat0Bitmap [CB008927-N] shall be set zero when NRCELL.actRAT1Alloc = True, such cases numbe of Allocated Prb shall be considered.[End CB008927-N]

Case 2: 1 DCI, rat0Bitmap (part 1 and part2) [CB008927-N] shall be non zero value when UE is allocated based on RAT0 or when NRCELL.actRAT1Alloc = True, and NRCELL.actDlDynSwitchAlloc = True.[End CB008927-N]
