Folder: [https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Forms/Tree_View.aspx?OR=Teams%2DHL&CT=1707824237057&clickparams=eyJBcHBOYW1lIjoiVGVhbXMtRGVza3RvcCIsIkFwcFZlcnNpb24iOiIyNy8yNDAxMDQxNzUwMyIsIkhhc0ZlZGVyYXRlZFVzZXIiOmZhbHNlfQ%3D%3D&cid=4e7adfda%2D44af%2D4402%2Da9e1%2Dd5b0c533219d&FolderCTID=0x012000F0A0A3BA325F7648AD307E6959BA7376&id=%2Fsites%2F5Gdoc%2FAS%5FTech%5FSpec%2FDrawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G%2FUser%20Plane%2F5G%20L2%20Entity%20Level%2F2%205G%2DL2%2DPS%20Component%20Requirements%2F2%2E5%20Interactions%20with%20other%20components%2F1%2E%20Interactions%20with%20L1%2DDL&viewid=967508b3%2D8e81%2D461c%2Db99d%2D145065cf0c1c](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/sites/5Gdoc/AS_Tech_Spec/Forms/Tree_View.aspx?OR=Teams%2DHL&CT=1707824237057&clickparams=eyJBcHBOYW1lIjoiVGVhbXMtRGVza3RvcCIsIkFwcFZlcnNpb24iOiIyNy8yNDAxMDQxNzUwMyIsIkhhc0ZlZGVyYXRlZFVzZXIiOmZhbHNlfQ%3D%3D&cid=4e7adfda%2D44af%2D4402%2Da9e1%2Dd5b0c533219d&FolderCTID=0x012000F0A0A3BA325F7648AD307E6959BA7376&id=%2Fsites%2F5Gdoc%2FAS%5FTech%5FSpec%2FDrawings%20and%20diagrams%20for%205G%2FUser%20Plane%2F5G%20L2%20Entity%20Level%2F2%205G%2DL2%2DPS%20Component%20Requirements%2F2%2E5%20Interactions%20with%20other%20components%2F1%2E%20Interactions%20with%20L1%2DDL&viewid=967508b3%2D8e81%2D461c%2Db99d%2D145065cf0c1c)

1.1.2 5G-L2-PS shall count resource elements for rate matching PDSCH around PDCCH DCI in the same symbol (pdschUnscheduledAreaConfig) as a product of PDCCH DCI and PDSCH common parts: PdschAllocation∩PdcchDciAllocation

1.1.3 5G-L2-PS shall fill and send pdschUnscheduledAreaConfig structure (5G_L1_IF_15220_replaced([11512929](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRs3X_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in DlData_DataPdschSendReq towards 5G-L1-DL.

1.1.4 If number of resource elements for rate matching PDSCH around PDCCH DCI in the same symbol=0, 5G-L2-PS shall fill pdschUnscheduledAreaConfig structure with zero values (5G_L1_IF_15220_replaced([11512929](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRs3X_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in DlData_DataPdschSendReq and send it towards 5G-L1-DL and proceed with the next step.

step 2: check if RBs overlap with CSI-RS for Tracking RBs:

If actSubTrsRateMatch is false,

1) contiguous RB allocation (rat0Bitmap IE equal to 0 in 5G_L1_5G21A_92)

L2-PS compares for the startPrb and numOfPrb IEs (see 5G_L1_5G21A_92) of the PDSCH grant with the csirsTrackingStartingPrb and csirsTrackingNumOfPrbs IEs (5G_UP_ALG_10885_replaced([11124985](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqsEg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in order to find if there are RBs which overlap with CSI-RS for Tracking RBs.

if startPrb >= csirsTrackingStartingPrb and startPrb <= (csirsTrackingStartingPrb + csirsTrackingNumOfPrbs),

nbrbcsirs = MIN((startPrb+numOfPrb),(csirsTrackingStartingPrb+ csirsTrackingNumOfPrbs)) - startPrb

else if startPrb < csirsTrackingStartingPrb and (startPrb + numOfPrb) > csirsTrackingStartingPrb,

nbrbcsirs = MIN((startPrb+numOfPrb),(csirsTrackingStartingPrb+csirsTrackingNumOfPrbs)) - csirsTrackingStartingPrb

else

nbrbcsirs = 0

If nbrbcsirs > 0,

go on with step 3

else

number of CSI-RS for tracking REs is zero and proceed with REs for rate matching PDSCH around PDCCH DCI in the same symbol in numRateMatchingRes

2) non contiguous RB allocation

nbrbcsirs = 0

For each RBG granted (bit =1 in the bitmap rat0Bitmap) , compute startRbRbg which is the first RB of this RBG and nbRbRbg = rbgSizeFirst if the first RBG is granted otherwise rbgSize (see 5G_L1_5G21A_92)

if startRbRbg >= csirsTrackingStartingPrb and startPrb <= (csirsTrackingStartingPrb + csirsTrackingNumOfPrbs),

nbrbcsirs = nbrbcsirs + MIN((startRbRbg+nbRbRbg ),(csirsTrackingStartingPrb+ csirsTrackingNumOfPrbs)) - startRbRbg

else if startRbRbg < csirsTrackingStartingPrb and (startRbRbg + nbRbRbg) > csirsTrackingStartingPrb,

nbrbcsirs = nbrbcsirs + MIN((startRbRbg+nbRbRbg),(csirsTrackingStartingPrb+csirsTrackingNumOfPrbs)) - csirsTrackingStartingPrb 

If nbrbcsirs > 0,

go on with step 3

else

number of CSI-RS for tracking REs is zero and proceed with REs for rate matching PDSCH around PDCCH DCI in the same symbol in numRateMatchingRes

If actSubTrsRateMatch is true,

TRS will occupy whole Bandwidth (filled by ZP TRS to avoid TRS symbol allocate to UE), Pdsch granted PRB will all overlapped with TRS, so overlap PRB equal to numOfPrb allocated for Pdsch.

step 3: check if symbols of PDSCH grant overlap with CSI-RS for Tracking symbols.

If actSubTrsRateMatch is false,

L2-PS compare for the startSymbol and numOfPdschSymbols IEs (see 5G_L1_5G21A_92) of the PDSCH grant with the csirsTrSymbol[ofdmIndex] for 0<=ofdmIndex<6 (see 5G_L2_57_replaced([11141810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23q85PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in order to find if PDSCH include some CSI-RS for Tracking symbols.

if startSymbol <= csirsTrSymbol[0] and (startSymbol+numOfPdschSymbols ) >= csirsTrSymbol[5],

numCsirsMappingRes = nbrbcsirs * [image-3][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical expression. The expression is a summation: $\sum_{ofdmIndex=0}^{5} numCsiRsTrRes[slotIndex][ofdmIndex]$[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_5644.004.png[/image_path][/image-3] 

(numCsirsTrRes: Defined in 5G_L2_57_replaced([11141810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23q85PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).)

else

if startSymbol <= csirsTrSymbol[0]

minCsirsTrIndex = 0

else if startSymbol <= csirsTrSymbol[5]

minCsirsTrIndex = csirsTrSymbol[indexmin]

where indexmin is such as 1<= indexmin < 6 and csirsTrSymbol[(indexmin-1)] < startSymbol <= csirsTrSymbol[indexmin]

else minCsirsTrIndex =

maxCsiRsTrIndex = 0 and numCsirsMappingRes = 0 for CSI-RS for Tracking

if (startSymbol+numOfPdschSymbols) >= csirsTrSymbol[5]

maxCsiRsTrIndex = 5

else if (startSymbol+numOfPdschSymbols) >= csirsTrSymbol[0]

maxCsiRsTrIndex = csirsTrSymbol[indexmax]

where indexmin is such as 0<= indexmax < 5 and csirsTrSymbol[indexmax] <= (startSymbol+numOfPdschSymbols) < csirsTrSymbol[indexmax+1]

else minCsirsTrIndex = maxCsiRsTrIndex = 0 and numCsirsMappingRes = 0 for CSI-RS for Tracking

if (minCsirsTrIndex>0) and (maxCsiRsTrIndex>0)

numCsirsMappingRes = nbrbcsirs * 

[image-4][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical formula. The formula is a summation with indices. The summation symbol is followed by "maxCsiRsTrIndex" in the superscript and "ofdmIndex=minCsiRsTrIndex" in the subscript. To the right of the summation, there is "numCsiRsRes[slotIndex][ofdmIndex]".[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_5644.005.png[/image_path][/image-4] 

(numCsirsTrRes: Defined in 5G_L2_57_replaced([11141810](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23q85PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).)

If actSubTrsRateMatch is true,

Symbols allocated for TRS will not available for Pdsch, numCsirsMappingRes =

[image-5][image_desc]maxCsiRsTrsIndex of dmIndex ∑ numCsirsTrsRes[slotIndex][of dmIndex][/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_5644.006.png[/image_path][/image-5]

and

[image-6][image_desc]The image contains a mathematical equation written in a serif font. The equation is: `numCsirsTrsRes[slotIndex[ofdmlndex]] = 12 * numOfPrb`[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_5644.007.png[/image_path][/image-6]

Symbols allocated for TRS will all punch for Pdsch rate matching.

Step 4: calculate number of PRB and symbols of PDSCH overlap with CSI-IM.

When actTddCsiIm is true and cell CSI-RS is used, CSI-IM symbol can schedule PDSCH with DCI11 too. The CSI-IM is wideband, so it's PRB number is same as the granted PDSCH PRB.

The CSI-IM always has 4 resource elements per RB. Following is example of CSI-IM in one PRB:

[image-7][image_desc]The image displays a grid representing a resource allocation in a communication system. The grid has rows labeled from 0 to 11 and columns labeled from 0 to 13. The grid is divided into several sections: * **Columns 0-2 (Blue):** These columns are labeled with letters 'P', 'D', 'C', 'C', and 'H' in rows 7 down to 3 respectively. This section appears to represent control or reference signals. * **Columns 3-13 (Green):** The majority of the grid, from column 3 onwards, is colored green. * In rows 8 and 9, there is text "". This indicates that a Physical Downlink Shared Channel (PDSCH) is allocated, and it is associated with a Downlink Control Information (DCI) of type 11. * In rows 1 to 3, there are two numbered points: 1\. "CSI-IM symbol is used for PDSCH." 2\. "Ratematching the CSI-IM RE." These points explain the usage of CSI-IM (Channel State Information - Interference Measurement) resources within the PDSCH allocation. * In columns 12 and 13, and rows 7 and 8, there are two yellow cells labeled "CSI" and "IM" stacked vertically. This likely represents the CSI-IM resource elements themselves. * **Bottom Label:** Below the grid, there is a bracket spanning columns 3 to 13 with the label "PDSCH SLIV.length". This indicates the length of the PDSCH allocation in terms of these resource elements. The grid visually represents how different types of resources (control, data, and CSI-IM) are allocated within a specific time-frequency resource block.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_5644.008.png[/image_path][/image-7]

numCsirsMappingRes = PdschSendReq.numOfPrb * 4.

Note, CSI-IM and TRS will not allocate in same slot when actTddCsiIm=True in current design.

Step 5:

Count number of elements that cannot be used for PDSCH due to CSI-RS, or CSI-IM, or PDCCH DCI, or CSI-RS and PDCCH DCI mapping:

numRateMatchingRes = numCsirsMappingRes + numOfPdcchandPdschOverlapingRes

This requirement shall also applicable to TDD FR1.

Refer to 5G_L2_2881_replaced([11174008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26gOdvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for rateMatchingOption setting.

---

##### 2.5.1.6.2.0-2 Sending DlData_PdschSendReq Setting symbolRateMatchingPositions (ID: 11178387)

**2.5.1.6.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11178394`)

Sending DlData_PdschSendReq if actSubTrsRateMatch is true, L2-PS need to indicate L1-DL which symbols are occupied by TRS, symbolRateMatchingPositions LSB0 mapping to symbol 0, LSB1 mapping to symbol 1, detail info refer to 5G_L1_IF_87_replaced([11512751](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRrpPvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

##### 2.5.1.6.2.0-3 Sending DlData_PdschSendReq Requesting Transport Block transmission from 5G-L1-DL [3GPP] (ID: 11178401)

**2.5.1.6.2.0-3.0-10**  (ID: `13347118`)

Sending DlData_PdschSendReq 5G-L2-PS shall request the transmission of Transport Blocks by sending the message DlData_PdschSendReq for each of them to 5G-L1-DL. See 5G_L1_5G21A_79 for details.

The IE subcellId shall be set according to 5G_UP_ALG_4327_replaced([11177617](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when subcellDeactivationDlAllowed = false, and 5G_UP_ALG_15393_replaced([11212871](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxDyS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) when subcellDeactivationDlAllowed = true

The IEs sfn and slot represent the TTI when the TB shall be on air. Note, from them 5G-L1-Dl derives the start of the corresponding L1 buffer.

The IE tbStartOffset_bits represents the relative start offset of the TB within subcell’s L1 buffer.

The IEs tbIndex & tbStartOffset_bits are set according to 5G_L2_319_replaced([11149707](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24Xge_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The IE tbSize_bits shall be set to the determined Transport Block size according to 5G_UP_ALG_4621_replaced([11192057](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kviITvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The IE rnti shall be set to Ue C-RNTI.

The IE mcs corresponds to rrmDlUsedMcs as determined in 5G_UP_ALG_4630_replaced([11192270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvjWafvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).  
If given UE allocation was affected by FD-POLITE PRB widening loop (see [12533165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_jm0A4Bw4EfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) IEs mcs and tbSize_bits shall be filled based on the final values in the last successful FD-POLITE attempt.

The IE numOfLayer and antPort shall be set according to 5G_UP_ALG_3165_replaced([11139212](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krlcZvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_4405_replaced([11142329](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3wSfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The precoding is set according to 5G_UP_ALG_3171_replaced([11139234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krlca_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Spatial mode:

dlMimoMode == SingleAntennaTransmission_1x1 then spatialMode = Single Antenna

dlMimoMode == ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_2x2 **or ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_4x4or4x2 or ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_8x4[CB008577-B] or ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_32x4[End CB008577-B]****then spatialMode = Closed loop spatial multiplexing**

dlMimoMode == OpenLoopSpatialMultiplexing_2x2 **or OpenLoopSpatialMultiplexing_4x4or4x2** then spatialMode = Open loop spatial multiplexing****

The IE pdschBundleSize shall be set according to bundleSize from pdschConfig (see 5G_L2_IF_428_replaced([10975561](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VBsNfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_3208_replaced([11139675](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krpGw_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). When bundleSize is wideband, pdschBundleSize is equal to the maximum number of PRB of the scheduled bandwidth.

The value of IE pdschTbTransmitPower is calculated in chapter 5G_UP_ALG_2549_replaced([11118308](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqB9OfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (DL Power Control). Expected value are -34.9dBFS for below 6GHz configuration & -28.9 dBFS for above 6GHz .

The IE dmrsScramblingSequenceInt shall be set to

  * The physical cell ID (physCellId in PsCell_CellSetupReq) is used for all PDSCH transmisisons scheduled by a DCI not scrambled with a C-RNTI (RA-RNTI or TC-RNTI). Otherwise, 5G-L2-PS uses then dmrsScramblingId_0 (_nscId set to 0) or dmrsScramblingId_1 (nscId set to 1), according to 5G_UP_ALG_24560_replaced([11096248](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmuKgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), for any PDSCH transmissions scheduled by a DCI scrambled with a C-RNTI._
  * The scrambling codes are received from C-Plane (see 5G_L2_IF_392_replaced([10974781](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U-B1fu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for detail).



The IE pdschScramblingSeqInit shall be set to the physical cell ID (physCellId in PsCell_CellSetupReq) of the corresponding subcell. **NOTE.** pdschScramblingSeqInit is added into DlData_PdschSendReq so that different values can be used for each cell which is utilizing the pooled subcell (this will avoid L1-DL (IP block Leka_tx) limitation to have same pdschScramblingSeqInit for all pooled subcells).****

The IE dlPtrsFlag is set according to enableDlPtrs received in 5G_L2_IF_428_replaced([10975561](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VBsNfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

PTRS IEs are set according to 5G_UP_ALG_4666_replaced([11192615](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvlyqPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The IE nscId shall be set to 0 or 1 (see 5G_UP_ALG_4405_replaced([11142329](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kr3wSfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

When actRateMatchedCsiIm is true, during SA transient phase, in msg2 slot when rateMatchedCsiImInMsg2Slot is true (see 5G_L2_IF_122_replaced([10969219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UbPTPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or in CSI-IM slot when rateMacthedCsiImInMsg2Slot is false (see 5G_L2_IF_122_replaced([10969219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UbPTPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the IE startPrb shall be set according to 5G_L2_3106_replaced([11178546](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27AkxPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and the IE numOfPrb shall be set according to the size of the granted number of PRBs (5G_UP_ALG_4489_replaced([11179193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku4oAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) with max value according to 5G_L2_3106_replaced([11178546](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27AkxPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In other cases:

The IE startPrb shall be set according to the start of the UE bandwidth part (5G_UP_ALG_1823_replaced([11110957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpJMY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**. For PDSCH during transient phase which is corresponding to the period between receiving PsUser_UserModifyReq and receiving PsUser_UserReconfCompletedReq, IE startPrb = [image-0][image_desc]The image is entirely black, with no discernible features, text, or patterns.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_5655.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] + coresetFreqDomain + coresetFreqDomainRbShift (refer to 5G_UP_ALG_4463_replaced([11178704](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2LzPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

The IE numOfPrb shall be set according to the size of the granted number of PRBs (5G_UP_ALG_4492_replaced([11179250](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku4oB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If given UE allocation was affected by FD-POLITE PRB widening loop (see [12533165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_jm0A4Bw4EfCQJ5daVHVkgg?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) IEs startPrb and numOfPrb shall be filled based on the final values in the last successful FD-POLITE attempt.

The IE numOfPdschSymbols shall be set to 11 if rdDataSlotTypes is set to 1 and IE numOfPdschSymbols shall be set to 10 if rdDataSlotTypes is set to 2 or 3.

The IE numOfPdschSymbols shall be set according to PDSCH configuration of current slot as per 5G_UP_ALG_2375_replaced([11115218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpr-_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**.**

The IE startSymbol shall be set according to PDSCH configuration of current slot as per 5G_UP_ALG_2375_replaced([11115218](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpr-_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**.**

The IE dlDmrsConfigType shall be set to the value of Dmrs Type parameter received in PsUser_SetupReq or PsUser_ModifyReq.

The IE dlDmrsLen shall be set to 1 according to 5G_UP_ALG_24560_replaced([11096248](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmuKgvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**.**

The IE dlDmrsMappingType shall be set to TypeA.

The IE dlDmrsAddPos is set according to the value of dmrsAdditionalPosition set in PsUser_UserSetupReq **or PsUser_UserModifyReq, see 5G_L2_IF_428_replaced([10975561](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VBsNfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)). **When adaptive re-transmission scheme is applied, see 5G_UP_ALG_11943_replaced([11184268](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvRCjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) dlDmrsAddPos is set according to the value of dmrsAdditionalPosition but with this value reduced if the number of DL symbol in the retransmission slot do not allow all requested positions see 38.211 Table 7.4.1.1.2-3: PDSCH DM-RS positions [image-1][image_desc]The image is too blurry to describe in detail.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_5655.002.png[/image_path][/image-1] for single-symbol DM-RS.****

The IE dlDmrsTypeAPos is read from dmrsTypeAPosition parameter in PsCell_CellSetupReq (see 5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The IE baseGraph (BG), numOfCodeBlocks (C), codeBlockSize (K), numOfFillerBits (F), liftSize (Z) ,liftSizeSetIndex (set_index), liftSizeColumnIndex (column_index) are set according to 5G_UP_ALG_6874_replaced([11192598](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvlypfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the number of DMRS OFDM being equal to (dlDmrsLen + dlDmrsAddPos). The IE ncb and k0divZ are computed as described in 5G_UP_ALG_4664_replaced([11192587](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvlyo_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The IE modulationOrder is set to 2 for a QPSK, 4 for a 16QAM, 6 for a 64QAM, 8 for a 256QAM, 10 for a 1024QAM. The modulationOrder field is filled according the Qm modulation order field and Imcs value listed in the following table (see 5G_L1_5G21A_722 for DL & 5G_UP_ALG_1006_replaced([11103434](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_knveN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UL too):

1) for PDSCH if DL UE capability is 1024QAM: table 5.1.3.1-4 in 38.214 §5.1.3.1. 

2) for PDSCH if DL UE capability is 256QAM: table 5.1.3.1-2 in 38.214 §5.1.3.1.

3) for PDSCH if DL UE capability is not 256QAM[1024QAM (only 64QAM) and for PUSCH: table 5.1.3.1-1 in 38.214 §5.1.3.1.

The IE rvIndex is set according to 5G_UP_ALG_13534_replaced([11184166](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbfvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), it shall be identical to the value set in the DL DCI.

The IE mcsTable is set to 64QAM.

The IE bestBeamPowerOffset is set according to 5G_UP_ALG_13465_replaced([11118538](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqDyZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

For other cases than conformance testing, IE rat0Bitmap shall be set according to 5G_UP_ALG_4459_replaced([11178370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2LwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Note that the MSB of Frequency resource Assignment in 5G_UP_ALG_4459_replaced([11178370](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku2LwvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) is the first RBG of the BWP. The MSB of rat0Bitmap is the first RBG from CRB0. Also, the parameters startPrb & numOfPrb are redundant with rat0Bitmap but they are needed in L1 in order to facilitate rate maching.

The IE numOfDmrsCdmGroupWithoutData shall be set to 2.

For FDD NR **and TDD NR, if the number of DMRS CDM group(s) without data is 1(refer to 5G_UP_ALG_3054_replaced([11129150](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq6uCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), IE numOfDmrsCdmGroupWithoutData shall be set to 1.**

In case that at least 1 one UE was scheduled via DlData_PdschSendReq the PM Counter handling described in 5G_L2_325_replaced([11192719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28mgM_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_348_replaced([11197550](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_29M9KvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) shall be performed.

In case of A1 subcell type L2 PS shall set _numCeAxCIndex = 1_ , ceAxcIndex = (0). patternId is omitted**

For analog beamforming for eCPRI RUs, L2 PS shall indicate beam of the corresponding UE through _numCeAxCIndex and_ ceAxcIndex and _patternId in DlData_PdschSendReq according to 5G_L1_5G21A_86 as_ **

_numCeAxCIndex number of eAxC index for D2 subcell type according to 5G_L1_5G21A_868._

_ceAxcIndex eAxC index of default data for D2 subcell type according to 5G_L1_5G21A_868 and 5G_UP_ALG_22399_replaced([11193226](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvqrJ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))._

_patternId map beam Id to pattern Id according to 5G_UP_ALG_1909_replaced([11111524](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOE7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).In case that one _patternId used for four _numStreamIndex case according to 5G_L2_5017_replaced([11165649](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25zD0vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L1_IF_112_replaced([11512969](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRteZfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the other _patternId filled in the same value as the first one.****

When supercell mode is enabled (numOfSuperSubcells >= 2) L2 PS shall set _patternId to 0 in DlData_PdschSendReq._

CP2 references:

\- 5G_UP_ALG_4665_replaced([11192609](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvlyp_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Configuration of 5G-L2-LO and 5G-L1-DL for Transport Block Transmission

##### 2.5.1.6.2.0-4 Sending DlData_PdschSendReq Request for RA Msg2, RA Msg4, SRB0 Transport Block transmission to 5G-L1-DL (ID: 11178509)

**2.5.1.6.2.0-4.0-5**  (ID: `11178539`)

Sending DlData_PdschSendReq 5G-L2-PS shall request the transmission of a RA Msg2 by sending the message DlData_PdschSendReq to 5G-L1-DL for each of them.

5G-L2-PS shall request the transmission of a RA SRB0 message/Msg4 by sending the message DlData_PdschSendReq to 5G-L1-DL.

The IEs are set as in 5G_L2_887_replaced([11178401](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26_9tfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) with the following exceptions:

For RA Msg2, the IE mcs is set as mentioned in 5G_UP_ALG_4627_replaced([11192210](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvivXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For SRB0 message/Msg4, the IE mcs is set to the one determined from 5G_UP_ALG_4628_replaced([11192229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvjWYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The IE rnti is set to RA-RNTI for RA Msg2.

The IE rnti is set to TC-RNTI for RA SRB0 message/Msg4.

For RA Msg2 when actRateMatchedCsiIm is true and rateMacthedCsiImInMsg2Slot is true (see 5G_L2_IF_122_replaced([10969219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UbPTPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) :

The IEs startPrb and numOfPrb shall be set according to 5G_L2_3106_replaced([11178546](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27AkxPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For other cases:

The IEs startPrb shall be set according to the start of the initial bandwidth part (5G_UP_ALG_1817_replaced([11110897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpIlVPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The IEs numOfPrb shall be set according to the size of the granted number of PRBs for RA message (5G_UP_ALG_4489_replaced([11179193](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ku4oAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

The IE numOfPrb shall be set to the size of the initial DL BWP.

For RA Msg2,The IE numOfLayers is set as mentioned in 5G_UP_ALG_4627_replaced([11192210](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvivXPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For SRB0 message/Msg4, the IE numOfLayers is set as mentioned in 5G_UP_ALG_4628_replaced([11192229](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvjWYfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[Before PR664928]

The IE spatialMode shall be set as according to 5G_UP_ALG_3171_replaced([11139234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krlca_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[PR664928]

Spatial mode:

dlMimoMode == SingleAntennaTransmission_1x1 then spatialMode = Single Antenna

dlMimoMode == ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_2x2 or ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_4x4or4x2 or ClosedLoopSpatialMultiplexing_8x4 then spatialMode = Closed loop spatial multiplexing

dlMimoMode == OpenLoopSpatialMultiplexing_2x2 or OpenLoopSpatialMultiplexing_4x4or4x2 then spatialMode = Open loop spatial multiplexing

[End PR664928]

The IE antPort is set to 0x8000 for antennaPort 1000 (5G_RAN_UP_12963).

For SRB0 message/Msg4, the IE antPort is set to 0x8000 for antennaPort 1000.

The IE dlPtrsConfig shall be set to 0, meaning no PTRS is configured.

For SRB0 message/Msg4, the IE dlPtrsConfig shall be set to 0, meaning no PTRS is configured.

For SRB0 message/Msg4, the IE mcsTable is set to 64QAM.

Additionally to be compliant with 5G_RAN_UP_12982 3GPP requirement, DMRS shall be configured such as dlDmrsMappingType=TypeA, dlDmrsLen=1, dlDmrsAddPos=2, dlDmrsTypeAPos=2.

dlDmrsTypeAPos is read from dmrsTypeAPosition parameter in PsCell_CellSetupReq (see 5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

For SRB0 Message/Msg4, DMRS shall be configured such as dlDmrsMappingType=TypeA, dlDmrsLen=1, dlDmrsAddPos=2, dlDmrsTypeAPos is read from dmrsTypeAPosition parameter in PsCell_CellSetupReq (see 5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

##### 2.5.1.6.2.0-5 Sending DlData_PdschSendReq Calculating max PRB allocation in initial BWP in presence of CSI-IM (ID: 11178546)

**2.5.1.6.2.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `12799437`)

Sending DlData_PdschSendReq [CB007372-A]  
For DSS with NRCELL.NRDSSLTE.actAsymmetricDss=true there is no CSI-IM and Msg2 in the same slot (see [11115079](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpqw2vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).  
[End CB007372-A]

The following calculation is applicable to FDD DSS cell, in msg2 slot, when actRateMatchedCsiIm is true and rateMacthedCsiImInMsg2Slot is true (see 5G_L2_IF_122_replaced([10969219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UbPTPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), for transmission of msg2 (see 5G_L2_890_replaced([11178509](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26_9vvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and transmission during SA transient phase (see 5G_L2_887_replaced([11178401](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26_9tfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or when actRateMatchedCsiIm is true and rateMacthedCsiImInMsg2Slot is false (see 5G_L2_IF_122_replaced([10969219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UbPTPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in CSI-IM slot for transmission during SA transient phase (see 5G_L2_887_replaced([11178401](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26_9tfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **.**

The purpose is to exclude PRBs containing ZP CSI-RS.

Input parameters (from cell setup):

NRB: DL cell bandwidth

start of initial DL BWP (in CRB), size of initial DL BWP

zpCsiRsStartingPrb, zpCsiRsNumOfPrbs: see 5G_L2_IF_124_replaced([10969280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Ub2U_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))

Output parameters:

startPrb: start PRB (in CRB)

numOfPrb: number of PRBs (case of msg2) or max number of PRBs (case of SA transient phase)

IF zpCsiRsStartingPrb < ceil(NRB/8) * 4 THEN

(CSI IM is in lower half bandwidth)

IF (zpCsiRsStartingPrb+zpCsiRsNumOfPrbs > start of initial bandwidth part) THEN

The IE startPrb shall be set to zpCsiRsStartingPrb+zpCsiRsNumOfPrbs

The IE numOfPrb shall be set to size of initial bandwidth part - (zpCsiRsStartingPrb+zpCsiRsNumOfPrbs - start of initial bandwidth part)

ELSE

The IE startPrb shall be set to start of initial bandwidth part

The IE numOfPrb shall be set to size of initial bandwidth part

END

ELSE

(CSI IM is in upper half bandwidth)

The IE startPrb shall be set to the start of the initial bandwidth part

The IE numOfPrb shall be set to min (size of initial bandwidth part, zpCsiRsStartingPrb - start of initial bandwidth part)

END

---

##### 2.5.1.6.2.0-6 Sending DlData_PdschSendReq Setting pdschRtBfConfig (ID: 11178562)

**2.5.1.6.2.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11178573`)

Sending DlData_PdschSendReq In eCPRI 7-2e (5G_L2_18130_replaced([11155228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2432wvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ) ,

If subband RT Beamforming is enable by IE actDlSrsSubbandBm =True in CellSetupReq ,[Before CB009527-E] and PDSCH allocation is not RAT1 which is triggered by transient phase [End CB009527-E] , and PRB mapping to SrsQualityTable and it is qualify to use SB beam ( no matter it is New TX or re-trans) , and it is scheduled as SB RT beam, refer 5G_UP_ALG_21411_replaced([11156802](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks3OzvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), then

1; PdschRtBfConfig shall be filled

2; rtBfUeIndex

3; patternID[0] & patternID[1] = 0xffff ( 0xffff as invalid value)

[CB009527-E]

4; eirpEnable (indication of EIRP coefficient computation, the UE shall schedule as RT Beamforming UE of this slot)

[End CB009527-E]

Else Fallback to legacy beam , and also rtBfUeIndex with MSB bits 0~3 , value =0.

##### 2.5.1.6.2.0-7 Sending DlData_PdschSendReq Setting bwvDumpGranularityInSubbands (ID: 11178580)

**2.5.1.6.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11178584`)

Sending DlData_PdschSendReq [CB009527-C]

1; bwvDumpGranularityInSubbands

LSB 7, it is filled by rdSampleStoreMethod, refer 5G_UP_ALG_27818_replaced([11158833](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktFRNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

LSB 0~6, it is filled by selBwvSubband, refer 5G_UP_ALG_27826_replaced([11156590](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks2AoPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

if HARQ-TX is new TX

selBwvSubband= rdSamplingRatePdsch, refer 5G_UP_ALG_27824_replaced([11158854](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktFROfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Else HARQ-ReTX

selBwvSubband= roundup(0.5* rdSamplingRatePdsch)

[End CB009527-C]

### 2.5.1.7 Physical Downlink Shared Channel Send Response

#### 2.5.1.7.0-1 Physical Downlink Shared Channel Send Response Description (ID: 11178598)

**2.5.1.7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11178601`)

Physical Downlink Shared Channel Send Response The purpose of message is to get the eirp coefficients response from L1 (L1 gets response from RU) for RT beamforming UE , this is because in eCPRI7-2e (5G_L2_18130_replaced([11155228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2432wvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the calculation of RT beamforming weight is triggered by message of Dldata_PdschSendReq and weight will be applied in same slot in RU side.

### 2.5.1.8 Channel-State Information Reference Signal Send

#### 2.5.1.8.1 Exceptions

##### 2.5.1.8.1.0-1 Exceptions Expected Exceptions (ID: 11178631)

#### 2.5.1.8.2 Calculation of K Bitmap (freqDomainAllocationKi IE in DlData_CsiRsSendReq) from L3 Configuration Parameters

##### 2.5.1.8.2.0-1 Calculation of K Bitmap (freqDomainAllocationKi IE in DlData_CsiRsSendReq) from L3 Configuration Parameters As specified in 38.211 § 7.4.1.5.3, the K Bitmap can be deduced from the L3 parameters B Bitmap and row number. Requirement 5G_L1_5G21A_799 describes the algorithm to calculate the K Bitmap from those. For CSI-RS for channel measurements the B Bitmap and the row number parameters are received within PsUser_UserSetupReq message: frequencyLocationBitmap and locationConfig IEs respectively. (ID: 11178649)

#### 2.5.1.8.3 Setting patternID

##### 2.5.1.8.3.0-1 Setting patternID (ID: 11178660)

**2.5.1.8.3.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `13343309`)

Setting patternID [CB008577-E] For TDD: [End CB008577-E]

In eCPRI 7-2e (5G_L2_18130_replaced([11155228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2432wvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ) ,

If RT beam is enabled for UE specific CSI-RS ( NRBTS/NRCELL/actDlSrsSubbandBm =True && rdCSIRSUseRTBeam=Enable ), && and a random valid SRS subband is selected for calclulating of CSI-RS BWV (refer 5G_UP_ALG_21094_replaced([11156669](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks2ns_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_18883_replaced([11171429](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26N6nPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

then L2 shal set PID as special value as WA, detail refer 5G_L1_IF_109_replaced([11513175](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRusjvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**pattnerIds[0] = 0xFFFE – represent this resource is used for SB or WB RT beam, in eCPRI, according to ORAN spec, valid range of beamId is 0~32767, L2-Ps shall use specific ID over 32767 without PatternId reservation.**

pattnerId[1] = ueIndex : LSB0~11, refer 5G_L1_IF_15303_replaced([11512951](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRteYPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

pattnerId[2] = StartPrb : StartPrb of selected BF SB for CSI-RS =StartPrb of SrsSb + (SizeSrsSb/2).

pattnerId[3] = Invalid 0XFFFF.

Else CSI-RS shall fallback to legacy beam, and PID is filled as legacy beam as 5G_L2_10506_replaced([11155506](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_245r8PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: L3 will make sure the startPrb of Srs SB align with BF SB. SrsSubbandSize is srs subband size and it is 4 Prb based, by checking table of 38.211 Table 6.4.1.4.3-1: SRS bandwidth configuration during UE's SRS resource allocation.

[CB008577-E] For FDD: 

In case of FDD Beamforming (NRCELL/actBeamforming = True and NRCELL.cellTechnology is equal to 'FDD'), 

If CSI-RS is row16 (locationconfig=16 , [12822322: perCsiRsResConfig structure content](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI__bO-U6m3EfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)), 8 patternIDs are required per L1 CSI-RS resource.

1st L1 CSI-RS resource:

patternId[i]=Ps_[i] , (i ∈ (0,7))

2nd L1 CSI-RS resource:

patternId[i]=Ps_[i+8] , (i ∈ (0,7))

3rd L1 CSI-RS resource:

patternId[i]=Ps_[i] , (i ∈ (0,7))

4th L1 CSI-RS resource:

patternId[i]=Ps_[i+8] , (i ∈ (0,7))

where Ps_[ ] are the CSI-RS beam patternID (split pannel based )are configured to L2PS through [12679725: bfSetupFdd structure content as bellow:](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_YhGc0E_iEfCeeMlEb49MrQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) , total 16 CSI-RS patternIDs will be configured to L2PS for 32 port CSI-RS.

[End CB008577-E]

eCpriConfigL1sw:

**[End CB103440-B]**

[CB008577-D]

For FDD Beamforming (NRCELL/actBeamforming = True and NRCELL.cellTechnology is equal to 'FDD') {

When PDSCH scheduling is triggered by artificial PDSCH load for DL performance testing which is defined in [11212150: General principles of artificial PDSCH load for DL performance testing](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2-joA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) and Configurable Artifical Load Generation which is defined in [11149986: Configurable Artifical Load Generation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24ZVr_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)

The Precoding related parameter setting shall apply the same mechanism as normal PDSCH 's scheduling CSI valid case, but due to this is fake UE, there is no CSI will be reported, L2PS will assume as 32 port CSI configuration with PMI_i2 as Zero to set the codebookIndex or/and i2Codebook4AntPorts (CSI not valid or common PDSCH case is not valid for artifical load).

The supporting rank follow the legacy artificial PDSCH load for DL performance testing and Configurable Artifical Load Generation's definition.

When PDCCH scheduling is triggered by artificial PDCCH load, due to implementation complexity, SW doesn't check the DCI format to distinguish the PDCCH for DL or UL , then it will be unlike the normal UE's scheduling to split to different streams, but this leaves to implementation because this doesn't impact the load generation and measurement. 

}

[End CB008577-D]

## 2.5.2 Interactions with L1-UL

### 2.5.2.0-2 Interactions with L1-UL L1-UL Message split between ABIL/FPGA and following HW Variant (ID: 11178763)

**2.5.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `13401546`)

Interactions with L1-UL The following UlData_* messages:

  * UlData_PucchReceiveReq
  * UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs
  * UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU
  * UlData_PuschReceiveRespLo
  * UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD
  * UlData_PucchReceiveRespHarqD



are separated between ABIL/FPGA and following HW variants (ABIO, ABIP [CB014419-SR-EB] , ABIR [End CB014419-SR-EB]).

The reason is that FPGA on ABIL has reached its hardware limits and cannot support any further adaptation of the L1-L2 Interface.

ABIL/FPGA messages will be renamed adding the suffix “Loner”:

  * UlData_PucchReceiveReqLoner
  * UlData_PucchReceiveRespPsLoner
  * UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqULoner
  * UlData_PuschReceiveRespLoLoner
  * UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqDLoner
  * UlData_PucchReceiveRespHarqDLoner



while ABIO/ABIP [CB014419-SR-EB] /ABIR [End CB014419-SR-EB] messages will be renamed adding the suffix “L1sw”:

  * UlData_PucchReceiveReqL1sw
  * UlData_PucchReceiveRespPsL1sw
  * UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqUL1sw
  * UlData_PuschReceiveRespLoL1sw
  * UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqDL1sw
  * UlData_PucchReceiveRespHarqDL1sw



Throughout this module these messages are referred by the name without suffix.

---

### 2.5.2.1 General Exceptions on the UlData Interface

#### 2.5.2.1.0-1 General Exceptions on the UlData Interface Expected Exceptions (ID: 11178780)

**2.5.2.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11178785`)

General Exceptions on the UlData Interface 5G-L2-PS may send out a limited amount of receive request messages late, such that L1-UL receives them after the closure of the L1 receive window. The L1 receive window for UlData_RimReceiveReq is defined in 5G_L1_IF_14869_replaced([11514904](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR6SsvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), for the other receive request messages it is defined in 5G_L1_IF_283_replaced([11514791](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5rpPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In the sequel, message X is a placeholder for exactly 1 of the following message names:

  * UlData_PuschReceiveReq (5G_L1_IF_183_replaced([11513708](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRyW7_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * UlData_PucchReceiveReq (5G_L1_IF_212_replaced([11513942](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MFfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * UlData_PrachReceiveReq (5G_L1_IF_228_replaced([11514270](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2oUvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * UlData_SrsReceiveReq (5G_L1_IF_235_replaced([11514315](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2oW_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))
  * UlData_RimReceiveReq (5G_L1_IF_14744_replaced([11514580](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR4dhPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))



5G-L2-PS shall obey the following rules:

  * During a time span of 5 slots after processing a PsCell_CellSetupReq (5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), a PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq (5G_L2_IF_220_replaced([10970911](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UlnW_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or a PsCell_CellDeleteReq (5G_L2_IF_179_replaced([10970510](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UjLHPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) 5G-L2-PS may send messages X late in any cell deployed on the same CPU core.



Rationale:

Cell procedures are not running in the background and take multiple slots to be completed. During the first slots after a cell procedure 5G-L2-PS has to process tasks which piled up during the procedure, thus message transmissions towards L1-UL can be delayed.

  * When the above time span has ended, the number of late messages X in a cell shall not exceed 1% of all messages X sent in the same cell within any given time interval of 1 second.



Rationale:

5G-L2-PS can send request messages to L1-UL only after UE scheduling. Since the processing time needed for UE scheduling in a certain slot can't be predicted, it is unavoidable that request messages are sent out late from time to time, in particular when the load on 5G-L2-PS is high.

Also, the message propagation delay on the L1-L2 interface is variable and not exactly known to 5G-L2-PS.

Note: L1-UL drops request messages which it receives after the message receive window and it doesn't perform the corresponding requests.

---

### 2.5.2.2 Handling of eCPRI fields

#### 2.5.2.2.0-1 Handling of eCPRI fields Definition of IE eCpriSectionID (ID: 11178796)

**2.5.2.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11178807`)

Handling of eCPRI fields The FD allocation region in UL where the FD BF applied is identified by region-ID of 5 bits and this value is used to set the fields of the eCpriSectionID which is represented by 12 bits mask (bb rrrrr RRRRR) binary, where:

  * ‘bb’ (2bits) : for future use, in the meanwhile set to zero; used by eCPRI extension type ‘A’ format, is always set to ‘00’



 ‘rrrrr’ (5bits) : for future use, in the meanwhile set to zero; region number for second hop, in case of intra-slot frequency hopping (useful for CB006466-B), (tracks upto 32 regions).

 ‘RRRRR’ (5bits): region ID for the UL FD allocation (tracks upto 32 regions)

e.g. eCpriSectionID = 00 00000 00011: represents region ID= 3 in binary for an UL FD allocation, no Frequency Hopping

[CB006135-A]

If compliance to O-RAN IF has to be guaranteed (see 5G_UP_ALG_5163_replaced([11204341](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkDDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), following 12bit mask representation is used for eCpriSectionId:

  * (CCCC aaaaaaaa) binary,
  * 'CCCC' (4bit) : represents the channel, to which the allocation is being made:



0000 : PRACH

0010 : PUSCH

0100 : PUCCH

1000 : SRS

1111 : reserved

  * 'aaaaaaaa' (8 bit): represents integer numbers, that shall be unique per slot (and per channel)
  * [PR596514] The numbering scheme is reset to 0 at the slot boundaries. [End PR596514]



The eCpriSectionID computation at L2PS is done for UlData_PrachReceiveReq, UlData_PuschReceiveReq, UlData_PucchReceiveReq andUlData_SrsReceiveReq.

The reserved pool of IDs is for L1H usage: In situations, when numPrb has value (255, 272) PRBs, single section is not enough (due to 8b length of numPrbc field). L1H creates 2 FCP sections out of such large allocation, and sets the eCpriSectionId to one of the reserved values

Note, the reserved pool of IDs is for L1H usage (transparent to L2-PS), because if single PUSCH allocation is between 255 and 272 PRB large, then single section is not enough (due to 8 bit length of numPrbc field). L1H creates 2 FCP sections out of such large allocations, and sets the eCpriSectionId to one of the reserved values.

[End CB006135-A]

The eCpriSectionID computation at L2PS is done for UlData_PrachReceiveReq, UlData_PuschReceiveReq, UlData_PucchReceiveReq andUlData_SrsReceiveReq.

---

#### 2.5.2.2.0-2 Handling of eCPRI fields Setting of IE eCpriSectionID in UlData_PuschReceiveReq (ID: 11178814)

**2.5.2.2.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11178826`)

Handling of eCPRI fields For UlData_PuschReceiveReq, eCpriSectionID assignment for each grant on each subcell is as below:

  * In a data slot with no PRACH, only PUSCH [CB006064-D] and Long PUCCH [End CB006064-D] is scheduled during PUSCH symbols across subcells



for subcellId = 0 to numSubcell -1

for j = 0 to numOfGrants of subcell=subcellId

regionId= (numOfGrants of (subcellId - 1)) * subcellId + j

RRRRR =(regionId) binary //assign region ID with 5bit binary value

eCpriSectionID =00 00000 RRRRR // for grant j in in subcell = subcellId

[CB006064-D] the highest assigned regionId shall be remembered as highestPuschRegionId [End CB006064-D]

end

end

  * In PRACH slot, if multiplexing is enabled and if PUSCH (with UL dedicated BWP) is FDM scheduled [CB006064-D] Note: FDM of PUSCH, dedicated LongPUCCH, PRACH, CommonPUCCH may exist in the slot[End CB006064-D]. Reserve regionID=0 to numPrachOccasion_FD-1 to the PRACH to be statically configured by L1, and assign only the rest of regionID values to PUSCH grants, if any in the slot, as follows:



for subcellId = 0 to numSubcell -1

for j = 0 to numOfGrants of subcell=subcellId

regionId= (numOfGrants of (subcellId - 1)) * subcellId + j + numPrachOccasion

RRRRR =(regionId) binary //assign region ID with 5bit binary value

eCpriSectionID =00 00000 RRRRR // for grant j in in subcell = subcellId

[CB006064-D] the highest assigned regionId shall be remembered as highestPuschRegionId [End CB006064-D]

end

end

[CB006064-D] highestPuschRegionId shall be initialized with 1 (for UL slots without PUSCH) [End CB006064-D]

---

#### 2.5.2.2.0-3 Handling of eCPRI fields Setting of IE eCpriSectionID in UlData_SrsReceiveReq (ID: 11178831)

**2.5.2.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11178835`)

Handling of eCPRI fields For UlData_SrsReceiveReq (5G_L1_5G21A_241), the eCpriSectionID is computed for each SRS Bandwidth configuration list per subcell.

\- This region ID calculation is applicable for the supported aperiodic SRS configuration in UL Data slot for SU-MIMO as per srsAllocationConfig parameter (5G_L1_5G21A_246) of the srsSuMimo struct (5G_L1_5G21A_243).

\- Currently, only wideband aperiodic SRS configuration is supported in FR1-TDD for SU-MIMO, hence, only one FD BF region for SRS in the srs symbol (regionId=0) in Data slot (5G_L1_5G21A_1260).

\- i.e. eCpriSectionID =00 00000 00000; for each UlData_SrsReceiveReq per subcell.

---

#### 2.5.2.2.0-4 Handling of eCPRI fields Setting of IE eCpriSectionID in UlData_PucchReceiveReq in case of short PUCCH (ID: 11178840)

**2.5.2.2.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11178846`)

Handling of eCPRI fields In case of short PUCCH (format 0 and 2), for UlData_PucchReceiveReq, eCpriSectionID is computed for each allocated resource per control data received on PUCCH to decode.

\- Dedicated PUCCH format 0/2: transmitted over 1 symbol, hence, no Frequency Hopping.

\- Common PUCCH Format 0, in SA Mode if configured for Msg4/SRB0 ACK, transmitted over 1 or 2 symbols and Frequency Hopping (FH) is enabled if 2 symbols is used.

\- eCpriSectionID for PUCCH is an array: first entry is for first hop in the first PUCCH symbol and second entry for second hop in the second symbol (if supported and enabled). If FH not supported or enabled, second entry is not assigned.

\- Note: as long as a unique region ID is assigned, same value can be always used for first hop and second hop, if FH is enabled.

if CommonPUCCHFormat0 in the slot and numberOfSymbols =2 with FH enabled

//assign region ID=0 for both hops of common PUCCH

eCpriSectionID[x] =00 00000 00000 //for both entry the common PUCCH resource

nextRegionIdStart=1:// start region id from 1 for the dedicated resources

if more than one common PUCCH resource with FH in the slot, assign the next region ID and set the value of

nextRegionIdStart =numberofcommonPUCCH with FH enabled in the slot

else

nextRegionIdStart=0;

end

\- For dedicated PUCCH resources per each symbol, assign region id as follows.

for subcellId = 0 to numSubcell -1

for j = nextRegionIdStart to numOfPucchResources of subcell=subcellId

regionId= (numOfPucchResourcesof of (subcellId - 1) )* subcellId + j

RRRRR =(regionId) binary //assign region ID with 5bit binary value

eCpriSectionID[0] =00 00000 RRRRR // for resource j in subcell = subcellId

end

end

---

#### 2.5.2.2.0-5 Handling of eCPRI fields Setting of IE eCpriSectionID in UlData_PucchReceiveReq in case of long PUCCH (ID: 11178853)

**2.5.2.2.0-5.0-4**  (ID: `11178878`)

Handling of eCPRI fields highestUlRegionId = highestPuschRegionId

If current slot is marked for RI measurement reception (see 5G_L2_8282_replaced([11175546](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26tCyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB006991-C] or RIM-RS reception (see 5G_L2_11755_replaced([11175442](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26r0rPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB006991-C], 5G-L2-PS shall increment highestUlRegionId by 1.

In case of long PUCCH (PUCCH formats 1 and 3), if PUCCH Format 3 beamforming is disabled (5G_UP_ALG_2215_replaced([11113083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), sector beam is used for all PUCCH allocations. There are 4 sections (of contiguous PRBs) in spectrum carrying only PUCCH, if any. Each section requires assignment of a unique eCpriSectionId set within UlData_PucchReceiveReq’s structure staticLongPucchConfigEcpri as follows:

Structures eCpriPucchResourceAllocationLowerDedicated and eCpriPucchResourceAllocationUpperDedicated contain UE dedicated PUCCH format 1 and/or PUCCH format 3 (for CSI, SR, HARQ AN). Their eCpriSectionId are set as follows:

eCpriPucchResourceAllocationLowerDedicated.eCpriSectionId = highestUlRegionId + 1

eCpriPucchResourceAllocationUpperDedicated.eCpriSectionId = highestUlRegionId + 2

Structures eCpriPucchResourceAllocationLowerCommon and

eCpriPucchResourceAllocationUpperCommon contain common PUCCH format 1 for HARQ AN of Msg4/SRB0. Their eCpriSectionId are set as follows:

eCpriPucchResourceAllocationLowerDedicated.eCpriSectionId = highestUlRegionId + 3

eCpriPucchResourceAllocationUpperDedicated.eCpriSectionId = highestUlRegionId + 4

If PUCCH Format 3 beamforming is enabled (5G_UP_ALG_2215_replaced([11113083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then UlData_PucchReceiveReq’s structure staticLongPucchConfigEcpri is not used. Instead, the eCpriSectionId is to be set for each individual PUCCH (via eCpriConfig structure) as follows:

All PUCCHs of a cell (over all its subcells) that are received on the same (combination of) patternIds shall get the same eCpriSectionId.

For example, in 4RX case, PUCCH F3 starting on PRB 6 and other PUCCH F3 starting on PRB 48 have to get the same eCpriSectionId if both are received on same beams (e.g. SSB beam 1 on Xpol0 and SSB beam 4 on Xpol1). 

All PUCCHs of a cell (over all its subcells) that are received on different (combination of) patternIds shall have different eCpriSectionId, i.e. eCpriSectionId shall be unique in that sense.

E.g. in similar example as above, PUCCH F3 starting on PRB 6 and other PUCCH F3 starting on PRB 48 have to get different eCpriSectionId if both are not received on same beams (e.g. one F3 on SSB beam 1 and 4 whereas other F3 on SSB beam 1 and 3, or one F3 on SSB beam 1 and sector beam whereas other F3 on SSB beam 2 and sector beam). 

The lowest eCpriSectionId assignable to PUCCH shall be highestUlRegionId + 1.

Note, it is ensured that maximum available number of regions/sections supported by the RU is not exceeded, see 5G_UP_ALG_2214_replaced([11113079](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSKvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for details.

highestPuschRegionId is given in 5G_L2_462_replaced([11178814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27CZ8fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

eCpriSectionId is defined in 5G_L2_2878_replaced([11178796](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27By7vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note, each long PUCCH has length 14 symbols with intra-slot frequency hopping enabled (hopping after half of the PUCCH length).

If PUCCH Format 3 beamforming is enabled (5G_UP_ALG_2215_replaced([11113083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSLPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), For the cases where in every UlData_PucchReceiveReq for L1-UL, having staticLongPucchConfigEcpri structure filled, when NRBTS/NRCELL/actDynUlResAlloc = ‘True’ , L2PS shall fill startprb and numprb in eCpriPucchResourceAllocationLowerDedicated and eCpriPucchResourceAllocationUpperDedicated) considering configuration of Long PUCCH F3 position changes dynamically every UL slot based on the highestPcsiPrbUsed(see 5G_L2_9101_replaced([11171997](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26SMDfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for calculations.) for CP2 requirements see 5G_UP_ALG_5166_replaced([11204379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkqIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

in case the NIDD parameter NRBTS/NRCELL/actDynUlResAlloc is set to false, then the L2PS shall continue to fill statically like as before (i.e., based on PUCCH allocation configurations received from L3 Cell Setup).

---

#### 2.5.2.2.0-6 Handling of eCPRI fields Setting of IE eCpriSectionID in UlData_RimReceiveReq (ID: 11178883)

**2.5.2.2.0-6.0-2**  (ID: `11178895`)

Handling of eCPRI fields For UlData_RimReceiveReq, eCpriSectionID assignment applies only to Unscheduled Regions. All Unscheduled Regions shall be assigned with one eCpriSectionId (see 5G_UP_ALG_5163_replaced([11204341](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkDDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

5G-L2-PS shall assign eCpriSectionID for UlData_PuschReceiveReq as follows:

RegionID = highestPuschRegionId + 1 // (see 5G_L2_462_replaced([11178814](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27CZ8fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for highestPuschRegionId)

RRRRR = (regionId) binary

eCpriSectionID = (00 00000 RRRR) binary

assign same eCpriSectionID to all Unscheduled Regions requested within the slot

If current slot is marked for RI measurement reception (see 5G_L2_8282_replaced([11175546](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26tCyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB006991-C] or RIM-RS reception (see 5G_L2_11755_replaced([11175442](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26r0rPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [End CB006991-C], 5G-L2-PS shall reserve RegionID = highestPuschRegionId + 1 for Unscheduled Regions for RI measurements [CB006991-C] and/or RIM-RS [End CB006991-C] allocation before proceeding with allocation of eCpriSectionID for Long PUCCH (see 5G_L2_2899_replaced([11178853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27CZ-fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

Note: UlData_RimReceiveReq does not support compliance with O-RAN IF.

---

#### 2.5.2.2.0-7 Handling of eCPRI fields Setting of IE eCpriSectionID for FDD BF (ID: 12708955)

**2.5.2.2.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `12708193`)

Handling of eCPRI fields For a FR1 FDD cell, if  _actBeamformingFdd (see_[10967202: PsCell_CellSetupReq Message Content](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) [CB008577-A] or otherwise if actBeamforming = TRUE[End CB008577-A] , for SU-MIMO, the eCpriSectionID shall be filled in compliance to O-RAN with 12 bits as [11178796: Definition of IE eCpriSectionID](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27By7vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), the lowest 8 bits for eCpriSectionID of PRACH can be hardcoded to 0, and PUSCH 1, for PUCCH F1/F3 it is hardcoded to 2, and SRS 3.

---

#### 2.5.2.2.0-8 Handling of eCPRI fields Setting of ceAxCIndex for PRACH reception (ID: 11178901)

**2.5.2.2.0-8.0-9**  (ID: `12827297`)

Handling of eCPRI fields The following describes how to set the ceAxCIndex in UlData_PrachReceiveReq:

eCpriFlag = true [PR852424] and associated prachOccasions[i] bit is set to 1 (where i = 0..7 according to [11514296](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2oWPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) [End PR852424]:

All subcell types:

When eCpriFlag is true, 5G-L2-PS uses the highest two ceAxCIndex choices (numCeAxCId-2, numCeAxCId-1) in the UlData_PrachReceiveReq. This is used to ensure that separate ceAxCIndex choices from data are used for PRACH allowing processing with different timing and filtering requirements.

if actEcpri72e is FALSE

**5G-L2-PS shall use as ceAxCIndex choices for UlData_PrachReceiveReq:**

\- For A2: the highest two

\- For A4: the highest four

\- For A8: the highest four if actPrachProbing is FALSE otherwise the highest 8

\- For C2: the highest 2*NRCELL-nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion

\- For C4,C8: the highest four (for NRCELL-nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion = 1 or 2) or highest eight (for NRCELL-nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion = 4)

else

\- For supported configurations C4'2 and C8'2 and C8'4 and C8'8**, [subcell type Cx’y where x is the number PUCCH streams and y is the number of MIMO layers Ref: 5G_UP_ALG_8_replaced([11094176](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kmaBffvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))], the MAX(4,N*2) eAxCIndex comes after x index shall be used.**

Where N is the NRCELL-nbrOfSsbPerRachOccasion.

Note: The order of prach ceAxCIndex references shall be available at OAM_REQ_RAT_1569 for UlData_PrachReceiveReq.

eCpriFlag = false [PR852424] or associated prachOccasions[i] bit is set to 0 (where i = 0..7 according to [11514296](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2oWPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) [End PR852424]:

[Before PR852424] When eCpriFlag is false, [End PR852424] 5G-L2-PS sets two ceAxCIndex choices (0, 0) and patternIds to value 0 in the UlData_PrachReceiveReq.

eCpriFlag and numCeAxCId are got from the subcell configuration in PsCell_CellSetupReq.

[PR852424] Refer to [11152306](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksfbU_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for detail about prachOccasions setting.[End PR852424]

---

#### 2.5.2.2.0-9 Handling of eCPRI fields Setting of ceAxCIndex for PUSCH/PRACH/SRS/PUCCH reception (ID: 11178941)

**2.5.2.2.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `12707974`)

Handling of eCPRI fields If actOranFDD = TRUE, the 5G-L2-PS shall set the IE numCeAxcIndex for an UL grant (PUSCH/PRACH/SRS/PUCCH):

  * 2 for ulSubcellType A2
  * 4 for ulSubcellType A4



[CB013442-D]

  * 8 for ulSubcellType A8 for PUSCH/SRS/PUCCH, and 4 for PRACH[CB008577-A] if actPrachProbing is FALSE otherwise 8 for PRACH[End CB008577-A][End CB013442-D]

#### 2.5.2.2.0-10 Handling of eCPRI fields Setting of IEs numCeAxcIndex and ceAxcIndex in UlData_RimReceiveReq (ID: 11178952)

**2.5.2.2.0-10.0-3**  (ID: `11178968`)

Handling of eCPRI fields According to 5G_UP_ALG_9328_replaced([11161420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), if RIM-RS reception is not present in the target slot (see 5G_L2_11755_replaced([11175442](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26r0rPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

only ceAxc {0, 1} are allocated for RI measurement, regardless of the subcell type, correspondingly:

IE numCeAxcIndex is set to 2.

[Before CB009363-I]IE ceAxcIndex is set to [0, 1, 0, 0].[CB009363-I]First two values of IE ceAxcIndex are set correspondingly to [0, 1]. Remaining values are set to 0.[End CB009363-I]

If RIM-RS reception is present in the slot:

IE numCeAxcIndex is set to 2.

IE ceAxcIndex shall be set for last two available indexes {n - 2, n - 1}, where n is number of RX (subcell C_n), and not set for all other indexes.

---

#### 2.5.2.2.0-11 Handling of eCPRI fields Setting of patternId (ID: 11178972)

**2.5.2.2.0-11.0-11**  (ID: `12708975`)

Handling of eCPRI fields 5G-L2-PS shall populate the patternId values for the UL channels and signals along with the ceAxCIndex choices outlined in 5G_L2_465_replaced([11178901](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27DBAPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_5161_replaced([11204321](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkDCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) as follows (in accordance with 5G_L1_IF_169_replaced([11513641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxv4_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

eCpriFlag = true:

For PRACH reception, one request includes multiple PRACH reception occasions for each subcell (determined by numPrachOccasions), one patternId is set for the pair of ceAxCIndex for each PRACH occasion. The patternId is specified within the occasions list.

In case of UCA cell scenario (5G_UP_921_replaced([11353688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucBWiPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for FR1-TDD, eCPRI, C4 subcell.

PRACH shall be fixedly configured with 4RX to ensure reception performance.

Fixed two pattern IDs of UL beams shall be used for PRACH to support fixedly 4RX receiver. (reference to 5G_UP_ALG_2212_replaced([11113055](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and the UL specific beams are provided in 5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and fixedly map to two ceAxc of PRACH (5G_L2_465_replaced([11178901](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27DBAPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for configuration).

as same to PRACH beam configuration, 4RX with same two fixed UL beams are also configured for MSG3 within PUSCH, L2 PS shall indicate beam of the MSG3 in PUSCH through numCeAxCIndex and ceAxcIndex and patternId according to 5G_L1_IF_191_replaced([11513756](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRy99_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For C4 or C8 **or C4_2** or C8_2 or C8_4 or C8_8 sub cell with beamforming, a second patternId shall be set for the pair of ceAxCIndex for each PRACH occasion. The second patternId shall be as same as first patternId.****

[CB013442-D]For A8 sub cell, 2 identical pattern ID shall be set for the 4 ceAxCIndex for each PRACH occasion[CB008577-A] if actPrachProbing = FALSE, and if actPrachProbing = TRUE 4 pattern ID shall be set. Each pattern ID is for 2 ceAxCIndex[End CB008577-A].[End CB013442-D]

When supercell mode is enabled (numOfSuperSubcells >= 2) for PRACH reception request for each subcell of supercell the patternIds are set to value of 0.

Other UL channels:

Each patternId is applicable to two consecutive ceAxCIndex. The number of patternIds selected is based this sharing of each patternId between ceAxCIndex. The total ceAxCIndex required is determined by the number of I/Q streams required in processing of the UL channel (PUSCH, PUCCH), and for Srs this shall be based on UL subcell type default antenna streams. [CB013442-D]And for FDD BF L3 Call, refer to [12704269: Beam ID for UL](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_AKvQAWB3EfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).[End CB013442-D][CB008577-A]For FDD Cell with actBeamforming = TRUE, refer to [12823081: Beam usage for UL](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_GGTJ4KpBEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).[End CB008577-A]

In case of UCA cell scenario (5G_UP_921_replaced([11353688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucBWiPvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for FR1-TDD, eCPRI, C4 subcell.

Ul channels shall be fixedly configured with 4RX to ensure reception performance.

Fixed two pattern IDs of UL beams shall be used for PUSCH/PUCCH/A-SRS to support fixedly 4RX receiver for UL channels (reference to 5G_UP_ALG_2212_replaced([11113055](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpaSI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the UL specific beams are provided via interface (5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))), and the first pattern ID is fixedly correspond to ceAxc {0, 1}, and the second pattern ID is fixedly to ceAxc {2, 3}, corresponding pattern ID configurations shall reference to 5G_L1_5G21A_1516 for eAxC allocation of UL channels and 5G_L1_IF_169_replaced([11513641](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRxv4_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for ceAxC configuration of UL channels

Especially, same two UL beams are fixedly used for Long PUCCH in C4 case, their pattern IDs are provided by CPRT via ulNumberOfBeams, instead of sectorBeamPatternId in bfSetup (see 5G_L2_IF_115_replaced([10968891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBKvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)),33004).

patternId is 0 as AiC not support beamforming

If RIM-RS reception is not present in the target slot (see 5G_L2_11755_replaced([11175442](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26r0rPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

For RI measurement, **if rdRiMonitorAllSsb = "1" (see 5G_UP_ALG_31909_replaced([11163711](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktbPc_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):**

first pattern ID is based on SSB Beam index of the currently measured beam in the iteration within RIM beam configuration algorithm (see 5G_UP_ALG_31912_replaced([11161588](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhzPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), remaining pattern IDs are set to 0.

else // rdRiMonitorAllSsb = "0": 

first pattern ID is based on SSB Beam Index derived from (_rrmRDRIMsession mod_ numberOfTransmittedSsBlocks), remaining pattern IDs are **set to 0 (see 5G_UP_ALG_9328_replaced([11161420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_31912_replaced([11161588](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhzPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).****

Else: // RIM-RS is present in the target slot

For both RI measurement and RIM-RS, pattern ID corresponding to ceAxc {n - 2, n - 1}, where n is number of RX (subcell C_n), is based on the full-sector beam from parameter PsCell_CellSetupReq/PsCell_CellReconfigurationReq.rimRsConfig.rsBeamPatternId (see 5G_L2_IF_2797_replaced([10970007](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgH0fu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_13190_replaced([11162584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_13206_replaced([11162604](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). If any other pattern IDs exist, they are set to 0.

When supercell mode is enabled (numOfSuperSubcells >= 2) the patternIds are set to value of 0.

eCpriFlag = false

In this case, the patternIds are set to default value 0.

Note: The patternId implementation can be referenced for mmWave/Analog beamforming based on 5G_UP_ALG_1909_replaced([11111524](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOE7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), and for digital beamforming for the section at 5G_UP_ALG_1939_replaced([11111782](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpQhIPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). The implementation details with respect to DlData_PatternConfig need to be considered (e.g. whether the mapping is done after collecting the channel specific beamIds before mapping to patternIds or after, while both options are possible for DlData_PatternConfig, this interface requires channel specific values).

[CB014301-C] Note1: L2-PS may receive ulNumberOfBeams via PsCell_BeamConfigUpdateReq from CP-RT ([12536044](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/TX_wLou8R9PEfCQJ5daVHVkgg)) in case of beamSet NIDD parameters online modification. [End CB014301-C]

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-1 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq (ID: 11179058)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-1.0-9**  (ID: `12722135`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq IEs sfn, slot are set to the sfn and NR-slot when the PUSCH transmission is on air

IE subcellId is set according to 5G_UP_ALG_4871_replaced([11196450](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwCepPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

IE bufferedUlConfig is set according to 5G_UP_ALG_5199_replaced([11209883](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw2W5vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Before sending lData_PuschReceiveReq for any subcell, 5G-L2-PS shall judge whether certain subcell shall be buffered according to 5G_UP_ALG_5214_replaced([11209976](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw298fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

IE tbSize_bits is set according to 5G_UP_ALG_5084_replaced([11203344](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For CG activated UEs:

IE rnti is set to the CS-RNTI of the UE if it is scheduled with HarqSlotType: cgSlot, refer 5G_L2_11008_replaced([11175697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26uQ4_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

IE rnti is set to the C-RNTI of the UE if it is scheduled with HarqSlotType: standard, refer 5G_L2_11008_replaced([11175697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26uQ4_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

For non CG activated UEs:

IE rnti is set to the C-RNTI of the UE, with HarqSlotType: standard, refer 5G_L2_11008_replaced([11175697](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26uQ4_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

IE fakeUe shall be set to false.

IE foeValid [Before CB007491-H-UPD002]and longTermCfoMetric[End CB007491-H-UPD002][PR831459]and longTermCfoMetric [End PR831459]:

IE foeValid [Before PR831459][Before CB007491-H-UPD002]and longTermCfoMetric are[CB007491-H-UPD002]is[End CB007491-H-UPD002][PR831459]and longTermCfoMetric are[End PR831459] set according to 5G_UP_ALG_3337_replaced([11151189](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksXfi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), for the Msg3 transmission.

For the other PUSCH transmissions:

Refer to 5G_L2_6947_replaced([11179618](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27HSdvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for detail.

IE longTermCfoMetricOfBeam is set according to 5G_UP_ALG_3333_replaced([11151157](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksXfhvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). When FDD Supercell feature is active (NRCELL.actSupercellSingleSSB = TRUE) for ABIL,

  * No special behaviour for Msg3 transmission

  * For the other PUSCH transmissions:




IEs foeValid and [Before CB007491-H-UPD002]longTermCfoMetric,[End CB007491-H-UPD002][PR831459]longTermCfoMetric, [End PR831459]longTermCfoMetricOfBeam are set according to 5G_UP_ALG_3324_replaced([11150688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksVDQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_9160_replaced([11150769](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksVDS_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_6911_replaced([11151021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksW4cfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_3322_replaced([11150515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksT1LvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [For non-Msg3 transmission]

When FDD Supercell feature is deactivated (NRCELL.actSupercellSingleSSB = FALSE),

L2-PS maintains legacy behaviour.

See 5G_L2_12757_replaced([11170198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26Hz-vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for relation between longTermCfoMetricOfAnt and longTermCfoMetricOfBeam.

IE eCpriSectionId is set according to 5G_UP_ALG_5163_replaced([11204341](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkDDfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for 7-2a, **set as 0 for actEcpri72e == TRUE** according to 5G_UP_ALG_25016_replaced([11204367](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkqH_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).****

IE ulRiSelectionThreshold is set according to 5G_UP_ALG_19771_replaced([11140083](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krrjEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

IE pBoost is set according to 5G_UP_ALG_19880_replaced([11119457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqKgGvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If the k2 values requested is higher than _k2max (5G_L1_5G21A_276), 5G-L2-PS shall store the associated request and delay the transmission to L1 until k2max slot before the targeted slot._

In FR2 CA case, 5G-L2-PS shall send UlData_PuschReceiveReq to 5G-L1-UL for the subcells that are allocated to the UE in the FD scheduling (see 5G_UP_ALG_5055_replaced([11201947](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwa5E_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). These messages are not sent for the subcells that are not allocated.

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-3 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting IEs of structure PuschAllocationConfig (ID: 11179127)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11179162`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq IE numOfPuschSymbols is set according to PUSCH configuration of current slot, i.e. in line with the selected SLIV value.

IE startSymbol is set according to PUSCH configuration of current slot, i.e. in line with the selected SLIV value.

IE numOfPrb:

For Msg3 transmission, IE numOfPrb shall be set to number of PRB granted by 5G_UP_ALG_4972_replaced([11199446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwNdvPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), but shall not be larger than longPucchNumPuschPrb if the long PUCCH is selected (IE pucchModeSelect in PsCell_CellSetupReq is set to longPucch).

For the other trasnmisssions it is set to number of PRBs granted by the Frequency Domain scheduler in 5G_UP_ALG_4970_replaced([11199433](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwNduvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For the UL grant sent to switch the active BWP, numOfPrb is limited as specified in under 5G_UP_ALG_4954_replaced([11199134](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwLohvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

IE startPrb:

The IE startPrb shall be set to [Before CB008917-A] [image-0][image_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_5766.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] specified in 5G_UP_ALG_4947_replaced([11198980](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwLBfvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB008917-A] RBstart + start PRB of UE active BWP, RBstart is specified in 5G_UP_ALG_4947_replaced([11198980](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwLBfvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))[END CB008917-A].

For Msg3 initial trasnmission:

The IE start PRB shall be set to [image-1][image_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_5766.002.png[/image_path][/image-1]+ start PRB of the uplink initial bandwidth part, where [image-2][image_desc]The image is entirely black.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_5766.002.png[/image_path][/image-2] shall be set to the value determined in 5G_UP_ALG_3419_replaced([11152630](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kshQifvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

For a re-transmission:

The IE start PRB is set as determined in 5G_UP_ALG_5026_replaced([11201742](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwZD4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note (only): For Msg3 retransmission, per statement above, it is expected that implementation shall make sure that the startPrb that results from 5G_UP_ALG_5026_replaced([11201742](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwZD4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (which is in fact generically covering multiple cases: msg3 initial transmission, msg3 retransmission, regular PUSCH) is selected with respect from the newly added requirement 5G_UP_ALG_5026_replaced([11201742](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwZD4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

For the UL grant sent to switch the active BWP, find further information under 5G_UP_ALG_4954_replaced([11199134](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwLohvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The first PRB allocated to the UE as determined in 5G_UP_ALG_5026_replaced([11201742](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwZD4vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-5 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting IEs of structure PuschSpatialConfig (ID: 11179191)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11179202`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq IE antPort:

The IE antPort is not used for Msg3 transmission as the numOfLayers equals to "single layer " & spatialMode equals to "single antenna" and is set to 0.

For the UL grant to switch the active BWP, the IE antPort shall be set to 0x8000 (DMRS antenna port 0).

[CB008360-A] If actUlMuMimo = true, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_9535_replaced([11147407](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksGZx_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_6275_replaced([11168724](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25-qD_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[End CB008360-A]

For the other PUSCH transmissions, refer to 5G_UP_ALG_3221_replaced([11139889](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU7fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G_UP_ALG_3216_replaced([11139853](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

IE spatialMode:

The IE spatialMode is set to "single antenna", for Msg3 transmission.

For the other PUSCH transmissions:

The IE spatialMode shall be set to "closed loop spatial multiplexing" or "single antenna" (aka "singleTx") depending of UE capability (“nrofSrsPorts" cf. 5G_L2_IF_411_replaced([10975309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeFfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). In SRS resource with srsResourceId 0 : if nrofSrsPorts =1, spatialMode is set to "single antenna" else spatialMode is set to"closed loop spatial multiplexing".

---

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-6 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting IEs of structure puschSpatialConfig for MU UE (ID: 11179206)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11179212`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq antPort in puschSpatialConfig(5G_L1_IF_194_replaced([11513774](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRy9-vvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) should be filled according to 5G_L2_6278_replaced([11168761](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_25_RF_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
