##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-7 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting IEs of structure PuschPrecodingConfig (ID: 11179217)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-7.0-2**  (ID: `11179226`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq The codebookIndex shall be set to 0

The supported values for the IE codebookIndex are [0..5] for Rank 1 reception and [0..2] for Rank 2 reception.

In case of spatialMode is "single antenna transmission" (aka "singleTx") (see 5G_L1_5G21A_190) the codebookIndex is not used.

The IE puschTransCoherence indicates the subset of the UL TPMI codebook the UE supports and, hence, limits the applicable search space for determining the ulPmiRank1 and ulPmiRank2 preferred codebook indices in PUSCH Receive Response (5G_L1_5G21A_199) and SRS Receive Response (5G_L1_5G21A_251). The value is set according to pusch-TransCoherence in PsUser_UserSetupReq message (5G_L2_IF_389_replaced([10974645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U9ayPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

IE puschTransformPrecoderFlag is missing

[5GC002396-A]

The IE fullPowerPuschPowerScalingRatio shall be set as follows:

If IE ulFullPowerTransmissionR16 (see 5G_L2_IF_430_replaced([10975648](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VCTQPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to notConfigured:

bits of IE fullPowerPuschPowerScalingRatio are set to 00 00 00 00

Else if ulFullPowerTransmissionR16 is set to fullpower:

bits of IE fullPowerPuschPowerScalingRatio are set to 00 10 10 00

[End 5GC002396-A]

[5GC002396-B]

Else if ulFullPowerTransmissionR16 is set to fullpowerMode1:

If UE is in power limit (see 5G_UP_ALG_3074_replaced([11130160](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq-_e_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

bits of IE fullPowerPuschPowerScalingRatio are set to 00 00 00 01

Else (if UE is not in power limit):

bits of IE fullPowerPuschPowerScalingRatio are set to 00 01 01 00

[End 5GC002396-B]

[5GC002396-C]

Else (if ulFullPowerTransmissionR16 is set to fullpowerMode2):

If IE ulFullPwrMode2TpmiGroupTwoPortsR16 (see 5G_L2_IF_401_replaced([10975032](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_P9Pu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to tpmi0:

bits of IE fullPowerPuschPowerScalingRatio are set to 00 10 01 00

Else (ulFullPwrMode2TpmiGroupTwoPortsR16 is set to tpmi1):

bits of IE fullPowerPuschPowerScalingRatio are set to 00 01 10 00

[End 5GC002396-C]

[5GC002396-A, 5GC002396-B, 5GC002396-C]

Note: For PUSCH power scaling ratio assignment see 5G_UP_ALG_6881_replaced([11140012](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krrjAPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End 5GC002396-A, 5GC002396-B, 5GC002396-C]

---

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-8 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting IEs of structure UlPtrsConfig (ID: 11179231)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11179237`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq IEs ulPtrsFlag, ulPtrsTimeDensity, ulPtrsFrequencyDensity, ulPtrsNumOfPorts, ulPtrsResElemOffset are set according to 5G_UP_ALG_5150_replaced([11204236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwjb_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For Ms3 transmission, [before 5GC000580-D]The IE ulPtrsFlag is set to false. [5GC000580-D] PTRS configuration shall followed 5G_UP_ALG_5150_replaced([11204236](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwjb_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End 5GC000580-D]

When a UE is in Transform Precoder Enabled state (see 5G_UP_ALG_3270_replaced([11140467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krt_UPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and UL PTRS is enabled, L1-UL is configured for PTRS as described below:

  * If UL PTRS is configured, per 5G_UP_ALG_5157_replaced([11204269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkDAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):



\- ulPtrsFlag =1 in UlData_PuschReceiveReq message

\- UL PTRS Time Density

\- ulPtrsTimeDensity =1 in UlData_PuschReceiveReq message

\- UL PTRS Sample Density

\- Set ulPtrsNumOfGroups and ulPtrsNumOfSamplesPerGroup in UlData_PuschReceiveReq message per 38.214 Table 6.2.3.2-1, where:

\- NRB0, NRB1, NRB2, NRB3, NRB4 are the sampleDensity parameters provided by C-Plane per 5G_UP_ALG_5157_replaced([11204269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkDAvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

\- NRB equals numOfScheduledPrb

  * If UL PTRS is not configured, per 5G_UP_ALG_5156_replaced([11204263](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkDAfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)):



\- Set ulPtrsFlag=0 UlData_PuschReceiveReq message

IEs ulPtrsNumOfGroups, ulPtrsNumOfSamplesPerGroup are missing

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-9 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting IEs of structure PuschHarqConfig (ID: 11179242)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-9.0-1**  (ID: `11179246`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Parameters setting

---

**2.5.2.3.2.0-9.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11179256`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq IE harqProcessIndex is set as in 5G_L2_423_replaced([11152361](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24n_KvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

IE absoluteHarqProcessIndex is set as in 5G_L2_914_replaced([11179261](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27FdQPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The IE freshHarqTrans shall be set to true for an initial HARQ transmission.

If DTX is reported on HARQ transmission with rvIndex = 0 and freshHarqTrans = TRUE, 5G-L2-PS shall set freshHarqTrans to TRUE for the next HARQ retransmission. Otherwise, 5G-L2-PS shall set freshHarqTrans to FALSE for HARQ retransmissions. Please note, DTX status is reported by L1 via the interface UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs (see 5G_L1_5G21A_200).

[CB007103-A]IE absoluteTxCount is set as in 5G_L1_8802_replaced([11403289](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e9NeNPvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[End CB007103-A]

---

**2.5.2.3.2.0-9.0-2**  (ID: `11179261`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting absoluteHarqProcessIndex

---

**2.5.2.3.2.0-9.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11179267`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq For the reception of an initial UL HARQ transmission (including RA Msg3) requested via UlData_PuschReceiveReq 5G-L2-PS shall provide an unused (free) absoluteHarqProcessIndex defined in 5G_L1_5G21A_1045. The absoluteHarqProcessIndex is associated with the transport block and shall be used to address this transport block within 5G-L1-UL for any possibly following HARQ retransmission. Earliest by freeing the UL HARQ process the absoluteHarqProcessIndex can be considered free. Note, the management of absoluteHarqProcessIndex is left to implementation. 5G-L2-PS shall ensure that the absoluteHarqProcessIndex values are assigned to HARQ processes uniquely [Before 5GC000679-C] within a subcell [End 5GC000679-C] [5GC000679-C] within an L1 instance [End 5GC000679-C].

---

**2.5.2.3.2.0-9.0-3**  (ID: `11179273`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting k2

---

**2.5.2.3.2.0-9.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11179278`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq When NRBTS.actLatencyPmCount is True, the IE k2 shall be set to [12429728: rdcgPuschPreparationTime](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3iyP0QYuEfCD_KNtuTnR7g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for Configured Grants(CG), set to K2 value for dynamic grants(DG), see 5G_L1_IF_197_replaced([11513788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRy9_fvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-10 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting numOfSlotsSinceUlGrantForInitRxPusch (ID: 12567371)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-10.0-1**  (ID: `12567372`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq When NRBTS.actLatencyPmCount is True, for the initial transmission, the IE numOfSlotsSinceUlGrantForInitRxPusch shall be set to [12429728: rdcgPuschPreparationTime](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_3iyP0QYuEfCD_KNtuTnR7g?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for Configured Grants(CG), otherwise set numOfSlotsSinceUlGrantForInitRxPusch to 0 for CG, set to K2 value for dynamic grants(DG), see 5G_L1_IF_197_replaced([11513788](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRy9_fvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-11 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting IEs of structure PuschDecoderConfig (ID: 11179283)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-11.0-2**  (ID: `12811443`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq The IE mcs is set according to 5G_UP_ALG_3071_replaced([11130097](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kq-_cfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_5101_replaced([11203496](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwfKiPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). For Msg3 transmission (5G_UP_ALG_5096_replaced([11203473](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwfKhPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or UL Grant sent to switch the active BWP, it is set to 0.

The IE mcsTable is set to 64QAM

The IE [Before CB008949-A] baseGraph, numOfCodeBlocks, codeBlockSize, numOfFillerBits, liftSize, liftSizeSetIndex, liftSizeColumnIndex [CB008949-A] baseGraph (BG), numOfCodeBlocks (C), codeBlockSize (K), numOfFillerBits (F), liftSize (Z), liftSizeSetIndex (set_index), liftSizeColumnIndex (column_index) [End CB008949-A] shall be set according to 5G_UP_ALG_6874_replaced([11192598](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvlypfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), the number of DMRS OFDM being equal to ulDmrsLen +ulDmrsAddPos. For Msg3 transmission, considering 3 DMRS OFDM Symbols.

The IE modulationOrder is set to 2 for a QPSK, 4 for a 16QAM, 6 for a 64QAM, 8 for a 256QAM. The modulation order is retrieved from table 5G_UP_IF_2251_replaced([11518398](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_tUpPCfv1Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) using the associated MCS.

The IE rvIndex is set according to 5G_UP_ALG_5077_replaced([11202379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwcuTfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))~~.~~

The IE ncb and k0divZ are computed as described in 5G_L2_418_replaced([11152113](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24mxA_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

The IE numOfLayers is set 5G_UP_ALG_3223_replaced([11139902](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krqU7_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). For Msg3 transmission or UL Grant sent to switch the active BWP, it is set to "single Layer".

For a retransmission, these IEs are set to the same values as for the corresponding first transmission.

For every to-be-scheduled UE, the following information is sent to the L1 UL using UlData_PuschReceiveReq:

  * mcs -- rrmUlUsedMcs as determined in 5G_UP_ALG_5102_replaced([11203503](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwfKifvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (original MCS _rrmDlProposedMcs is the MCS used for the calculation of the number of PRBs in 5G_UP_ALG_5010_replaced([11201008](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwTkUfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) )_

---

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-12 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting IEs of structure ECpriConfig (ID: 11179293)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-12.0-4**  (ID: `11179313`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq If actUlMuMimo = true,

5G-L2-PS shall populate fields in structure eCpriConfig in UlData_PuschReceiveReq messages (as per 5G_L1_5G21A_170) based on the receiver model UE used.

Refer to 5G_L2_6787_replaced([11179319](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27FdS_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for detail.

For analog beamforming for eCPRI RUs, L2 PS shall indicate beam of the corresponding UE (or corresponding PRACH occasion, if Msg3 transmission) through numCeAxCIndex and ceAxcIndex and patternId in UlData_PuschReceiveReq according to 5G_L1_5G21A_190 as

numCeAxCIndex number of eAxC index for D2 subcell type according to 5G_L1_5G21A_1516.

ceAxcIndex eAxC index of default data for D2 subcell type according to 5G_L1_5G21A_1516 and 5G_UP_ALG_5161_replaced([11204321](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwkDCvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

patternId map beam Id to pattern Id according to 5G_UP_ALG_1909_replaced([11111524](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOE7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

NOTE1: Linked to both 5GC000399 and 5GC000918 features to avoid creating a dependency on their mutual implementation order. And based on CP3 discussion, 5GC000399-KX will fill numCeAxCIndex, ceAxcIndex and patternId.

[Before CB010708-D]

NOTE2: numCeAxCIndex and ceAxcIndex and patternId are still filled as legacy even if L1 doesn't use it(5G_L1_IF_191_replaced([11513756](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRy99_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for [Before CB009514-L] EActEcpri72e != disabled [CB009514-L] actEcpri72e == TRUE [End CB009514-L]

[CB010708-D]

NOTE2: For 7-2e([Before CB009514-L] EActEcpri72e != disabled [CB009514-L] actEcpri72e == TRUE [End CB009514-L]), ceAxcIndex and patternId shall be set as 0, numCeAxCIndex shall be set as default value as CPRI.

[End CB010708-D]

---

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-13 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting IEs of structure ECpriConfig for MU UE (ID: 11179319)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-13.0-3**  (ID: `11179334`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq 5G-L2-PS shall populate fields in structure eCpriConfig in UlData_PuschReceiveReq messages (as per 5G_L1_5G21A_170) based on the receiver model(refer to 5G_L2_6228_replaced([11169502](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26CUbPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) UE used.

If subcell type is set to C4 in given subcell (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

|  |   
---|---|---  
| SU-IRC | MU-IRC  
numCeAxcIndex | 4 | 2  
ceAxcIndex[8] | {0,1,2,3} | {0,1}/{2,3}  
patternId[4] | {1st best beam, 2nd best beam} | {1st best beam}  
  
If subcell type is set to C8 in given subcell (5G_UP_8362_replaced([11388556](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ufKxMfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

|  |   
---|---|---  
| SU-IRC | MU-IRC  
numCeAxcIndex | 8 | 2 or 4 **[CB009363-OO] or 6**[End CB009363-OO]****  
ceAxcIndex[8] | {0,1,2,3,4,5,6,7} | For UEs with 1 beam used: {0,1}/{2,3}/{4,5}/{6,7} For UEs with 2 beams used: {0,1,2,3}/{2,3,4,5}/{4,5,6,7} **[CB009363-OO]** For UEs with 3 beams used: {0,1,2,3,4,5}/{2,3,4,5,6,7} **_*[End CB009363-OO]_** *  
patternId[4] | {1st best beam, 2nd best beam, 3rd best beam, 4th best beam} | {1st best beam}/ {1st best beam, 2nd best beam}/ **[CB009363-OO]** {1st best beam, 2nd best beam, 3rd best beam} **[End CB009363-OO]**  
  
\- When **UEs go to same MU receiver (are scheduled within same subcell), they should be assigned ceAxCIndex ranges that do not overlap. There is no rule which UEs should get which indices, however** L2-PS should store this assignment for processing cfo(5G_L2_6916_replaced([11170152](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26Hz8PvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).****

\- When not all available storage is filled in ceAxcIndex **or** patternId arrays, remaining elements **should be set as 0.** ****

\- IF isUsingTaperedBeam && UE is MU UE

patternId should be the tapered beam pattern Id

Else

patternId should be the non-tapered beam pattern Id

isUsingTaperedBeam is calculated and stored according to 5G_L2_8061_replaced([11169121](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26BtUfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-14 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq setting IEs of structure ECpriConfig for FDD BF (ID: 12708997)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-14.0-1**  (ID: `12708993`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq If actBeamformingFdd (see [10967202: PsCell_CellSetupReq Message Content](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))[CB008577-A] or otherwise actBeamforming = TRUE[End CB008577-A], SU receiver for subcell A8, eECpriConfig shall be filled as bellow :

|   
---|---  
| SU-IRC  
numCeAxcIndex | 8  
ceAxcIndex[8] | {0,1,2,3,4,5,6,7}  
patternId[4] | 4 beams as in [12704269: Beam ID for UL](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_AKvQAWB3EfCLrcnPCspVyQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)[CB008577-A] if actBeamformingFdd = TRUE or otherwise actBeamforming = TRUE as in [12823081: Beam usage for UL](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_GGTJ4KpBEfCrANRYxAlR5A?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)[End CB008577-A]

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-15 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting IEs of structure PuschUciConfig (ID: 11179340)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-15.0-3**  (ID: `11179355`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq If L2-PS doesn’t expect any CSI report multiplexed in PUSCH, i.e. there is no PUCCH with periodic CSI report and overlapping PUSCH and if there is no aperiodic CSI requested to be multiplexed with PUSCH data , then IE numOfUciCsiPart1Bits, IE numOfUciCsiPart1Symbols, IE maxNumOfUciCsiPart2Symbols and IE numOfCsiReports shall be set to 0. Accordingly, the IEs per CSI report, IE riStartPos, IE riUsageMap, IE numOfUciCsiPart2BitsRi1, IE numOfUciCsiPart2BitsRi2, IE numOfUciCsiPart2BitsRi3, IE numOfUciCsiPart2BitsRi4 shall be set to 0 and IE csiPart1Only can be set to any value.

If L2-PS expects a (single) periodic CSI report multiplexed in PUSCH, then

IE numOfUciCsiPart1Bits is set to the number of expected CSI bits calculated in 5G_UP_ALG_3609_replaced([11159986](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktNNBvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB007827-G] where in case of CSI report multiplexing the aggregated number of bits of both reports is to be considered, see also 5G_UP_ALG_3638_replaced([11160479](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktObIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CB007827-G].

IE numOfUciCsiPart1Symbols is set as calculated in 5G_UP_ALG_3661_replaced([11160631](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktPCPvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

In addition, a single CSI report is added with IE csiPart1Only set to true (i.e. no CSI part 2). Accordingly, the following IEs are ignored by L1 and can be set to any value: maxNumOfUciCsiPart2BitsPlusCrc, maxNumOfUciCsiPart2Symbols, csiPart2Coderate, riStartPos, riUsageMap, numOfUciCsiPart2BitsRi#i with 1<=i<=4.

IE numOfUciAckBits shall be set to the expected number of A/N bits multiplexed in PUSCH.

IE numOfUciAckSymbols and IE numOfUciAckSymbols1bit shall be set as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_5143_replaced([11204128](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwjb8PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note, the UCI (e.g. A/N bits) which was multiplexed in the initial PUSCH transmission is not retransmitted but instead new UCI might be multiplexed in it!

IE uciOnly is set as in 5G_L2_747_replaced([11172332](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26VPV_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If aperiodic CSI was requested from the UE, according to 5G_UP_ALG_3506_replaced([11159352](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktI7mPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), L2-PS shall request the reception of the aperiodic CSI report(s) multiplexed with PUSCH data from L1-UL by filling the IEs numOfUciCsiPart1Bits, numOfUciCsiPart1Symbols, numOfUciAckBits, numOfUciAckSymbols, uciOnly, maxNumOfUciCsiPart2Symbols, [Before CB008131-A] csiPart2Coderate, [End CB008131-A] numOfCsiReports, riStartPos, riUsageMap, csiPart1Only, numOfUciCsiPart2BitsRi#i with 1<=i<=4 according to their values computed with 5G_L2_747_replaced([11172332](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26VPV_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

maxNumOfUciCsiPart2BitsPlusCrcUpTo11Bits and maxNumOfUciCsiPart2BitsPlusCrcMoreThan11Bits are calculated as in 5G_L2_754_replaced([11172372](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26V2YfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). to be clarified: 5G_L2_747_replaced([11172332](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26VPV_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_3660_replaced([11160619](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktPCPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) refer to a 'maxNumOfUciCsiPart2BitsPlusCrc'.

IEs numOfRiBits, numOfWidebandCsiPart2BitsRi0, numOfWidebandCsiPart2BitsRi1, numOfWidebandCsiPart2BitsRi2, numOfWidebandCsiPart2BitsRi3 are set as in 5G_L2_747_replaced([11172332](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26VPV_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

For FDD + TDD(FR1) CA UEs, L2-PS will include the details of HARQ-ACK bit for P(S)Cell and Scell in l2CtxtAnMgt of PuschUciConfig according to 5G_L1_5G21A_198 so UL L1 will return back in the response to help to parse the HARQ-ACK bits for PCell and Scell. Note: The purpose of the structure is to decrease the processing time in L2-PS so improving the delay budget for Scell HARQ-ACK processing, the details will be up to implementation.

Note, there is no UCI on a PUSCH containing RA Msg3, i.e. no HARQ A/N and no CSI report. Accordingly L2-PS shall set the related IEs to what is specified in 5G_L1_5G21A_190.

---

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-17 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting IEs of structure eCpriFcpSectionConfig (ID: 11179370)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-17.0-1**  (ID: `11179374`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq IE population

---

**2.5.2.3.2.0-17.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12639737`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq eCpriFcpSectionConfig(5G_L1_IF_14853_replaced([11513816](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRy-AfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is a new IE introduced by CB008360-B. And IEs in this structure should be populated as follows **[Before CNI-137616-B]according to rdUlMuReceiverBeamUsedOverlappingPRB**[End CNI-137616-B]based on 5G_L2_8321_replaced([11169541](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26C7dPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).****

An example for eCpriFcpSectionConfig **[Before CNI-137616-B]when** rdUlMuReceiverBeamUsedOverlappingPRB = true****[End CNI-137616-B]can be found in 5G_L2_8332_replaced([11179542](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27GrafvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).****

**2.5.2.3.2.0-17.0-2**  (ID: `11179386`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq fcpStartPrbc

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq fcpAddSectionEnable

---

**2.5.2.3.2.0-17.0-4.0-3**  (ID: `12639649`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq **[Before CNI-137616-B]If rdUlMuReceiverBeamUsedOverlappingPRB = true && **[End CNI-137616-B]PRB of UE is the smaller one in the subcell **& & Pusch is 4Rx(numOfRxPusch=4, see 5G_L2_16925_replaced([11141685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23qV0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**,****

fcpAddSectionEnable shall be set as TRUE.

Else,

fcpAddSectionEnable shall be set as FALSE.

If fcpAddSectionEnable = TURE, fcpAddSectionId, fcpAddStartPrbc, fcpAddNumPrbc, fcpAddPatternId shall be set for section contains the PRB diff between 2 UEs in the same subcell.

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-18 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting of the IE pairedUe (obsoleted) (ID: 11179570)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-18.0-1**  (ID: `11179575`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq If actUlMuMimo = true, 5G-L2-PS shall populate pairedUe in UlData_PuschReceiveReq messages according to 5G_L2_7035_replaced([11179582](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27GrbfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-19 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting of the IE pairedUe (ID: 11179582)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-19.0-3**  (ID: `11179599`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq L2RT shall decide the subcell and receiver model of UE based on 5G_L2_6228_replaced([11169502](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26CUbPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If only one UE is scheduled in the subcell, pairedUe should be set as 0 as default.

Otherwise pairedUe should be filled as follows:

 For [Before CB010708-C] C8 subcell (see 5G_UP_ALG_8267_replaced([11145665](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksBhQfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) [CB010708-C] Pusch is 8Rx or 16Rx(numOfRxPusch=8 or 16, see 5G_L2_16925_replaced([11141685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23qV0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB010708-C] rnti of root UE of given virtual UE should be used (for non root UEs as well as for root UE)

 Rnti of other UE in the same subcell should be used otherwise.

Examples:

For C4 subcell configuration if UE(i) goes to MU-receiver with UE(j), then the rnti of UE(j) should be filled in the pairedUe of UE(i) and pairedUe of UE(j) should be filled with rnti of UE(i).

---

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-20 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting of the IE Subcell (ID: 11179604)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-20.0-1**  (ID: `11179609`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq L2RT shall decide the subcell of UE based on 5G_L2_6228_replaced([11169502](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26CUbPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Then the UE will be filled to the corresponding subcell.

---

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-21 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting of the IE longTermCfoMetric and longTermCfoMetricOfBeam (ID: 11179614)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-21.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11179641`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Dependent on subcell configuration L2-PS shall fill long term carrier frequency offset metric data in UlData_PuschReceiveReq (see 5G_L1_IF_191_replaced([11513756](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRy99_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) according to following procedure:

IF SU-IRC receiver is used for UE

IF [Before CB010708-C] C4 subcell type is configured [CB010708-C] Pusch is 4Rx(numOfRxPusch=4, see 5G_L2_16925_replaced([11141685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23qV0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB010708-C] 

LT CFO metric data shall be filled according to 5G_L2_14383_replaced([11179647](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27HSfPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

IF [Before CB010708-C] C8 subcell type is configured [CB010708-C] Pusch is 8Rx(numOfRxPusch=8, see 5G_L2_16925_replaced([11141685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23qV0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB010708-C]

LT CFO metric data shall be filled according to 5G_L2_14384_replaced([11179669](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27HSgPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB010708-C] IF Pusch is 16Rx(numOfRxPusch=16, see 5G_L2_16925_replaced([11141685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23qV0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

LT CFO metric data shall be filled according to 5G_L2_17344_replaced([11179688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27H5gvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB010708-C]

IF MU-IRC receiver is used for UE

IF [Before CB010708-C] C4 subcell type is configured [CB010708-C] Pusch is 4Rx(numOfRxPusch=4, see 5G_L2_16925_replaced([11141685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23qV0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB010708-C] and rdMUIRCCfo is set to true

LT CFO metric data shall be filled according to 5G_L2_14385_replaced([11179702](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27H5hfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

IF [Before CB010708-C] C4 subcell type is configured [CB010708-C] Pusch is 4Rx(numOfRxPusch=4, see 5G_L2_16925_replaced([11141685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23qV0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB010708-C] and rdMUIRCCfo is set to false

LT CFO metric data shall be filled according to 5G_L2_14386_replaced([11179722](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27H5ifvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

IF [Before CB010708-C] C8 subcell type is configured [CB010708-C] Pusch is 8Rx(numOfRxPusch=8, see 5G_L2_16925_replaced([11141685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23qV0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB010708-C] and rdMUIRCCfo is set to true

LT CFO metric data shall be filled according to 5G_L2_14387_replaced([11179743](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27H5jfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

IF [Before CB010708-C] C8 subcell type is configured [CB010708-C] Pusch is 8Rx(numOfRxPusch=8, see 5G_L2_16925_replaced([11141685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23qV0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB010708-C] and rdMUIRCCfo is set to false

LT CFO metric data shall be filled according to 5G_L2_14388_replaced([11179764](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27IgkfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB010708-C] IF Pusch is 16Rx(numOfRxPusch=16, see 5G_L2_16925_replaced([11141685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23qV0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

LT CFO metric data shall be filled according to 5G_L2_17350_replaced([11179785](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27IglfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [End CB010708-C]

**2.5.2.3.2.0-21.0-2**  (ID: `12697810`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq UE level LT CFO

---

**2.5.2.3.2.0-21.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `12697811`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq For eCPRI7-2e (actEcpri72e=True)

For UE level CFO longTermCfoMetric shall be calculated as below.

longTermCfoMetric = sum of each longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[k]

longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[k] is LT CFO corresponds to beam k used by UE.

That is,   
longTermCfoMetric Real part = sum (Real part from each of those LT Beams contributes)  
longTermCfoMetric Imm part = sum (Real part from each of those LT Beams contributes)

For eCPRi 7-2a (actEcpri72e=False)

For UE level CFO longTermCfoMetric ,

longTermCfoMetric = 0+j0 as default value.

---

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-22 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting of the IE eCpriSectionId for MU UE (ID: 11179800)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-22.0-1**  (ID: `11179807`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq The lowest 12 bits of eCpriSectionId is used as DD XXXXX YYYYY, where

 DD – is always set to ‘00b’

 XXXXX – number of regions

 YYYYY – starting region ID

Number of regions of UE should always be 1. And it could be set as 0 or 1.

Starting region ID for the UE in the same virtual UE should be same.

[CB008360-B]

For the UE paired with UE group, number of regions should be greater than 1.

For example, UE0 paired with a UE group consisting of UE1, UE2 and UE3.

Number of regions of UE0 should be 3. Starting region ID of UE0 should be 0.

Number of regions of UE1/UE2/UE3 should be 1. Starting region ID of UE1/UE2/UE3 should be 0/1/2.

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating a grid-like structure with labels and colored cells. The grid is divided into rows labeled "region0", "region1", and "region2" on the left side. The columns are divided into two main sections, "subcell0" and "subcell1", each further subdivided into columns labeled "еанс0", "еанс1", "еанс2", and "еанс3". Within the grid, there are colored rectangular cells representing different User Equipments (UEs) and their associated beams. \- **Region0, Subcell0, еанс0** : This cell is colored yellow. \- **Region0, Subcell1, еанс0** : This cell is colored red and labeled "UE1 (beam 7&beam 8)". \- **Region1, Subcell0, еанс0 & еанс1**: This area is colored yellow and labeled "UE0 (beam 1&beam 2)". It spans across two sub-column labels within subcell0. \- **Region1, Subcell1, еанс0 & еанс1**: This cell is colored green and labeled "UE2 (beam 5&beam 6)". It spans across two sub-column labels within subcell1. \- **Region2, Subcell0, еанс0 & еанс1**: This area is colored yellow and spans across two sub-column labels within subcell0. \- **Region2, Subcell1, еанс0 & еанс1**: This cell is colored blue and labeled "UE3 (beam 3&beam 4)". It spans across two sub-column labels within subcell1. The text in the image is: subcell0 еанс0 еанс1 еанс2 еанс3 subcell1 еанс0 еакс1 еакс2 еано3 region0 UE1 (beam 7&beam 8) region1 UE0 (beam 1&beam 2) UE2 (beam 5&beam 6) region2 UE3 (beam 3&beam 4)[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_5871.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

Then eCpriSectionId for these UEs should be filled as following.

|   
---|---  
| eCpriSectionId  
UE0 | 00 00011 00000(96)  
UE1 | 00 00001 00000(32)  
UE2 | 00 00001 00001(33)  
UE3 | 00 00001 00010(34)  
  
[End CB008360-B]

Note: For the number of regions, value 0 and 1 should have the same meaning for one section with one region from L1’s point of view.

---

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-23 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting of the IE numOfDmrsCdmGroupWithoutData for MU UE (ID: 11179815)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-23.0-1**  (ID: `11179819`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq MU UE doesn't support DMRS multiplexing with PUSCH, that is MU UE support CDM group without data = 2 only, including initial trasnmission and re-transmission.

\- initTx UE, should set numOfDmrsCdmGroupWithoutData = 2 finally to replace CB006062 logic.

\- reTx UE, can't be paired if CDM group without data = 1 in initial trasnmission.

CP2 reference: 5G_UP_ALG_3098_replaced([11137832](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krbravvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

##### 2.5.2.3.2.0-24 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq Setting of the IE suSplitpanelMode for 7-2a (ID: 12978516)

**2.5.2.3.2.0-24.0-1**  (ID: `12978518`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReq For 7-2a FDD beamforming SU-MIMO, according to [12771852: FDD: four beams for 8RX receiver](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI__UhkgYlZEfCrqOdGJPoCRA?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) and [12884359: eCpriConfig](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_PgRfkLU6EfCQT7hYUxERAg?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), if PUSCH/SU-MIMO SRS is received via full panel beam beam set#4 or the refine beam of PRACH probing beam, the suSplitpanelMode shall be 0 as case1:

|   
---|---  
case1 |   
patternId | suSplitpanelMode  
patternId[0] = beamset4PatternId[4] | suSplitpanelMode[0] = 0  
patternId[1] = beamset4PatternId[5] | suSplitpanelMode[1] = 0  
patternId[2] = beamset4PatternId[6] | suSplitpanelMode[2] = 0  
patternId[3] = beamset4PatternId[7] | suSplitpanelMode[3] = 0  
  
If PUSCH is received via 4 split beam of one UL PMI beam as per [11112829: PatternIDs for PMI beams based on 8 ports CSI-RS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZrEfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) and [11112950: PatternIDs for PMI beams based on 32 ports CSI-RS](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpZrE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), the suSplitpanelMode shall be 9,10,11,12 for 1x4 split according to [11354596: Split panel beamforming in UL](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ucJSWfvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) and as case2.

|   
---|---  
case2 |   
patternId | suSplitpanelMode  
patternId[0] = selected UL PMI beam | suSplitpanelMode[0] = 9  
patternId[1] = patterId[0] | suSplitpanelMode[1] = 10  
patternId[2] = patterId[0] | suSplitpanelMode[2] = 11  
patternId[3] = patterId[0] | suSplitpanelMode[3] = 12  
  
Note: For SU-MIMO SRS the suSplitpanelMode is array[8] according to[11514390: srsSuMimo structure](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), for A8 UL subcell, only first 4 element of the array[8] shall be used.

---

#### 2.5.2.3.3 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru

##### 2.5.2.3.3.0-1 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru (ID: 11179832)

**2.5.2.3.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11179836`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru All IE setting are from UlData_PuschReceiveReq, it is sent when UL Scheduler finish FD scheduling.

---

##### 2.5.2.3.3.0-2 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru Setting of the IE patternId (ID: 11179842)

**2.5.2.3.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11179854`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru [CB010708-G] For SU UEs with rdUlSplitPanelModeFor16RX (5G_UP_ALG_29390_replaced([11114144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to 0(none) or Mu UEs:[End CB010708-G]

patternId is a dynamic array, only fills patternId of real used beams.

Number of beams to be used refer to 5G_UP_ALG_1880_replaced([11111411](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd1PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SSB/refine beam and 5G_UP_ALG_2135_replaced([11154028](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqacvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for oDFT beam.

[CB010708-G]

For SU UEs with rdUlSplitPanelModeFor16RX (5G_UP_ALG_29390_replaced([11114144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to 1(hybrid split mode) or 2(UD split mode):

For full panel beams, fill its patternId.

For subpanel beams, fill the patternId of full panel beam which split into these subpanel beams, see examples in 5G_L2_20445_replaced([11179997](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27JutvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[End CB010708-G]

[CB010708-I]

If fake UE is scheduled as 5G_L2_10790_replaced([11152474](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24omPfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), patternId shall be set as 5G_UP_ALG_17489_replaced([11215719](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxU4CvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

If scheduling for RIM RS detection is triggered in current slot(5G_UP_ALG_13070_replaced([11117417](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp_g9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_13188_replaced([11162108](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktW-D_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_15475_replaced([11162234](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlE_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

and if UE's allocated PRB location is overlaping with RIM-RS PRB(5G_UP_ALG_13076_replaced([11117993](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqAIB_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_13190_replaced([11162584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktXlF_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

and if one of UE's beam is corresponding to streamIndex {n-2, n-1}, where n is numberOfRxBeamforming(5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

this beam's patternId shall be replaced as rimRsBeamPatternId (5G_L2_IF_2797_replaced([10970007](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgH0fu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

[End CB010708-I]

---

##### 2.5.2.3.3.0-3 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru Setting of the IEs for muMiMO case (ID: 11179860)

**2.5.2.3.3.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `11179910`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru antPort: bitmap indicating used PUSCH DMRS antenna port number(s).

numOfPrbExtra: Number of unscheduled PRBs for each paired UE in vUE.

startAntIndex: Indicate the first spatial stream of each paired UE in vUE.

patternId: Real used beams in current slot as 5G_UP_ALG_26054_replaced([11149038](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksL5WvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note:

  1. If numOfPrb is limited by ATB(5G_UP_ALG_17299_replaced([11132066](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krEfCfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) or slow instantaneous throughput pooling(5G_UP_ALG_29119_replaced([11215165](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxR0tvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), numOfPrbExtra shall be updated accordingly.

  2. If one or more UEs in a vUE is/are droppred due to FD skipping(see 5G_L2_1858), the rest UE(s) shall re-allocate beams, numOfPrb and numOfPrbExtra shall be set as real used value.

  3. The sequence of antPort and startAntIndex may not mapped.

##### 2.5.2.3.3.0-4 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru Setting of the IE ueReceiverSize (ID: 11179917)

**2.5.2.3.3.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11179927`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru For SU UE, ueReceiverSize shall be set as below.

|  |  |  |   
---|---|---|---|---  
numberOfRxBeamforming | rdSuUeReceiverSize | isDftValid | numberOfSSB | ueReceiverSize  
8Rx | 8 | Yes / No | 1 / 2 | 8  
16Rx | 8 | Yes / No | 1 / 2 | 8  
16Rx | 16 | Yes | N/A | 16  
16Rx | 16 | No | 1 | 8  
16Rx | 16 | No | 2 | 16  
  
[CB010708-I]For MU UE,ueReceiverSize always set as 16.[End CB010708-I]

Note:

\- 4 is reserved for 4Rx.

\- 0 is invalid value.

---

##### 2.5.2.3.3.0-5 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru Setting of the IE longTermCfoMetric and longTermCfoMetricOfBeam (ID: 11179934)

**2.5.2.3.3.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11179939`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru Overview

---

**2.5.2.3.3.0-5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11179943`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru longTermCfoMetricOfBeam is a dynamic array, only fills longTermCfoMetricOfBeam related to the real used beams.

Relation between longTermCfoMetricOfAnt and longTermCfoMetricOfBeam refer to 5G_L2_12757.

Number of beams to be used refer to 5G_UP_ALG_1880_replaced([11111411](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpNd1PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SSB/refine beam and 5G_UP_ALG_2135_replaced([11154028](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqacvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for oDFT beam.

---

**2.5.2.3.3.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11179949`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru LongTerm CFO Metric for PUSCH SU-IRC Receiver

---

**2.5.2.3.3.0-5.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11179961`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru For SU-IRC receiver, [Before CB007491-H-UPD002]longTermCfoMetric and [End CB007491-H-UPD002]longTermCfoMetricOfBeam shall fill as below.

[Before CB007491-H-UPD002]longTermCfoMetric = nextLongTermCfoMetricOfAnt[i,j,m][End CB007491-H-UPD002]

[PR831459]longTermCfoMetric = longTermCfoMetric as [12697810: UE level LT CFO](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_oq7yElxiEfCPFofqMEsORA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) [End PR831459]

If rdBeamSpecificCfoEnabled(5G_L2_1366) is true:

longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[k] = nextLongTermCfoMetricOfAnt[i,j,n]

If rdBeamSpecificCfoEnabled(5G_L2_1366) is flase:

**_*[CB010708-G]_** *

If rdUlSplitPanelModeFor16RX (5G_UP_ALG_29390_replaced([11114144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to 1(hybrid split mode) and DFT beam is valid,

longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[x] = longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[i,j, _1st best beam index] , x = 0, 2~7_

longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[1] = longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[i,j, _2nd best beam index]_

Else If rdUlSplitPanelModeFor16RX (5G_UP_ALG_29390_replaced([11114144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to 2(UD split mode) and DFT beam is valid,

longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[a] = longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[i,j, _1st best beam index] , a = 0, 1_

longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[b] = longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[i,j, 2nd _best beam index] , b = 2, 3_

longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[c] = longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[i,j, 3rd _best beam index] , c = 4, 5_

longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[d] = longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[i,j, 4th _best beam index] , d = 6, 7_

**Else rdUlSplitPanelModeFor16RX (5G_UP_ALG_29390_replaced([11114144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to **0(none),****

**_*[End CB010708-G]_** *

longTermCfoMetricOfBeam [k] = nextLongTermCfoMetricOfAnt[i,j,m]

where,

\- nextLongTermCfoMetricOfAnt[i,j,m] is corresponds to first best beam.

\- nextLongTermCfoMetricOfAnt[i,j,n] is corresponds to beam k.

\- k is the related to real used beams, number of beams to be used for paired UEs refer to 5G_UP_ALG_2031_replaced([11112294](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpUyl_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for SSB/refine beam and 5G_UP_ALG_2135_replaced([11154028](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksqacvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for oDFT beam.

\- max number of used beams extend to 8 for 16 Rx Receiver.

---

**2.5.2.3.3.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `11179969`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru LongTerm CFO Metric for PUSCH MU-IRC Receiver

---

**2.5.2.3.3.0-5.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `13359199`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru For MU-IRC receiver, longTermCfoMetric and longTermCfoMetricOfBeam shall fill as below.

If rdMUIRCCfo(5G_L2_6392) is true:

longTermCfoMetric = longTermCfoMetric as [12697810: UE level LT CFO](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_oq7yElxiEfCPFofqMEsORA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[k] = nextLongTermCfoMetric

If rdMUIRCCfo(5G_L2_6392) is false:

longTermCfoMetric = longTermCfoMetric as [12697810: UE level LT CFO](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_oq7yElxiEfCPFofqMEsORA?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[k] = nextLongTermCfoMetricOfAnt[i,j,n]

[PR868318]If nextLongTermCfoMetricOfAnt[i,j,n] is invalid longTermCfoMetric shall be used. [End PR868318]

where ,

\- nextLongTermCfoMetric corresponds to rrmAvgCfo[i,j,0] in 5G_UP_ALG_6911_replaced([11151021](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksW4cfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), refer to 5G_UP_ALG_3324_replaced([11150688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksVDQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for rrmAvgCfo calculation.

\- nextLongTermCfoMetricOfAnt[i,j,m] is corresponds to first best beam.

\- nextLongTermCfoMetricOfAnt[i,j,n] is corresponds to beam k.

\- k is the related to real used beams, number of beams to be used for paired UEs refer to 5G_UP_ALG_20045_replaced([11148991](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksL5UfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

##### 2.5.2.3.3.0-6 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru Setting of the IE pairedUe (ID: 11179987)

**2.5.2.3.3.0-6.0-1**  (ID: `11179992`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru For normal constructed vUE(5G_L2_6223), refer to 5G_L2_7035.

For enhance constructed vUE(5G_L2_20417), pairedUe of all UEs in vUE shall be set as the rnti of root UE.

For beam group based vUE(5G_L2_20419), pairedUe of all UEs in vUE shall be set as the rnti of first UE of first beamGroup.

---

##### 2.5.2.3.3.0-7 Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru Setting of the IE suSplitpanelMode (ID: 11179997)

**2.5.2.3.3.0-7.0-1**  (ID: `11180009`)

Transmission of UlData_PuschReceiveReqL1Ru For SU UEs with rdUlSplitPanelModeFor16RX (5G_UP_ALG_29390_replaced([11114144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to 0(none) or Mu UEs:

suSplitpanelMode shall be set to 0.

For SU UEs with rdUlSplitPanelModeFor16RX (5G_UP_ALG_29390_replaced([11114144](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to 1(hybrid split mode):

Assume 5 best beams(a, b, c, d ,e) are selected as 5G_UP_ALG_20247_replaced([11154965](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksuE2_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) or 5G_UP_ALG_20257_replaced([11155127](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksur5PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

suSplitpanelMode shall be set as following base on 5G_UP_ALG_29246_replaced([11155345](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksvS8vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_29283_replaced([11155383](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksvS9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L1_16910_replaced([11412389](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_e96oxvvvEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Otherwise, fakeUe shall be set as false.

#### 2.5.2.3.4 Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU

##### 2.5.2.3.4.0-1 Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU Ignoring the message for the Fake UE for NR UL Received Total Wideband Power PM counters (ID: 11180040)

**2.5.2.3.4.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11180047`)

Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU If the rnti IE from UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU (see 5G_L1_IF_209_replaced([11513897](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlD_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set with the value specified in 5G_L2_10793, 5G-L2-PS shall stop further processing of UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU.

Rationale: The fake UE shall be scheduled only in order to collect thermal noise and interference measurements for NR UL Received Total Wideband Power PM counters.

---

##### 2.5.2.3.4.0-2 Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU Evaluation of harqProcessIndex, absoluteHarqProcessIndex (ID: 11180051)

**2.5.2.3.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11180058`)

Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU 5G-L2-PS shall use the harqProcessIndex & absoluteHarqProcessIndex IE from UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU to identify the corresponding HARQ Process.

---

##### 2.5.2.3.4.0-3 Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU Evaluation of crc, dtx (ID: 11180061)

**2.5.2.3.4.0-3.0-5**  (ID: `11180089`)

Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU At the reception of the HARQ Feedback in UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU for a given UE, subcell and HARQ process:

If crc = OK:

 HARQ process can be freed, absoluteHarqProcessIndex can be freed only after the reception of the matching LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd,

 5G-L2-PS shall update successful transmissions counter as described in 5G_L2_8135.

If crc = NOK or dtx = DTX [CB008124-B] and rrmBufferedDataUlTotal_bytes > 0 [End CB008124-B] :

If the maximum number of HARQ transmissions (maxHarqMsg3Tx or maxUlHarqTxNum as described in 5G_UP_ALG_12741_replaced([11203324](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) has been reached (HARQ failure):

  * The retransmission scheduling of the related transport block shall be stopped.
  * the HARQ process is freed, the dlHarqBufferIndex is freed.
  * 5G-L2-PS shall update failed transmissions counter as described in 5G_L2_8129.



Else if the conditions for stopping retransmissions in 5G_UP_ALG_5082_replaced([11203301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejdPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) are met:

  * The retransmission scheduling of the related transport block shall be stopped.
  * the HARQ process is freed, the dlHarqBufferIndex is freed.



Else:

  * L2-PS shall consider the UE as candidate to retransmit the data of that HARQ process.



[CB008124-B]

If dtx = DTX and rrmBufferedDataUlTotal_bytes = 0 (considered as "normal" DTX, or "skipped DTX", meaning the UE has nothing to transmit):

  * no retransmission is performed
  * HARQ process can be freed, absoluteHarqProcessIndex can be freed



[End CB008124-B]

Note that there is no UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU and LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd in case of PUSCH in UCI only mode.

Regarding any DTX of PUSCH mentioned in this requirement: response is not applicable if DTX determined

  * for a skippable Proactive grant

  * for a fake SR (SR indication received from L5-HI) or TA grant or extra UL grant before zero BSR is received at l2-ps and UE is configured for skippable grants (5G_UP_ALG_4839_replaced([11195286](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kv7J1fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))




CP2 reference: 5G_UP_ALG_5082_replaced([11203301](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejdPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

##### 2.5.2.3.4.0-4 Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU Evaluation of HARQ Feedback (ID: 11180095)

**2.5.2.3.4.0-4.0-2**  (ID: `11180106`)

Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU The PUSCH HARQ Feedback contained in UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU shall be stored by 5G-L2-PS to be used by the Link Adaptation.

If UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU provides CRC check result on received RACH Msg3 5G-L2-PS UL scheduler shall inform DL scheduler to follow handling described in 5G_UP_ALG_3433_replaced([11152848](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksiepvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) (and 5G_UP_ALG_17990_replaced([11153010](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksjswvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). [CNI-81991] Furthermore, L2-PS shall handle sendRachMsg4WithOutHIMessage timer and RA Msg4 scheduling as specified in 5G_UP_ALG_17990_replaced([11153010](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksjswvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [End CNI-81991]

---

##### 2.5.2.3.4.0-5 Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU Evaluation of transmissions number (ID: 11180111)

**2.5.2.3.4.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11180116`)

Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU At the reception of the HARQ Feedback in UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqU for a given UE, subcell and HARQ process:

If HARQ feedback is related to initial transmission:

 5G-L2-PS shall update initial transmissions counter as described in 5G_L2_8401.

Else:

 5G-L2-PS shall update retransmissions counter as described in 5G_L2_8403.

---

##### 2.5.2.3.5.0-1 Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD Ignoring the message for the Fake UE for NR UL Received Total Wideband Power PM counters (ID: 11180129)

**2.5.2.3.5.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11180134`)

Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD If the rnti IE from UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD (see 5G_L1_IF_210_replaced([11513919](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MEPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set with the value specified in 5G_L2_10793, 5G-L2-PS shall stop further processing of UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD.

Rationale: The fake UE shall be scheduled only in order to collect thermal noise and interference measurements for NR UL Received Total Wideband Power PM counters.

---

##### 2.5.2.3.5.0-2 Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD (ID: 11180141)

**2.5.2.3.5.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11180146`)

Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD 5G-L2-PS shall process UlData_PuschReceiveRespHarqD (see 5G_L1_IF_210_replaced([11513919](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MEPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as specified in 5G_L2_291.

#### 2.5.2.3.6 Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs

##### 2.5.2.3.6.0-1 Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs Evaluation of fakeUE (ID: 11180157)

**2.5.2.3.6.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12747739`)

Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs If the fakeUe IE from UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs (see 5G_L1_IF_200_replaced([11513831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is set to true, 5G-L2-PS shall:

  1. [CNI-136895-A]If rdEnableFakeUeLogIntoTtiTrace (see [12731647](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_BlW2VnNvEfCRE7eh4Ndkrw)) is set to TRUE then [End CNI-136895-A] add a TTI Trace entry for ulPuschReceiveRespPsData event (see 5G_L2_6586) and fill only the following IEs: EventHeader, fakeUE, linRssiOfAnt and linNoiseOfAnt.
  2. Evaluate NR UL Received Total Wideband Power measurement results, as specified in 5G_L2_10818.
  3. Evaluate UL scheduler Power Measurements, as specified in 5G_UP_ALG_5284_replaced([11215657](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxU4AfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) - only if for the given subcell eCpriFlag (see 5G_L2_IF_77_replaced([10968024](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UVvvfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) was set to false in PsCell_CellSetupReq (see 5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) event.
  4. [CNI-140840] Monitor the validity of measurements as specified in [12747754](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Mbx0oX9UEfCiUemk-K-C4g)[End CNI-140840]
  5. Stop further processing of UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs.



**Rationale: The fake UE shall be scheduled only in order to collect:**

  * thermal noise and interference measurements for NR UL Received Total Wideband Power PM counters and

  * UL scheduler Power Measurements when the PUSCH Request in unallocated Slots (see 5G_UP_ALG_5282_replaced([11215633](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxUQ_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) was superceded by fake UE scheduling (see 5G_L2_10788)

  * Unscheduled PUSCH PRBs for UL Received Interference Power (RIP) - [11194280](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28yGZ_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) .

---

##### 2.5.2.3.6.0-2 Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs Evaluation of Power Measurement Results (ID: 11180168)

**2.5.2.3.6.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `11180179`)

Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs The PUSCH power measurements contained in the message shall be stored by 5G-L2-PS for next use.

In case that at least 1 one UE was scheduled via UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs the PM Counter handling related to class 'NR Uplink Signal Quality Level' shall be performed.

[CB010708-I]

UL power measurements(5G_UP_ALG_5284_replaced([11215657](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxU4AfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for remote RU-Diagnostics(5G_UP_ALG_5275_replaced([11215584](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxUQ9PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), that is AvgRtwpOfAnt[], AvgRssiOfAnt[] and AvgSinrOfAnt[] in message PsCell_UlTestMeasurementInd (5G_L2_IF_361_replaced([10972998](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UybpPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) shall be extended to 16RX.

[End CB010708-I]

---

##### 2.5.2.3.6.0-3 Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs Evaluation of NR UL Received Interference Power measurement results (ID: 11180186)

**2.5.2.3.6.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `12463431`)

Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs When UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs message (5G_L1_IF_200_replaced([11513831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is received by 5G-L2-PS from 5G-UL-L1,

5G-L2-PS reads configuration parameter [Before CB012464-C] actNrUlRipMeasurement [End CB012464-C] [CB012464-C-UPD002] actNrUlRipCounter [End CB012464-C-UPD002] (see 5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_IF_1988_replaced([10971056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Um1c_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If [Before CB012464-C] actNrUlRipMeasurement [End CB012464-C] [CB012464-C-UPD002] actNrUlRipCounter [End CB012464-C-UPD002] is not equal to disabled, then:

For each subcell in subcells field of UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs message:

• for each prbIndex in range of [0 .. numOfNoisePerPrbElem - 1]:

with:

numOfNoisePerPrbElem : is the size of noisePerPrb array

5G-L2-PS UL Scheduler updates instantAvgUlRipSchedPrbForCurrentSlot_dBm[ prbIndex ] internal counter with a new received interference power measurement value from noisePerPrb [ prbIndex ] field, as specified in 5G_L2_5369.

---

##### 2.5.2.3.6.0-4 Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs Evaluation of NR UL Received Total Wideband Power measurement results (ID: 11180202)

**2.5.2.3.6.0-4.0-4**  (ID: `12690600`)

Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs When UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs message (5G_L1_IF_200_replaced([11513831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is received by 5G-L2-PS from 5G-L1-UL,

5G-L2-PS shall read configuration parameter actRtwpMeasurement (see 5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_IF_1988_replaced([10971056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Um1c_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in PsCell_CellSetupReq(see 5G_L2_IF_61_replaced([10967196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTc_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and MeasurementTypeList in PsCell_TestMeasurementReq if any.

If actRtwpMeasurement is set to true,or MeasurementTypeList IE equal to RTWP until processing period is completed(see 5G_UP_ALG_5276_replaced([11215591](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxUQ9fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), then:

for each subcell:

  * 5G-L2-PS shall use IE subcellId to access ulSpatialStreamIds (see 5G_L2_10801) array for the given UL subcell.
  * Then, for each grant:



for each ulSpatialStreamOfTheSubcell (from 0 to numOfmeas):

on 7-2a (actEcpri72e == FALSE), numOfmeas = the maximum size of linRssiOfAnt - 1,

on 7-2e (actEcpri72e == TRUE), numOfmeas = ueReceiverSize(5G_L2_17840) - 1.

  * 5G-L2-PS shall set ulSpatialStreamOfTheCell = ulSpatialStreamIds[ulSpatialStreamOfTheSubcell].
  * If ulSpatialStreamOfTheCell is a valid number:
  * 5G-L2-PS shall read the following values from PuschAntMeas structure (5G_L1_IF_14994_replaced([11519518](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSXlvfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

  * linRssiOfAnt[ulSpatialStreamOfTheSubcell] - RSSI received for all the scheduled PRBs for the given UE,

  * linNoiseOfAnt[ulSpatialStreamOfTheSubcell] - I+N (Interference and Noise power) value received for all the scheduled PRBs for the given UE.

  * If any of those two values above is less than or equal to 10 attowatts (10^(-17) W (Watt), see 5G_UP_ALG_7421_replaced([11109729](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ko7J_fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L1([13337195](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Qwj9YNnGEfCmxLW1M7HMrQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9))), the sample shall be discarded.

  * 5G-L2-PS shall perform the aggregation logic to calculate the value of RTWP, as specified in 5G_UP_ALG_17492_replaced([11215790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxVfFPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).



With:

ulSpatialStreamOfTheSubcell - UL spatial stream of the subcell.

ulSpatialStreamOfTheCell - UL spatial stream of the cell.

Rationale: 5G-L1-UL shall provide linRssiOfAnt and linNoiseOfAnt measurements independently for each of the subcells, while 5G-L2-PS shall aggregate the measurements and fill NR UL RTWP PM counters for all the spatial streams of the whole cell. Each UL spatial stream of the subcell shall have a unique identifier within the cell (ulSpatialStreamOfTheCell).

Note that:

  1. The measurements shall be aggregated independently for each ulSpatialStreamOfTheCell.
  2. During the aggregation, 5G-L2-PS shall use the locally stored startPrb and numOfPrb IE from PuschAllocationConfig structure (5G_L1_IF_14958_replaced([11519502](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FSXluvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of UlData_PuschReceiveReq (see 5G_L1_IF_191_replaced([11513756](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRy99_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).
  3. During the aggregation, 5G-L2-PS shall use the locally stored longPucchStartPuschPrb and longPucchNumPuschPrb [CB012299-A] , longPucchStartPuschPrb2 and longPucchNumPuschPrb2 [End CB012299-A] IE from cellBwp structure (5G_L2_IF_95_replaced([10968336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UXk5_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsCell_CellSetupReq (see 5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))). Restriction of number of PRBs, which is specified in 5G_UP_ALG_17492_replaced([11215790](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kxVfFPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), shall be considered as required only if pucchModeSelect IE from PsCell_CellSetupReq was set to longPucch.

---

##### 2.5.2.3.6.0-5 Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs Evaluation of sinr measurements for IRC Gain estimation (ID: 11180227)

**2.5.2.3.6.0-5.0-1**  (ID: `11180231`)

Reception of UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs When UlData_PuschReceiveRespPs message (5G_L1_IF_200_replaced([11513831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FRzlAPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is received by 5G-L2-PS from 5G-L1-UL,

5G-L2-PS shall perform SINR long-term averaging as described in 5G_UP_ALG_19665_replaced([11140137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsKFvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for IRC gain estimation.

#### 2.5.2.3.7 PM Counter Support

##### 2.5.2.3.7.0-1 PM Counter Support Number of failed receptions of UL TBs at gNB after reaching DRB specific max HARQ ReTx by UE (ID: 11180242)

**2.5.2.3.7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11180248`)

PM Counter Support For 'NR UL HARQ' class, according to 5G_UP_ALG_6272_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PM Counter M55302C15001 (UL_TB_F_MAX_RTX_DRB_MAX_LM) shall be incremented each time a maximum number of HARQ transmissions has been reached for transport block for which DRB-specific transmissions limit was selected (please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_12741_replaced([11203324](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_7971_replaced([11144196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_234YSvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_7973_replaced([11145642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24A7IvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

##### 2.5.2.3.7.0-2 PM Counter Support Number of initial transmissions of UL TBs for which DRB specific HARQ maxTx limit applied (ID: 11180253)

**2.5.2.3.7.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11180257`)

PM Counter Support For 'NR UL HARQ' class, according to 5G_UP_ALG_6272_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PM Counter M55302C15002 (UL_TB_INTX_DRB_MAX_LM) shall be incremented each time any HARQ feedback (ACK, NACK or DTX) is received for an initial transmission of the transport block for which DRB-specific transmissions limit was selected (please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_12741_replaced([11203324](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_7971_replaced([11144196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_234YSvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_7973_replaced([11145642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24A7IvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

---

##### 2.5.2.3.7.0-3 PM Counter Support Number of HARQ ReTx of UL TBs for which DRB specific HARQ maxTx limit applied (ID: 11180264)

**2.5.2.3.7.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11180271`)

PM Counter Support For 'NR UL HARQ' class, according to 5G_UP_ALG_6272_replaced([11230269](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kytYEPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), PM Counter M55302C15003 (UL_TB_RETX_DRB_MAX_LM) shall be incremented each time any HARQ feedback (ACK, NACK or DTX) is received for a retransmission of the transport block for which DRB-specific transmissions limit was selected (please refer to 5G_UP_ALG_12741_replaced([11203324](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwejePvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_7971_replaced([11144196](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_234YSvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_7973_replaced([11145642](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24A7IvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

##### 2.5.2.3.7.0-4 PM Counter Support Number of successfully received UL TBs after any Txn for TBs with DRB specific HARQ maxTx limit applied (ID: 11180276)

**2.5.2.3.7.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11180281`)

#### 2.5.2.4.1 Exceptions

Exceptions The general exceptions in 5G_L2_13440_replaced([11178780](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27By6_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) apply.
