#### 2.5.2.4.2 Filling of UlData_PucchReceiveReq

##### 2.5.2.4.2.0-1 Filling of UlData_PucchReceiveReq PUCCH format 0 (ID: 11180313)

**2.5.2.4.2.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12568966`)

Filling of UlData_PucchReceiveReq To request a PUCCH format 0, 5G-L2-PS shall populate the UlData_PucchReceiveReq message as followed:

IE pucchFormat is set to 0

IE numOfLayers is set to 1 in all cases.

IE dmrsSequenceType is set to "type1" in all cases

IE startingPrb is set to

**\- if PrbBlanking is activated and TDD or FDD configuration, IE startingPrb of PucchFormat0 structure of PsUser_UserSetupReq**(5G_UP_ALG_1823_replaced([11110957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpJMY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))****

-Otherwise IE startingPrb of PucchFormat0 structure of PsUser_UserSetupReq **\+ the start PRB of the active bandwidth part**.****

**When HARQ feedback is not for a msg4 transmission, IE firstSymbol set to IE startingSymbol of PucchFormat0 structure with PUCCH Resource index as chosen in 5G_UP_ALG_18087_replaced([11187133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-UvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

**For PUCCH for Msg4/SRB0 message, IE firstSymbol is set to starting OFDM symbol determined at 5G_UP_ALG_18087_replaced([11187133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-UvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

IE numOfSymbols is set to 1.

IE frequencyHopping is set to FALSE.

IE initialCyclicShift is determined at 5G_UP_ALG_18087_replaced([11187133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-UvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

IE nANPucch is set to 1.

**IE nANPucch is set to the number of scheduled DL transport blocks, the value is same as total DAI value in DCI (see 5G_L2_278_replaced([11150432](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24cY8fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). The range is 1 and 2.**

IE nANPucch is set to 1 for Msg4/SRB0 message PUCCH feedback.

IE numOfBitsOfUciInformation set to 1.

numOfBitsOfUciInformation is set to the same as nANPucch if the UCI is used for HARQ ack report

**On a FDD carrier shared with LTE (DSS), and according 5G_UP_ALG_2460_replaced([11116030](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp0h0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_18087_replaced([11187133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-UvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_22280_replaced([11187527](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvbanPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),**

 if SR is multiplexed with HARQ feedback (same starting symbol)

o numOfBitsOfUciInformation=1,

o srBitDetection is set to ’true’,

o nANPucch is set to ‘1’

 for SR only,

o numOfBitsOfUciInformation=0,

o srBitDetection is set to ’true’,

o nANPucch is set to ‘0’

 for HARQ A/N only,

o numOfBitsOfUciInformation=1,

o srBitDetection is set to ’false’,

o nANPucch is set to ‘1’

Note: above settings of numOfBitsOfUciInformation IE assume that SR is counted as UCI bit in 5G_L1_5G21A_218 and in 5G_L1_5G21A_1134.

IE harqProcessIndex set to value selected in 5G_UP_ALG_4531_replaced([11184177](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvQbgPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

IE harqProcessIndex is not used. 5G-L2-PS will maintain the relationship between PUCCH and HARQ process information according to 5G_UP_ALG_18215_replaced([11187299](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvaMdPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 5G-L2-PS can set any value within range defined in 5G_L1_5G21A_215 (e.g. 0)

Note, as dmrsScramblingSequenceInt is not meaningful with PUCCH format 0, it is not needed to set it to a specific value.

In TDD/FDD, srBitDetection is set to FALSE for SA mode, PUCCH ACK for Msg4/SRB0 message.

**If SR only is multiplexed with HARQ feadback (as decided in 5G_UP_ALG_4327_replaced([11177617](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsNPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), IE srBitDetection is set to true.**

IE modulationType is meaningless for PUCCH Format 0

IE additionalDMRS is set to DISABLED

Note, the IE secondHopPrb is meaningless if the IE frequencyHopping is set to FALSE

**[Before CB007491-H-UPD002]IE longTermCfoMetric is not used by L1 and can be set to any allowed value.**[End CB007491-H-UPD002]****

IE longTermCfoMetricOfAnt[0..3] shall be set to 0.

**Based on the number of PUCCH symbols to be received (as determined in 5G_UP_ALG_4587_replaced([11187257](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvZlhPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) & the common PUCCH resources (5G_UP_ALG_18087_replaced([11187133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-UvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the following is set:**

For one PUCCH symbol reception

  * IE numberOfSymbols is set to 1.

  * IE frequencyHopping is set to FALSE.




If symbol 12 is used:

  * IE startingPrb is set to Prb index determined for the 1st hop (as in 5G_UP_ALG_18087_replaced([11187133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-UvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) + the PRB offset of the initial UL bandwidth part.

  * IE firstSymbol is set to 12.




otherwise (symbol 13)

  * IE startingPrb is set to Prb index determined for the 2nd hop (as in 5G_UP_ALG_18087_replaced([11187133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-UvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) + the PRB offset of the initial UL bandwidth part.

  * IE firstSymbol is set to 13.




For two PUCCH symbol reception

  * IE numberOfSymbols is set to 2.

  * IE frequencyHopping is set to TRUE.

  * IE startingPrb is set to Prb index determined for the 1st hop (as in 5G_UP_ALG_18087_replaced([11187133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-UvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) + the PRB offset of the initial UL bandwidth part.

  * IE secondHopPrb is set to Prb index determined for the 2nd hop (as in 5G_UP_ALG_18087_replaced([11187133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-UvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) + the PRB offset of the initial UL bandwidth part.

  * IE firstSymbol is set to 12.




On a FDD carrier shared with LTE (DSS), 

  * IE numberOfSymbols is set to 1,

  * IE startingPrb shall be set according 5G_UP_ALG_2455_replaced([11116019](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp0h0PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)),

  * IE firstSymbol is set to shall be set according 5G_UP_ALG_2460_replaced([11116030](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp0h0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_18087_replaced([11187133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-UvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_22280_replaced([11187527](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvbanPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))




CP2 references:

\- 5G_UP_ALG_4601_replaced([11187373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvazg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Configuration of 5G-L1-UL for UCI Reception on xPUCCH

---

##### 2.5.2.4.2.0-2 Filling of UlData_PucchReceiveReq PUCCH format 1 (ID: 11180342)

**2.5.2.4.2.0-2.0-12**  (ID: `12568970`)

Filling of UlData_PucchReceiveReq Separate resources are defined for HARQ A/N feedback, and the scheduling request indication and hence different configuration structures are applied. The pucchConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_403_replaced([10975137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Afu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is relevant for the related to HARQ A/N and the perSrConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_424_replaced([10975471](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VBFKfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the resources related to SR. The PUCCH resource carrying HARQ A/N **of Msg4/SRB0** is determined in 5G_UP_ALG_ 18087.****

To request a PUCCH Format 1, 5G-L2-PS shall populate the UlData_PucchReceiveReq message (see 5G_L1_IF_216_replaced([11513990](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR0MIfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) as follows:

IE pucchFormat shall be set to 1

IE numOfLayers shall be set to 1

IE dmrsSequenceType is set to "type1" in all cases

IE startPrb:

 For SR resource, shall be set to

\- If TDD or FDD configuration and PrbBlanking activated, the start PRB of the active bandwidth part (5G_UP_ALG_1823_replaced([11110957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpJMY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

-Otherwise the start PRB of the active bandwidth part (5G_UP_ALG_1823_replaced([11110957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpJMY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **plus IE startingPrb of perSrConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_424_replaced([10975471](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VBFKfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq**

. if the UE's startingPrb of perSrConfig for periodic SR is aligned with sharedSrPrb and actSharedSr is True in PsCell_CellSetupReq, there is no need to request SR for the UE in UlData_PucchReceiveReq, even the UE is the only UE using sharedSrPrb for SR.

 For HARQ A/N resource, shall be set to

\- the start PRB of the active bandwidth part (5G_UP_ALG_1823_replaced([11110957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpJMY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) if TDD or FDD configuration and PrbBlanking feature activated

-otherwise the start PRB of the active bandwidth part (5G_UP_ALG_1823_replaced([11110957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpJMY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) **plus IE startingPrb of the PUCCH resource selected from pucchResourcesSet0 as per 5G_UP_ALG_4330_replaced([11177663](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_ 18087**

 For HARQ A/N of Msg4/SRB0, shall be set to the start PRB of the initial bandwidth part (5G_L2_IF_95_replaced([10968336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UXk5_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) plus the startingPrb for the 1st hop determined in 5G_UP_ALG_ 18087.

IE numOfPrb shall be set to 1

IE firstSymbol:

 For SR resource, shall be set to IE startingSymbolIndex of perSrConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_424_replaced([10975471](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VBFKfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq.

 For HARQ A/N resource, shall be set to IE startingSymbol of the PUCCH resource selected from pucchResourcesSet0 as per 5G_UP_ALG_4330_replaced([11177663](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_ 18087.

 For HARQ A/N of Msg4/SRB0, shall be set to the starting OFDM symbol defined in 5G_UP_ALG_ 18087.

IE numOfSymbols:

 For SR resource, shall be set to IE numOfSymbols of perSrConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_424_replaced([10975471](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VBFKfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq.

 For HARQ A/N resource, shall be set to IE numOfSymbols of the PUCCH resource selected from pucchResourcesSet0 as per 5G_UP_ALG_4330_replaced([11177663](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_ 18087.

 For HARQ A/N of Msg4/SRB0, shall be set to the number of symbols defined in 5G_UP_ALG_ 18087.

IE frequencyHopping:

 For SR resource, shall be set to IE intraSlotFrequencyHopping of the perSrConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_424_replaced([10975471](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VBFKfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq.

 For HARQ A/N resource, shall be set to IE intraSlotFrequencyHopping of the PUCCH resource selected from pucchResourcesSet0 as per 5G_UP_ALG_4330_replaced([11177663](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_ 18087.

 HARQ A/N of Msg4/SRB0, shall be set to ENABLED.

Note, by default C-Plane will set IE intraSlotFrequencyHopping to enabled but for testing/debugging purposes there is an R&D parameter in C-Plane allowing to disable intraSlotFrequencyHopping.

IE secondHopPrb:

 For SR resource, shall be set to

\- IE secondHopPrb of the perSrConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_424_replaced([10975471](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VBFKfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq **if PrbBlanking feature is activated** and TDD or FDD configuration.****

\- Otherwise IE secondHopPrb of the perSrConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_424_replaced([10975471](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VBFKfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq **plus start PRB of the active bandwidth part (5G_UP_ALG_1823_replaced([11110957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpJMY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**

 For HARQ A/N resource, shall be set

**-IE secondHopPrb of the PUCCH resource selected from pucchResourcesSet0 as per 5G_UP_ALG_4330_replaced([11177663](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_ 18087 if TDD or FDD configuration and PrbBlanking is activated**

-**]Otherwise IE secondHopPrb of the PUCCH resource selected from pucchResourcesSet0 as per 5G_UP_ALG_4330_replaced([11177663](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_ 18087 **plus start PRB of the active bandwidth part (5G_UP_ALG_1823_replaced([11110957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpJMY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**.** ****

 For HARQ A/N of Msg4/SRB0, shall be set to the start PRB of the initial bandwidth part (5G_L2_IF_95_replaced([10968336](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UXk5_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) plus the startingPrb for the 2nd hop determined in 5G_UP_ALG_ 18087.

IE initialCyclicShift:

 For SR resource, shall be set to IE initialCyclicShift of perSrConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_424_replaced([10975471](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VBFKfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq.

 For HARQ A/N resource, shall be set to IE initialCyclicShift of the PUCCH resource selected from pucchResourcesSet0 as per 5G_UP_ALG_4330_replaced([11177663](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_ 18087.

 For HARQ A/N of Msg4/SRB0, shall be set to the initial cyclic shift index determined in 5G_UP_ALG_ 18087.

IE timeDomainOcc shall be set according to 5G_UP_ALG_4330_replaced([11177663](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuwsPPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

IE nANPucch shall be set to the number of expected A/N bits.

IE srBitDetection:

 For SR resource, shall be set to TRUE

 For HARQ A/N or HARQ A/N of Msg4/SRB0, shall be set to FALSE

If nANPucch > 0 then IE numOfBitsOfUciInformation shall be set to nANPucch + number of expected SR bits, else IE numOfBitsOfUciInformation shall be set to zero (SR only). Note, numOfBitsOfUciInformation is used by L1 to select correct DTX threshold.

IE harqProcessIndex is not used. 5G-L2-PS will maintain the relationship between PUCCH and HARQ process information according to 5G_UP_ALG_ 18215. 5G-L2-PS can set any value within range defined in 5G_L1_5G21A_215 (e.g. 0)

IE modulationType shall be set to BPSK **if zero or single A/N bit is expected and to QPSK otherwise (corresponding to two A/N bits)**

Note, since always only 1 UCI bit is assigned to HARQ A/N and SR resources in FDD case, except the case of FDD-TDD CA **and except the case of FDD-FDD CA, BPSK shall be requested for all PUCCH Format 1 resources.**

IE additionalDMRS shall be set to DISABLED

[Before CB007491-H-UPD002]IE longTermCfoMetric shall be set to rrmAvgCfo computed in 5G_UP_ALG_3324_replaced([11150688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksVDQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[End CB007491-H-UPD002]

IE longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0..3] shall be set according to 5G_UP_ALG_3322_replaced([11150515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksT1LvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_12757_replaced([11170198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26Hz-vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

When FDD Supercell feature is active (NRCELL.actSupercellSingleSSB = TRUE),

[Before CB007491-H-UPD002]longTermCfoMetric,[End CB007491-H-UPD002]longTermCfoMetricOfBeam is set according to 5G_UP_ALG_3331_replaced([11151200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksXfjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_UP_ALG_3322_replaced([11150515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksT1LvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

When FDD Supercell feature is deactivated (NRCELL.actSupercellSingleSSB = FALSE),

L2-PS maintains legacy behaviour.

IE dataScramblingInt shall be set to the physCellId of the cell.

Note, as dmrsScramblingSequenceInt and maxCodeRate are meaningless for PUCCH Format 1, it is not needed to set the corresponding IEs to a specific value.

CP2 references:

 5G_UP_ALG_4601_replaced([11187373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvazg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Configuration of 5G-L1-UL for UCI Reception on xPUCCH

##### 2.5.2.4.2.0-3 Filling of UlData_PucchReceiveReq PUCCH format 2 (ID: 11180418)

**2.5.2.4.2.0-3.0-4**  (ID: `12568977`)

Filling of UlData_PucchReceiveReq If PUCCH f2 is scheduled for HARQ report, **IE startingPRB is set according to harqStartingPrb of pucchResourceSet[1] structure with PUCCH Resource index as chosen in 5G_UP_ALG_18087_replaced([11187133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-UvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

If PUCCH f2 is scheduled for HARQ report, **IE startingSymbol is set according to harqStartingSymbol of pucchResourceSet[1] structure with PUCCH Resource index as chosen in 5G_UP_ALG_18087_replaced([11187133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-UvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).**

If PUCCH f2 is scheduled for CSI report without HARQ report, IE startingPRB is set to startingPRB in perCsiReportConfig.

If PUCCH f2 is scheduled for HARQ report, IE nANPucch set to the number of scheduled serving cells over the DL slots reporting to the HARQ feedback reporting slot. The range is 3 to 8 for format 2

The range of nANPucch is 3 to 32 for format 2, with 8 scheduled serving cells over 4 consecutive DL slots.

otherwise, IE nANPucch is set to 0.

If _rdUsePucchF2OnlyForHarq is true (5G_L2_1189_replaced([11181836](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27XKEfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), nANPucch shall be incremented by 2 (first two bits are unused)._

numOfBitsOfUciInformation shall be set to the sum of nANPucch and the size of the expected CSI report, if any.

If PUCCH F2 is scheduled for HARQ report, numOfPrb is computed as per 5G_UP_ALG_4607_replaced([11187418](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvazi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**.**

IE dataScramblingInt shall be set to the physCellId of the cell.

IE dmrsScramblingSequenceInt shall be set to the physCellId of the cell.

IE harqProcessIndex is not used. 5G-L2-PS will maintain the relationship between PUCCH and HARQ process information according to 5G_UP_ALG_18215_replaced([11187299](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvaMdPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 5G-L2-PS can set any value within range defined in 5G_L1_5G21A_215 (e.g. 0)

On a FDD carrier shared with LTE (DSS), 

the IEs shall be set according 5G_UP_ALG_2460_replaced([11116030](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kp0h0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_18087_replaced([11187133](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvY-UvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_UP_ALG_22280_replaced([11187527](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvbanPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

IE modulationType is set to PucchFormat1to4_QPSK only

IE additionalDMRS is set to DISABLED

IE frequencyHopping is set to FALSE and thus the IE secondHopPrb is meaningless if the IE frequencyHopping is set to FALSE

[Before CB007491-H-UPD002]IE longTermCfoMetric is not used by L1 and can be set to any allowed value.[End CB007491-H-UPD002]

IE longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0..3] shall be set to 0.

IE dmrsSequenceType is set to "type1" in all cases

CP2 references:

\- 5G_UP_ALG_4601_replaced([11187373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvazg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Configuration of 5G-L1-UL for UCI Reception on xPUCCH

---

##### 2.5.2.4.2.0-4 Filling of UlData_PucchReceiveReq PUCCH format 3 (ID: 11180444)

**2.5.2.4.2.0-4.0-10**  (ID: `12568982`)

Filling of UlData_PucchReceiveReq Separate resources are defined for HARQ A/N feedback and periodic CSI reporting and hence different configuration structures are applied.The pucchConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_403_replaced([10975137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Afu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is relevant for the PUCCH Format 3 resources related to HARQ A/N (pucchResourceSet[1]) and **the perCsiReportConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_414_replaced([10975373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeHPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) for the PUCCH Format 3 resource related to periodic CSI.**

To request a PUCCH Format 3, 5G-L2-PS shall populate the UlData_PucchReceiveReq message (see 5G_L1_5G21A_215) as follows:

IE pucchFormat shall be set to 3

IE numOfLayers shall be set to 1

IE dmrsSequenceType shall be filled according to 5G_UP_ALG_21114_replaced([11104870](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koDAOPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If the PUCCH Format 3 contains periodic CSI resource but no HARQ A/N then

IE startPrb shall be set to

\- if TDD or FDD configuration and PrbBlanking feature is activated IE startingPrb of perCsiReportConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_414_replaced([10975373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeHPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq configuration.

\- Otherwise IE startingPrb of perCsiReportConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_414_replaced([10975373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeHPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq **plus the start PRB of the active bandwidth part (5G_UP_ALG_1823_replaced([11110957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpJMY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).**

IE numOfPrb shall be set to IE maxNrOfPrbs of perCsiReportConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_414_replaced([10975373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeHPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq

IE firstSymbol shall be set to IE startingSymbolIndex of perCsiReportConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_414_replaced([10975373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeHPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq

IE numOfSymbols shall be set to IE numOfSymbols of perCsiReportConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_414_replaced([10975373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeHPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq

nANPucch shall be set to 0

IE frequencyHopping shall be set to IE intraSlotFrequencyHopping of perCsiReportConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_414_replaced([10975373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeHPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq

IE secondHopPrb shall be set to

\- **if TDD or FDD configuration and PrbBlanking feature is activated** IE secondHopPrb of perCsiReportConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_414_replaced([10975373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeHPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq****

-Otherwise IE secondHopPrb of perCsiReportConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_414_replaced([10975373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeHPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq **plus start PRB of the active bandwidth part (5G_UP_ALG_1823_replaced([11110957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpJMY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**.****

If the PUCCH Format 3 contains HARQ A/N then

IE startPrb shall be set to 

\- if PrbBlanking feature is activated and TDD or FDD configuration IE startingPrb of the selected PUCCH resource (5G-UP_ALG_18087) of pucchConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_403_replaced([10975137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Afu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq

-Otherwise**[ IE startingPrb of the selected PUCCH resource (5G-UP_ALG_18087) of pucchConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_403_replaced([10975137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Afu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq **plus the start PRB of the active bandwidth part (5G_UP_ALG_1823_replaced([11110957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpJMY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))****

IE numOfPrb shall be set as calculated in 5G_UP_ALG_458_replaced([11098681](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_km_3UfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

IE firstSymbol shall be set to IE startingSymbol of the selected PUCCH resource (5G-UP_ALG_18087) of pucchConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_403_replaced([10975137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Afu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq

IE numOfSymbols shall be set to IE numOfSymbols of the selected PUCCH resource (5G-UP_ALG_18087) of pucchConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_403_replaced([10975137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Afu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq

IE nANPucch shall be set to the number of expected HARQ A/N bits

IE frequencyHopping shall be set to IE intraSlotFrequencyHopping of the selected PUCCH resource (5G-UP_ALG_18087) of pucchConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_403_replaced([10975137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Afu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq

IE secondHopPrb shall be set to

  * if PrbBlanking feature is activated and TDD or FDD configuration IE secondHopPrb of the selected PUCCH resource (5G-UP_ALG_18087) of pucchConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_403_replaced([10975137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Afu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq

  * Otherwise IE secondHopPrb of the selected PUCCH resource (5G-UP_ALG_18087) of pucchConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_403_replaced([10975137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Afu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq **plus start PRB of the active bandwidth part (5G_UP_ALG_1823_replaced([11110957](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpJMY_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))**




IE numOfBitsOfUciInformation shall be set to the sum of nANPucch and the size of the expected CSI report, if any, plus 1 bit for SR, if any.

IE srBitDetection shall be set to FALSE

IE maxCodeRate shall be set to IE maxCodeRate of pucchFormatConfigF3 structure of pucchConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_403_replaced([10975137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Afu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq

IE dataScramblingInt shall be set to the physCellId of the cell.

IE dmrsScramblingSequenceInt shall be set to the physCellId of the cell.

IE harqProcessIndex is not used. 5G-L2-PS will maintain the relationship between PUCCH and HARQ process information according to 5G-UP_ALG_18215. 5G-L2-PS can set any value within range defined in 5G_L1_5G21A_215 (e.g. 0)

IE modulationType shall be set to QPSK **if pi2Bpsk is false and to BPSK if pi2Bpsk is true, whereby pi2Bpsk is an IE initially provided by PsUser_UserSetupReq. pi2Bpsk can be reconfigured by C-Plane via PsUser_UserModifyReq (from false to true once the UE capability is known in SA case)**

Note, only QPSK is supported for PUCCH Format 3 before 5GC000885-F.

IE additionalDMRS shall be set according to IE additionalDmrs in pucchFormatConfigF3 structure in pucchConfig (5G_L2_IF_403_replaced([10975137](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2U_3Afu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in PsUser_UserSetupReq or PsUser_UserModifyReq.

[Before CB007491-H-UPD002]IE longTermCfoMetric shall be set to rrmAvgCfo computed in 5G_UP_ALG_3324_replaced([11150688](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksVDQ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).[End CB007491-H-UPD002]

[PR831459] [End PR831459]

IE longTermCfoMetricOfBeam[0..3] shall be set according to 5G_UP_ALG_3322_replaced([11150515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksT1LvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L2_12757_replaced([11170198](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26Hz-vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

When FDD Supercell feature is active (NRCELL.actSupercellSingleSSB = TRUE),

[Before CB007491-H-UPD002]longTermCfoMetric,[End CB007491-H-UPD002]longTermCfoMetricOfBeam is set according to 5G_UP_ALG_3331_replaced([11151200](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksXfjfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))/5G_UP_ALG_3322_replaced([11150515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksT1LvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

When FDD Supercell feature is deactivated (NRCELL.actSupercellSingleSSB = FALSE),

L2-PS maintains legacy behaviour.

Note, the IEs initialCyclicShift is meaningless for PUCCH Format 3

Note, by default C-Plane will set IE intraSlotFrequencyHopping to enabled but for testing/debugging purposes there is an R&D parameter in C-Plane allowing to disabled intraSlotFrequencyHopping.

CP2 references:

\- 5G_UP_ALG_4601_replaced([11187373](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kvazg_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) Configuration of 5G-L1-UL for UCI Reception on xPUCCH

#### 2.5.2.4.3 Reception of UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs

##### 2.5.2.4.3.0-1 Reception of UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs Evaluation of NR UL Received Interference Power measurement results (ID: 11180510)

**2.5.2.4.3.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12463450`)

Reception of UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs When UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs message (5G_L1_IF_221_replaced([11514182](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2BQvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is received by 5G-L2-PS from 5G-UL-L1,

5G-L2-PS reads configuration parameter [Before CB012464-C] actNrUlRipMeasurement [End CB012464-C] [CB012464-C-UPD002] actNrUlRipCounter [End CB012464-C-UPD002] see 5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_IF_1988_replaced([10971056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Um1c_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If [Before CB012464-C] actNrUlRipMeasurement [End CB012464-C] [CB012464-C-UPD002] actNrUlRipCounter [End CB012464-C-UPD002] is not equal to disabled, then:

For each subcell in subcells field of UlData_PucchReceiveRespPs message:

  * If pucchModeSelect is equal to longPucch and [Before CB012464-C] actNrUlRipMeasurement [End CB012464-C] [CB012464-C-UPD002] actNrUlRipCounter [End CB012464-C-UPD002] is equal to enabledWithoutPUCCH_F1 or enabledWithoutPRACH_PUCCH_F1, then for each decoded control data on PUCCH:



If pucchFormat == 1:

  * 5G-L2-PS shall exclude measurements where prbIndex >= startPrb and prbIndex < startPrb + numOfPrb.
  * If secondHopPrb != startPrb:



5G-L2-PS shall exclude measurements where prbIndex >= secondHopPrb and prbIndex < secondHopPrb + numOfPrb.

with:

prbIndex: measurement index for a given Physical Resource Block in noisePerPrb array.

To exclude Received Interference Power measurements for PUCCH Format 1 PRBs, 5G-L2-PS shall override the received values from noisePerPrb array with Invalid Value = -140 dBm.

  * 5G-L2-PS DL Scheduler forwards field array noisePerPrb to UL Scheduler.
  * For each prbIndex in range of [0 .. numOfNoisePerPrbElem - 1]:



with:

numOfNoisePerPrbElem : size of noisePerPrb array

5G-L2-PS UL Scheduler updates instantAvgUlRipSchedPrbForCurrentSlot_dBm[ prbIndex ] internal counter

with the new received interference power measurement value from noisePerPrb [ prbIndex ] field, as specified in 5G_L2_5369_replaced([11194326](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28ytcPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**2.5.2.4.4.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11180544`)

rdForceAckOnPucch (see 5G_L2_12250_replaced([11183211](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27hiLPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) must be set to TRUE.

[End CB009363-B]

##### 2.5.2.4.4.0-3 Sending of UlData_PucchReceiveReq workaround Use staticLongPucchConfigEcpri in PUCCH receive requests (ID: 11180548)

**2.5.2.4.4.0-3.0-3**  (ID: `12825306`)

Sending of UlData_PucchReceiveReq workaround If 8Rx IRC receiver – ABIP FR1 TDD feature (CB009363) is active (see 5G_RAN_OP_2643) and pucchF3BeamformingEnabled is false

Then:

For the initial 8RX IRC tests with the uplink C8 subcell and PUCCH=8RX (5G_L2_12903_replaced([11155753](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2466HvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) in case of long PUCCH (PUCCH formats 1 and 3) staticLongPucchConfigEcpri should be used.

For example: For C8 subcell the L2-PS should fill patternIds, numCeAxCIndex, ceAxCIndex of staticLongPucchConfigEcpri.

The patternIds arrays of pucchResources should be set to invalidPatternId (0x0000) in this case.

Please check: 5G_UP_2089_replaced([11379387](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_uegp0PvkEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

Note: This requirement shall be changed or removed when all tests of CB009363-B will be done (likely for dynamic 8RX PUCCH scheme in CB009363-E).[CB008577-A]For PUCCH=8RX in FDD cell with actBeamforming = TRUE, pucchF3BeamformingEnabled is false but staticLongPucchConfigEcpri shall be ignored.[End CB008577-A]

### 2.5.2.5 Physical Random Access Channel Receive

#### 2.5.2.5.1 Exceptions

##### 2.5.2.5.1.0-1 Exceptions Expected Exceptions (ID: 11180574)

**2.5.2.5.1.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11180578`)

Exceptions The general exceptions in 5G_L2_13440_replaced([11178780](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27By6_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) apply.

---

#### 2.5.2.5.2 Transmission of UlData_PrachReceiveReq

##### 2.5.2.5.2.0-1 Transmission of UlData_PrachReceiveReq Skipping UlData_PrachReceiveReq Transmissions (ID: 11180590)

**2.5.2.5.2.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12828383`)

Transmission of UlData_PrachReceiveReq In FR2 in PRACH slots 5G-L2-PS shall skip the transmission of the UlData_PrachReceiveReq if at least one of the slots preceding the PRACH slot has been skipped.

When at least one slot preceding the PRACH slot has been skipped it means that there was a long runnig task which lastet more than one slot duration and which ended at an unusal point in time, maybe in the middle or at the end of the PRACH slot. Thus, the PRACH scheduling might start late and 5G-L2-PS might send the UlData_PrachReceiveReq too late, missing the allowed L1 receive window (see L1 receive window definition in 5G_L2_459_replaced([11153052](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24rpivvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L1_IF_283_replaced([11514791](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5rpPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) and 5G_L1_IF_285_replaced([11514834](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR5rqvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))). This shall be prevented to avoid error logs in 5G-L1-UL.

[PR852424] L2-PS shall also skip the transmission of the UlData_PrachReceiveReq if all prachOccasions[0] bits are set to 0. Refer to [11152306](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksfbU_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for detail about prachOccasions setting. [End PR852424]

When 5G-L2-PS skips the UlData_PrachReceiveReq transmission it shall not increment the PM counter NR Rach Usage/PRACH_REC_REQ (M55306C10003).

---

#### 2.5.2.5.3 Reception of UlData_PrachReceiveInd

##### 2.5.2.5.3.0-1 Reception of UlData_PrachReceiveInd Evaluation of NR UL Received Interference Power measurement results (ID: 11180606)

**2.5.2.5.3.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `12466413`)

Reception of UlData_PrachReceiveInd When UlData_PrachReceiveInd message (5G_L1_IF_234_replaced([11514309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2oWvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is received by 5G-L2-PS from 5G-UL-L1,

5G-L2-PS reads configuration parameter [Before CB012464-C] actNrUlRipMeasurement [End CB012464-C] [CB012464-C-UPD002] actNrUlRipCounter [End CB012464-C-UPD002] see 5G_L2_IF_73_replaced([10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_IF_1988_replaced([10971056](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2Um1c_u6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

If [Before CB012464-C] actNrUlRipMeasurement [End CB012464-C] [CB012464-C-UPD002] actNrUlRipCounter [End CB012464-C-UPD002] is equal to enabledWithPRACH_PUCCH_F1 or enabledWithoutPUCCH_F1, then:

For each subcell in subcells field of UlData_PrachReceiveInd message:

  * 5G-L2-PS DL Scheduler forwards the new received interference power measurement value from noisePower field to UL Scheduler.
  * 5G-L2-PS UL Scheduler accesses cell configuration parameters prachPrbOffset and prachWidth.
  * As PRACH estimation is done per slot for whole bandwidth, not per each PRB (see 5G_PM_552),



5G-L2-PS UL Scheduler calculates prachReceivedInterferencePowerForPrb by following the formula:

prachReceivedInterferencePowerForPrb = noisePower - 10 × log10(prachWidth)

with:

noisePower PRACH Received Interference Power for whole bandwidth forwarded from DL Scheduler;

prachWidth : Width of PRACH channel obtained from cell configuration.

Note: Operation 10 × log10(prachWidth) in logarithmic domain (in dBm unit) is equivalent to dividing by the channel width in the linear domain.

  * For each prbIndex in range of [prachPrbOffset .. prachPrbOffset + prachWidth- 1]:



5G-L2-PS UL Scheduler updates instantAvgUlRipSchedPrbForCurrentSlot_dBm[ prbIndex ] internal counter with prachReceivedInterferencePowerForPrb value, as specified in 5G_L2_5369_replaced([11194326](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28ytcPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

---

#### 2.5.2.6.2 SRS Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL

##### 2.5.2.6.2.0-1 SRS Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL Transmission of UlData_SrsReceiveReq for aperiodic SRS (ID: 11180649)

**2.5.2.6.2.0-1.0-5**  (ID: `11180676`)

SRS Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL 5G-L2-PS shall request the reception of an aperiodic SRS as specified in 5G_UP_ALG_5057_replaced([11201982](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwa5GvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) by sending the message UlData_SrsReceiveReq to 5G-L1-UL, see5G_L1_IF_235_replaced([11514315](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2oW_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall set the numCeAxCIndex according to 5G_L2_13125_replaced([11180760](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27OnPfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall set the ceAxcIndex according to 5G_L2_13128_replaced([11180785](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27PORPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall set the patternId according to 5G_UP_ALG_1909_replaced([11111524](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpOE7PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). For [Before CB010708-C] ulSubcellType C8 [CB010708-C] Srs is 8Rx or 16Rx(numOfRxSrs=8 or 16, see 5G_L2_16925_replaced([11141685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23qV0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB010708-C]patternId shall be set according to 5G_UP_ALG_1538_replaced([11106491](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koY-c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB010708-C] and 5G_L2_17842_replaced([11179842](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27Ign_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))(for eCPRI 7-2e)[End CB010708-C].

5G-L2-PS shall not send UlData_SrsReceiveReq to 5G-L1-UL for reception of aperiodic SRS and stop scheduling aperiodic SRS as SRS muted as in 5G_UP_ALG_5062_replaced([11202027](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwbgJvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) during the transient phase, which is corresponding to the period between receving PsUser_UserModifyReq and receiving PsUser_RrcReconfCompleteReq, if the IE nrofSrsPorts in srsResource[0], as in 5G_L2_IF_411_replaced([10975309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeFfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)), is updated in PsUser_UserModifyReq.

Before sending UlData_SrsReceiveReq for any subcell, 5G-L2-PS shall judge whether certain subcell shall be buffered according to 5G_UP_ALG_5214_replaced([11209976](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kw298fvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). bufferedUlConfig is a structure used in UlData_SrsReceiveReq to control buffered UL usage and it shall be filled regardless of whether buffered UL is used or not (5G_L1_5G21A_264).

##### 2.5.2.6.2.0-2 SRS Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL Transmission of UlData_SrsReceiveReq for periodic SRS (ID: 11180683)

**2.5.2.6.2.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `11180706`)

SRS Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL 5G-L2-PS shall request the reception of periodic SRS, for users which are configured with periodic SRS in active BWP, by sending the message UlData_SrsReceiveReq to 5G-L1-UL, see 5G_L1_IF_235_replaced([11514315](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR2oW_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

About SRS measurement for UL beam management, 5G-L2-PS shall provide parameters to 5G-L1-UL according to algorithm defined in 5G_UP_ALG_2151_replaced([11154219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrolPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

About SRS measurement for SU-MIMO, 5G-L2-PS shall provide parameters to 5G-L1-UL according to algorithm defined in 5G_UP_ALG_3246_replaced([11155645](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kswhHPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

5G-L2-PS shall set the patternId according to 5G_UP_ALG_1538_replaced([11106491](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_koY-c_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) [CB010708-C] and 5G_L2_17842_replaced([11179842](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27Ign_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))(for eCPRI 7-2e)[End CB010708-C] for [Before CB010708-C] ulSubcellType C8 [CB010708-C] Srs is 8Rx or 16Rx(numOfRxSrs=8 or 16, see 5G_L2_16925_replaced([11141685](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23qV0_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)))[End CB010708-C].

---

##### 2.5.2.6.2.0-3 SRS Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL Setting IEs of SrsReceiveReq (ID: 11180713)

**2.5.2.6.2.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11180718`)

SRS Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL IEs srsPowerThreshold are set according to the table below:

|   
---|---  
srsPowerThreshold | srsPowerThresholdDl  
From NIDD NRBTS.NRCELL.srsForBeamMgmt.srsPowerThresholdForUlBm | From NIDD NRBTS.NRCELL.srsForBeamMgmt.srsPowerThresholdForDlBm  
  
Note: 

1, In eCPRI 7-2e (5G_L2_18130_replaced([11155228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2432wvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), the SRS CoMa DTX detection is done by L1 itself, the related DTX threshold is indicated by L2 per UlData_SrsReceiveReq mesage, which means online modification of NIDD parameter of srsPowerThresholdForDlBm and srsPowerThresholdForUlBm , new threshold will apply to exist UEs and new attaching UE . This is unlike in eCPRI 7-2a, the DTX detection is done by L2PS and new threshold only is applied to new attaching UEs. Also in eCPRI 7-2a case, L1 doesn't use this IE, for common implementation purpose, L2 sets those threshold always.

---

**2.5.2.6.2.0-4.0-8**  (ID: `11180831`)

SRS Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL Setting of the IE freqDomainPosition

---

**2.5.2.6.2.0-4.0-8.0-1**  (ID: `11180836`)

SRS Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL For eCPRI 7-2e (5G_L2_18130_replaced([11155228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2432wvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), with Pscell_cellSetup > actDlSrsSubbandBm = ture, in case of uetype=3 (refer 5G_L1_IF_244_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), L2-PS shall fill the freqDomainPosition with the actually hopping SRS sunband's freqDomainPosition , rather than fixed initial value which is configured by L3.

freqDomainPosition= srsSubbandId* (sizeSrsSb/4).

sizeSrsSb is from Pscell_cellSetup.

srsSubbandId is from srsRtBf structure.

Note: This is to help L1 that , with informations is contained in srsSuMimo structure ( doesn't need cross check in srsRtBf structure), to find the relative start Prb position within the SB BF SRS's pilot.

---

SRS Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL Setting of commons IEs

**2.5.2.6.2.0-5.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `11180891`)

SRS Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL If srsBmEnable filled with False, since L1 will ignore srsBmStruct(5G_L1_IF_241_replaced([11514379](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZPvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), IEs in srsBmStruct will not be filled, random value maybe exist in the interface.

IEs srsPowerThreshold & numSrsSymbols are set according to the table below:

|   
---|---  
actEcpri72e | numSrsSymbols  
[Before CB009514-L] disabled [CB009514-L] FALSE [End CB009514-L] | 1  
[Before CB009514-L] enabled [CB009514-L] TRUE [End CB009514-L] | If two different startPositions scheduled for this slot 2 else 1 startPositions is configured in srsConfig structure (5G_L2_IF_411_replaced([10975309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeFfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of PsUser_UserSetupReq/PsUser_UserModifyReq

**2.5.2.6.2.0-5.0-2**  (ID: `11180897`)

SRS Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL Setting IEs of the SRS_BM_resource structure

---

**2.5.2.6.2.0-5.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `13455724`)

SRS Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL IE rnti is set to the C-RNTI of the UE.

[CB015122-A]

IE bmUeContextIndex shall be set to 0 when actSrsBmCalcInL1 is set to False (see [10966124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) or [11153567](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24vT4vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)); otherwise it shall be set as a unique ID for each UE with SRS BF context per subcell (see [11153909](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24xJHvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), [11154564](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_240zcfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and [11155222](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2432wfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). The parameter is used to distinguish UEs and proceed the DFT beam selection algorithm in 5G-L1-DU (see [11153978](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspzZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). The maximum value is limited according to [11514405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

IE srsResourceInfo IE shall be filled according to [13456276](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_1CPuWSzqEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

IE bmUeContextOperation is a bitmask parameter. It shall be set to 0 when actSrsBmCalcInL1 is set to False (see [10966124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) or [11153567](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24vT4vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)); otherwise it shall be filled according to [11514405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9). The UL BM reset shall be triggered according to [11153981](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24xwKvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)[End CB015122-A][CB015122-B] and the DL BM reset according to [11154615](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_240zePvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).[End CB015122-B].

IE ignoreBm shall be set to True, if UE is selected for skipping SRS BM decoding request (refer [11180831](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27POTfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), otherwise shall be set to False.

IE symbolPosition shall be set to IE startPosition of the selected srs resource in srsConfig structure ([10975309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeFfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) of PsUser_UserSetupReq/PsUser_UserModifyReq ([11154174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))**.**

IE srsBmSubbandId shall be set to IE subBandId of the selected srs resource in srsConfig structure ([10975309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeFfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) of PsUser_UserSetupReq/PsUser_UserModifyReq.

IE transmissionCombId shall be set to IE subBandId of the selected srs resource in srsConfig structure ([10975309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeFfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) of PsUser_UserSetupReq/PsUser_UserModifyReq.

IE bmCyclicShift shall be set to IE cyclicShift of the selected srs resource in srsConfig structure ([10975309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeFfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) of PsUser_UserSetupReq/PsUser_UserModifyReq ([11154174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

IE srsResourceIdentity shall be set to IE srsRecourceId of the selected srs resource in srsConfig structure ([10975309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeFfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) of PsUser_UserSetupReq/PsUser_UserModifyReq.

IE startPrb shall be set to IE freqDomainPosition of the selected srs resource in srsConfig structure ([10975309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeFfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)) of PsUser_UserSetupReq/PsUser_UserModifyReq ([11154174](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksrBi_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

**2.5.2.6.2.0-5.0-3**  (ID: `13456276`)

SRS Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL Setting srsResourceInfo IE from SRS_BM_resource structure

---

**2.5.2.6.2.0-5.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `13456286`)

SRS Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL IE srsResourceInfo is a bitmask parameter. It shall be set to 0 when actSrsBmCalcInL1 is set to False (see [10966124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) or [11153567](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24vT4vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)); otherwise it shall be filled according to [13456276](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_1CPuWSzqEfGxldjOZQLezQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), and:

  * Bit 0: usageUlBm shall be set to 1 only when actUlSrsBm is True (see [10968891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBKvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).

  * [CB015122-B]Bit 1: usageDlBm: shall be set to 1 only when actDlSrsBm is True (see [10968891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBKvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).[End CB015122-B]

  * Bits 2-3: portIndex shall be set to:

  * when usageUlBm is 1 and usageDlBm is 0, then 0
  * when usageUlBm is 0 and usageDlBm is 1, then both bits shall be set to 1
  * when usageUlBm is 1 and usageDlBm is 1, then:
    * if (srsTypeAllocForDlBm is TAS or UE does not support TAS), then it shall be 0;
    * if (srsTypeAllocForDlBm is CODEBOOK or (srsTypeAllocForDlBm is TASORCODEBOOK and UE does not support TAS)), then it shall be 0;
  * [CB015122-B]Bits 4-6: numOfSrsPortDlBm shall be set to 0 when usageDlBm is 0, otherwise it is set to the number of antenna ports for SRS transmission (see [11155756](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksxvM_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) according to parameter nrofSrsPorts from srsResource in srsConfig structure: [10975309](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2VAeFfu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).[End CB015122-B]

---

##### 2.5.2.6.2.0-6 SRS Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL Setting IEs of structure srsRtBf (ID: 11180919)

**2.5.2.6.2.0-6.0-4**  (ID: `12726585`)

SRS Receive Request to 5G-L1-UL In eCPRI 7-2e (refer 5G_L2_18130_replaced ([11155228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2432wvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ) 

5G-L2-PS shall send UlData_SrsReceiveReq message to trigger SRS decoding for 5G-L1-UL. 

IF the Sub-Band Beamforming SRS is configured for UE, the UE shall be scheduled in UlData_SrsReceiveReq message as below:

The srsRtBfEnable IE shall be set to ‘true’, and srsBwvEnableIE shall be set to ‘false’

The srsRtBf structure shall be set is the number of Sub-Band Beamforming SRS UEs that are scheduled in current slot.

Below parameters shall be set per SrsRtBf structure ,pls refer to 5G_L1_IF_15277_replaced ([11514438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3Pb_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for the detailed description, ceDumpGranularityInSubbands, SRS CE dump granularity. defaults value LSB0~7=0. LSBbit7, It is filled by rdSampleStoreMethod, refer 5G_UP_ALG_27818_replaced ([11158833](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktFRNfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). LSBbit0~6,it is filled by rdSamplingRateSrsCe, refer 5G_UP_ALG_27822_replaced ([11158844](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktFRN_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 

  1. numOfRtBfUeIndex, Number of UEs are received in current slot with configured as SB_BF_SRS. rtBfUeIndex, LSB bits 0~11 , unique identifier of the SB_BF_SRS UE. it is assigned by 5G-L2-PS, refer 5G_L2_9825_replaced([11155315](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2432z_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9)) MSB bits 0~3, value =1 for RT SB BF UE.
  2. symbolPosition, per UE’s per SRS srsResourceIdentity .
  3. numSrsCyclicShifts, Number of CSs active in the corresponding srsResourceIdentity.
  4. srsSubbandId ,Subband identifier for subband SRS frequency domain position indication.
  5. startPRB , Start PRB of the SB_BF_SRS. startPrb is aligned SB_BF boundary. 5G-L3 shall make sure the is freqDomainShift is even number and the alignment with SB_BF boundary, L2 will not do additional validation protection. Refer 5G_UP_ALG_27068_replaced ([11156577](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks1ZnfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Note, the start PRB should consider freqDomainShift. (same as CB009915) refer 5G_L1_IF_411_replaced([11515854](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR_LP_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Also, the freqDomainPosition has considered for SRS_subbandID calculation.
  6. startPrbLtCoMa, start PRb for LT CoMa. There is no need for sweeping the SB within SRS bandwidth, only contain the middle PRB. (in case of uetype=3 (5G_L1_IF_244_replaced([11514390](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PZvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , the startPrb of srsSuMimo is same with startPrbLtCoMa). And L1 needs the startPrbLtCoMa is even number. Then 5G-L2-PS can set startPrbLtCoMa= startPRB + (SizeSrsSb/2)–( srsSubbandSize/2) . Higher level (CP) shall make sure ( refer 5G_CP_ARC_ALG_14229_replaced([11307007](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Tq5XCvvcEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), sizeSrsSb is not smaller than srsSubbandSize. Where startPrb, current SB BF SRS subband's start PRB. sizeSrsSb: Num PRBs per SRS Subband for subband beamforming, decided by Csrs and Bsrs(the output of SRS adaptation). srsSubbandSize : num PRBs for subband TAS SRS for wideband beamforming, decided by Csrs and Bsrs.
  7. srsBmSubbandIdLtCoMa, there is no need to make sure the startPrbLtCoMa is aligned with srsBmSubbandIdLtCoMa correctly.5G_L2_PS shall set srsBmSubbandIdLtCoMa=rounddown[(startPrbLtCoMa-freqDomainShift)/ srsSubbandSize].where freqDomainShift is from dlSbBfSrsBmConfig during cell setup.
  8. ceOperation, refer 5G_L1_IF_15277_replaced ([11514438](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3Pb_vxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) bitmap, Refer 5G_UP_ALG_13879_replaced([11156605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks2Ao_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_UP_ALG_21817_replaced([11157124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  9.      1. LSB bit0, 5G-L2-PS needs per subband & per Port(T1R4)/Ports(T2R4) of SB BF SRS checking whether it is the first time receiving of current subband of SB BF SRS after this RT Bf UE setup, if Yes, LSBbit 0=1. else then LSBbit0=0.
     2. LSB bit1, refer 5G_UP_ALG_13879_replaced([11156605](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks2Ao_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 5G-L2-PS only check whether the current SB BF SRS is first subband of SB BF SRS, if subbandID=0, then mark as 1. else, then mark as 0.
     3. LSB bit2, 5G-L2-PS only check whether the current SB BF SRS is last subband of SB BF SRS, if subbandID= (numSrsSb– 1), then mark this bit as 1. else , then mark this bit as 0. special case, WB SRS is configured for SB BF UE, then subbandID=0= (numSrsSb– 1), in this cae, LSB bit 1 and LSB bit 2 should both be marked as 1 same time. numSrsSb, number of SRS subbands. refer 5G_L2_IF_115_replaced([10968891](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBKvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
     4. LSB bit3 , L2PS only fill the bit by rdSrsCeOperation refer 5G_UP_ALG_27472_replaced([11158704](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktEDIfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). note, this RD is online modifiable.
     5. LSB bit4, NRBTS.NRCELL.wbSbSrsSwitch.channelStabilityThreshold >0 in cellsetup && the LSB bit 0 =0 ，then L2 shall mark this bit as 1.
  10.      1.         1. LSB bit5, 5G-L2-PS needs checking whether it is the first time receiving of SB BF SRS after this RT Bf UE setup ( no matter the subband and Port). if yes LSB bit 5=1. [CB012971-E]
     2. LSB bit6 , if this subband beamforming UE's SVD value is required, LSB bit6=1, else LSB bit6=0. see [12738349: Singular values from SRS channel](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_9bNh9XjQEfCdZt6bzaG3fw?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for selecting UE.[End CB012971-E]
  11. numOfCorrCalcInfo , The number of RT beamforming UEs that are required to calculate correlation with current RT BF UE. Refer [12444668: Scheduling of APS calculation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_Xeo6oAlfEfCT35inaBGo7g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for UE selection for APS correlation calculation.



Per CorrCalcInfo:

  * rtBfCorrUeIndex, the UE that is required to calculate correlation with current RT BF UE.
  * corrSubbandId, SRS subband identifier for correlation calculation.



Note: According to [11156649: Indication for SRS Covariance Matrices(CoMa) calculation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks2nsPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), if 2 SRS symbol position present in srsSymbolPos[] in [10968891: bfSetup structure content](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UaBKvu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9), for the SB BF UE if srsSubbandSize < 8 then make it as 8.

---

#### 2.5.2.6.3 SRS Receive Response from 5G-L1-UL

##### 2.5.2.6.3.0-1 SRS Receive Response from 5G-L1-UL Reception of UlData_SrsReceiveRespPs (ID: 11180938)

**2.5.2.6.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11180941`)

SRS Receive Response from 5G-L1-UL When UlData_SrsReceiveRespPs message (5G_L1_IF_253_replaced([11514446](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PcfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is received, 5G-L2-PS shall perform SINR long-term averaging as described in 5G_UP_ALG_19742_replaced([11140202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_krsxI_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for IRC gain estimation.

---

##### 2.5.2.6.3.0-2 SRS Receive Response from 5G-L1-UL Reception of UlData_SrsReceiveRespRtBfPs (ID: 11180948)

**2.5.2.6.3.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12438329`)

SRS Receive Response from 5G-L1-UL In eCPRI 7-2e ( see definition in 5G_L2_18130_replaced([11155228](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2432wvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), with actDlSrsSubbandBm = True, when receiving Uldata_SrsReceiveRespRtBfPs (5G_L1_IF_15279_replaced([11514515](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32evvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))),

  * 5G-L2-PS shall store dtx and interferedSrsSubband information , to update the SrsQualityTable per UE. **SRSSubBandID and PortID can be got from SrsReceiveRespRtBfPs**
  * 5G-L2-PS shall update SrsQualityTable per SrsSB’s status to non-initial if all ports of current SrsSB's response are all received, refer 5G_L2_18883_replaced([11171429](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26N6nPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * 5G-L2-PS shall store sinr , ( if SINR measurement is enable , refer 5G_UP_ALG_22633_replaced([11157155](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks6SEvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) , ( SINR is calculated by L1 refer 5G_UP_ALG_26696_replaced([11107622](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kohhW_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_ UP_ALG_13821) and feed for long term filter averaging . Before long term filter averaging ,SINR validation should be done first, also exceptional case should be considered, refer 5G_UP_ALG_22633_replaced([11157155](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks6SEvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
  * 5G-L2-PS shall store correlation if the correlation calculation is enable by CE operation ( refer 5G_L2_9827_replaced([11155365](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_244d1_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) ), before long term filter, the correlation validation should be done first. refer 5G_UP_ALG_21817_replaced([11157124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks5rDvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). the inst_ correlation and inst_SINR should be validated ( validation before average) and averaged between two ports in case of T2R4 case, there are two ports measurement results per response.
  * 5G-L2-PS shall store numInterferedBfSubband to update related PM counter.
  * 5G-L2-PS shall store power and SINR ( if SINR measurement is enable , refer 5G_UP_ALG_22633_replaced([11157155](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ks6SEvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) related measurement results to update related PM counter.



[CB012971-A]

  * 5G-L-PS shall store and update correlationvalue based on [12444681: Maintaining of Long-term APS based correlation](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_jMM4gQlgEfCT35inaBGo7g?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9).



[End CB012971-A]

##### 2.5.2.6.3.0-3 SRS Receive Response from 5G-L1-UL Reception of UlData_SrsReceiveRespBmPs (ID: 11180961)

**2.5.2.6.3.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `13456555`)

SRS Receive Response from 5G-L1-UL With receiving of UlData_SrsReceiveRespBmPs.ignoreBm=True, L2_Ps shall discard this UE's BM response. 

Note: with ignoreBm equal to True, the CovarianceMatrixHorizontal and CovarianceMatrixVertical size shall be with length equal to 1, for detail refer [11514467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ).

[CB015122-A]

When actSrsBmCalcInL1 parameter is set to True (see [10966124](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UMlxPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) or [11153567](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24vT4vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)), then the 5G-L2-PS shall process the coMaStatus (see [11514467](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR32cvvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) for additional references) as follows:

  * When isLongTermCoMaReadyUl is equal to 1, then 5G-L2-PS shall change the UL SRS BM state machine for the UE to SRS_UL_BM_VALID state (see [11153981](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24xwKvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).
  * When isInstCoMaValidUl is equal to 1, then that indicates that a valid UL instantaneous CoMa is received (see [11153992](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24xwLPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), [11154015](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24yXMPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and [11154046](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24yXNfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).
  * [CB015122-B]When isLongTermCoMaReadyDl is equal to 1, then 5G-L2-PS shall change the DL SRS BM state machine for the UE to SRS_DL_BM_VALID state (see [11153981](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24xwKvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).
  * When isInstCoMaValidDl is equal to 1, then that indicates that a valid DL instantaneous CoMa is received (see [11154583](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_240zdPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and [11154651](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_240zfvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)).[End CB015122-B]



[End CB015122-A]

#### 2.5.2.7.2 Transmission of UlData_RimReceiveReq

##### 2.5.2.7.2.0-1 Transmission of UlData_RimReceiveReq UlData_RimReceiveReq message filling (ID: 11180997)

**2.5.2.7.2.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11181013`)

Transmission of UlData_RimReceiveReq IEs sfn, slot are set to the target sfn and NR-slot on air for which the RI measurement is taken.

IE numSubcell is set to 1.

IE subcellId is set to the ID of Primary Subcell.

[Before CB008205-F]

IE msgCountCtrl is set to 0xFF.

[End CB008205-F]

IE numOfUnscheduledRegions is set according to 5G_L2_8455_replaced([11175573](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26tC0vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

IE rimRssiRequest is set to true if the target slot is marked for RI reception (see 5G_L2_8280_replaced([11175424](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26r0qPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) and RI measurement will be performed, else it is set to false.

IE rimRsDetectionRequest is set to true if the target slot is a target for RIM-RS reception (see 5G_L2_11755_replaced([11175442](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26r0rPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), else it is set to false.

IE numOfPrbPerSubBand is set to 6.

##### 2.5.2.7.2.0-3 Transmission of UlData_RimReceiveReq Setting IEs of structure rimRsDetectionConfig (ID: 11181030)

**2.5.2.7.2.0-3.0-2**  (ID: `11181048`)

Transmission of UlData_RimReceiveReq IE numPrb is set according to PsCell_CellSetupReq/PsCell_CellReconfgurationReq.rimRsConfig.numRbForRs (see 5G_L2_9432_replaced([11142710](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_23wccfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_IF_2797_replaced([10970007](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UgH0fu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

IE numOfFreqResource is set according to the size of PsCell_CellSetupReq/PsCell_CellReconfgurationReq.rimRsConfig.startRbForRs.

IE startPRB is set according to PsCell_CellSetupReq/PsCell_CellReconfgurationReq.rimRsConfig.startRbForRs. 

[CB009823-F] IE subCarrierOffset is set according to PsCell_CellSetupReq/PsCell_CellReconfgurationReq.rimRsConfig.rimRsSubCarrierOffset. [End CB009823-F]

IE numCandidateSequences is set to the number of unique sequences requested for RIM-RS detection in the slot (see 5G_UP_ALG_13156_replaced([11161857](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW9_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))).

For each RIM-RS sequence candidate requested in the slot:

IE seqInit is set according to [image-0][image_desc]The image contains a blurry, close-up view of a mathematical expression. The expression appears to be a variable with a bar over it, followed by the subscript "inlr", and then a parenthesis containing the letter "t". The overall impression is that of a scientific or mathematical notation, possibly representing a time-dependent quantity. The colors are muted and the focus is soft, making it difficult to discern fine details.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_6084.001.png[/image_path][/image-0] calculation from 5G_UP_ALG_12629_replaced([11117907](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kqAIBPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

IE nScId is set according to the entry in PsCell_CellSetupReq/PsCell_CellReconfgurationReq.rimRsConfig.rsType1NScId that is being requested for reception.

IE numOfDetectResUnits is set according to number of detection units requested for given sequence (one unit is one symbol on one frequency resource for one sequence).

For each detection resource (one symbol on one frequency resource for one sequence):

IE symbolIndex is set according to the symbol position of requested resource.

IE freqResIndex is set to the index of requested frequency resource as provided in PsCell_CellSetupReq/PsCell_CellReconfgurationReq.rimRsConfig.startRbForRs.

IE numBlankedRegions shall be set to the number of reported blanked PRB regions depending on presence and utilization in the current target slot (see 5G_UP_ALG_16851_replaced([11162029](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktWW_PvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) (those allocations include PRACH, two frequency hops for both common and dedicated PUCCH PRB region, excluding PRBs that were given back for PUSCH allocation).

For each Blanked Region present in the slot (see also 5G_L2_8455_replaced([11175573](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26tC0vvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

IE blankStartPrb is set to the starting PRB of given blanked resource.

IE blankNumPrb is set to the number of PRB of given blanked resource.

#### 2.5.2.7.3 Reception of UlData_RimReceiveRespPs

##### 2.5.2.7.3.0-1 Reception of UlData_RimReceiveRespPs RI measurement handling (ID: 11181085)

**2.5.2.7.3.0-1.0-3**  (ID: `11181104`)

Reception of UlData_RimReceiveRespPs When UlData_RimReceiveRespPs message (see 5G_L1_IF_14752_replaced([11514630](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR4djfvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) is received and received value of IE rimRssiValid is equal to true, 5G-L2-PS shall smooth interference measurement reported by 5G-L1-UL according to 5G_UP_ALG_9340_replaced([11161622](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktVI0_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

[PR792104] Before processing RSSI feedback, 5G-L2-PS shall remap subband indexes received in IE rimRssi from size requested as per IE numOfSubBands and order requested as per IE startPrbPerSubBand in rimAllocationConfig structure (see 5G_L1_IF_14749_replaced([11514607](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR4divvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) of UlData_RimReceiveReq message (see 5G_L1_IF_14748_replaced([11514602](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR4difvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) to corresponding original indexing in relation to the total number of subbands in the cell in ascending order (lower frequency first) starting from 0 (see 5G_UP_ALG_9328_replaced([11161420](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ktUhwfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)), 5G_L2_8282_replaced([11175546](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_26tCyPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))), considering subbands PRB allocation. [End PR792104]

5G-L2-PS shall handle reception of multiple UlData_RimReceiveRespPs messages as a response to single UlData_RimReceiveReq.

#### 2.5.2.8.1 DTX detection

##### 2.5.2.8.1.0-1 DTX detection [Before PR504694] dtx = dtx &amp;&amp; crc; with: crc: either 1 (i.e. OK) or 0 (i.e. NOK) dtx: either 1 (i.e. DTX) or 0 (i.e. nonDTX) '&amp;&amp;': stands for the 'AND' operation [End PR504694] [PR504694] if (crc = NOK) or (dtx = DTX) dtx = DTX else dtx = nonDTX - the values of crc is defined in 5G_L1_5G21A_220; - the values of dtx is defined in 5G_L1_5G21A_222; [End PR504694] CP2 reference: 5G_UP_ALG_22403_replaced( 11187538 ) (ID: 11181143)

###### 2.5.2.9.1.2.0-2 SRS Beam Calculation Request to 5G-L1-UL Setting IEs of UlData_SrsBeamCalcUlReceiveReq (ID: 13456643)

**2.5.2.9.1.2.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `13456649`)

SRS Beam Calculation Request to 5G-L1-UL IEs shall be set according to [13379639](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_XsxbgP9rEfChFrIQm2O4Ew?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), additionally:

The parameter is used to distinguish UEs and proceed the DFT beam selection algorithm in 5G-L1-DU (see [11153978](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kspzZ_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). The maximum value is limited according to [11514405](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_FR3PafvxEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).
  * IE numUlBeamToCalc shall be set based on the value of numberOfRxBeamforming in PsCell_CellSetupReq message (see [10967202](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UTTdPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)) and rdSuUeReceiverSize (see [11114156](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kpiN9vvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)). For additional information see [11154211](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24y-SvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9), [11154431](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_24zlWfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9) and [11154514](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_240MaPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9).

##### 2.5.2.9.1.3 SRS Beam Calculation Response from 5G-L1-UL

###### 2.5.2.9.1.3.0-1 SRS Beam Calculation Response from 5G-L1-UL Reception of UlData_SrsBeamCalcUlReceiveRespPs (ID: 13456660)

**2.5.2.9.1.3.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `13456662`)

## 2.5.3 Interactions with L2-LO

### 2.5.3.0-1 Interactions with L2-LO Document Owner Roosen, Fabienne (Nokia - FR/Paris-Saclay) (ID: 11181152)

### 2.5.3.1 UL MAC PDU Reception Indication

#### 2.5.3.1-1 Reception of LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd

##### 2.5.3.1-1.0-1 Reception of LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd If 5G-L2-PS is triggered by [Before PR675846]5G_L2_8583_replaced( 11146758 )[PR675846]5G_L1L2_FLOW_1870_replaced( 11198042 ) (see also 5G_L2_8583_replaced( 11146758 ))[End PR675846] to send LoCtrl_StopFlowControlReq message (5G_L2_IF_901_replaced( 10984943 )), it shall set logicalChannelIdentity to the same value(s) as received in the triggering message. [PR675846] If 5G-L2-PS is triggered by 5G_L1L2_FLOW_2462_replaced( 11183306 ) to send LoCtrl_StopFlowControlReq message, it shall suspend* scheduling in Scell for given UE. *) Rationale: From 5G-L2-PS PoV the DL Data Transfer Stop procedure (5G_L1L2_FLOW_2366_replaced( 11197896 )) can either stop or suspend the traffic flow and UE scheduling, depending on which other (outer) procedure triggered it (see 5G_L1L2_FLOW_2742_replaced( 11197922 )), and the outer procedure after the stop or suspend may also deactivate or release Scell, or not, and delete the UE context from that Scell, or not. Hence the SW implementation of DL Data Transfer Stop procedure itself in 5G-L2-PS may be generic only to certain extent. This different impact on the UE scheduling in 5G-L2-PS, i.e. either suspend or stop, may not be SCT testable. [End PR675846] (ID: 11181203)

#### 2.5.3.1-2 Reception of LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd

##### 2.5.3.1-2.0-2 Reception of LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd Upon reception of LoCtrl_CcchDataInd  from L2-LO, L2-PS shall take below actions, as required: After the successful MAC CE CRI transmission, and upon reception of LoCtrl_CcchDataInd from L2-LO, indicating the availability and the size (IE sizeOfRrcMsg) of the CCCH data, L2-PS shall execute the procedure specified in 11153402 and below requirements (RRC Setup). [CNI-133878] Upon receiving the indication with IE isRrcReject = TRUE (UE marked as rejected), L2-PS shall (in the following order): Delete corresponding temporary UE context immediately after all the following conditions are met: There are no more data in buffers (the CCCH message has been sent) There are no ongoing DL HARQ processes (to mitigate the issue of CRI sent independently of the CCCH). Indicate the deletion of corresponding temporary UE to L2-LO by sending LoCtrl_DeleteTempUeReq ( 10985706: Release Temporary UE Request ) SFS reference: 11153584 . [End CNI-133878] (ID: 12462112)

#### 2.5.3.1-3 Reception of LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd

##### 2.5.3.1-3.0-3 Reception of LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd Upon reception of LoCtrl_DlBufferStatusInd indicating data availability for SRB1 (logicalChannelIdentity set to 1; DL-DCCH RRC message) is received, L2-PS needs to consider the execution trigger of below procedures. Note: for concrete trigger condition, please check the list SFS/EFS requirement. 5G_UP_ALG_17972_replaced( 11153597 ) "DL-DCCH: RRC reconfiguration or restablishment or reject or resume(with an explicit state of UE dedicated configuration)" and below requirements (RRC RRC Reconfiguration /Re-establishment/Reject/Resume). 5G_L2_22678_replaced( 11170598 ) DL-DCCH RRC Message Delivery Procedure. [CB013742-A] 5G_L2_22365_replaced( 11170588 ) DL-DCCH RRC Complete Detection for RRC Messages Requiring RRC Completion. [End CB013742-A] (ID: 11181232)

#### 2.5.3.1-4 Reception of LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd

##### 2.5.3.1-4.0-3 Reception of LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd When condition defined in 5G_L2_20264_replaced( 11142433 ) is fullfilled and in case actHarqStatusUpdateReqVonr=TRUE: HARQ ACKs for VoNR HARQ NACKs or DTX for initial transmissions with VoNR data possibly multiplexed, OR in case actLatencyPmCount=TRUE (and at the same time rdEnableHarqStatusUpdateReq is set to 1): HARQ ACKs, [CB008600-B] HARQ NACK,  this NACK is sent only when the maximum number of retransmissions has been exhausted, otherwise no send. [End CB008600-B] OR in case actHarqStatusUpdateReqVonr=TRUE and actLatencyPmCount=TRUE (and at the same time rdEnableHarqStatusUpdateReq is set to 1): HARQ ACKs HARQ NACKs or DTX for initial transmissions with VoNR data possibly multiplexed, are received on PUCCH or PUCCH over PUSCH (including also CA scenario), L2-PS shall fill it into LoCtrl_Fr1HarqStatusUpdateReq (5G_L2_IF_6401_replaced( 10985550 )) and LoCtrl_Fr2HarqStatusUpdateReq (5G_L2_IF_6675_replaced( 10985631 )) messages accordingly for FR1 and FR2, and send to L2-LO at the beginning of next DL slot trigger event handling to make sure the information already sent to L2-LO before the corresponding HARQ buffer index reused in new DL scheduling. Moreover, HarqStatusUpdateReq messages shall be sent to L2-LO per Cell group and the destination address of HarqStatusUpdateReq messages shall be same as LoCtrl_PduMuxReq (5G_L2_IF_3458_replaced( 10984546 )) message. (ID: 11181252)

#### 2.5.3.1.1 Reception of LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd

##### 2.5.3.1.1.0-1 Reception of LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd Handling UL Buffer Level Information (ID: 11181166)

**2.5.3.1.1.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `11181175`)

Reception of LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd Upon reception of a LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd 5G-L2-PS shall carry out the evaluation [Before CB008709-A] specified in 5G_UP_ALG_5129_replaced([11203795](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwg_v_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). [CB008709-A] as specified in:

  * 5G_UP_ALG_5129_replaced([11203795](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kwg_v_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for UEs UL transmission buffer utilization,

  * 5G_L2_16389_replaced([11176836](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_262zzvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)) for Slice Aware Scheduler PRB bookkeeping. [End CB008709-A]




Every ueUlBufferInfo element in LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd corresponds to 1 received UL TB (UL MAC PDU). Frame and slot number are valid for all ueUlBufferInfo elements in LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd and indicate the TTI on the air interface when the UL TBs were received successfully. The ueUlBufferInfo elements in LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd can be associated with different UEs or with the same UE. The latter case can happen with UEs with CA. Such UEs may send multiple UL TBs per TTI on different carriers. For simplicity, L2-LO may send only a single ueUlBufferInfo element per LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd, see 5G_L2_6732_replaced([11216782](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2_AT-_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).
