**2.5.3.1.1.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11181184`)

Reception of LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd 5G-L2-PS shall use the harqProcessIndex & absoluteHarqProcessIndex IE from LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd to identify the corresponding HARQ Process.

**2.5.3.1.1.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11181194`)

Reception of LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd During Random Access procedure, upon reception of LoCtrl_UlMacPduReceiveInd with isUlCcchData IE set to TRUE, indicating successful reception of RA Msg3, L2-PS shall add the UE to the pre-scheduler candidate set to initiate scheduling of RA Msg4 MAC PDU (either TC-RNTI or C-RNTI), as specified in 5G_UP_ALG_18004_replaced([11153469](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_ksmwEvvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

#### 2.5.4.7.0-1 EN DSS DL CELL RESOURCE AREA ALLOCATION REQUEST Handling EN DSS DL Cell Resource Area Allocation Request message for M55332C00002 and M55332C00003 counters (ID: 11181307)

**2.5.4.7.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11181311`)

EN DSS DL CELL RESOURCE AREA ALLOCATION REQUEST If DL PRB Allocation Info (CRM_1768) includes Extension 02 (CRM_3688) (5G_UP_ALG_4746_replaced([11172256](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuK2VfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then counters M55332C00002 and M55332C00003 shall be incremented, at each DL slot allocated to NR, as follow:

If Extension 02.Dl Allocation type = “min share”

L2-PS increments M55332C00003 by the

Else if Extension 02.Dl Allocation type = “max share”

L2-PS increments M55332C00002 by one

Else if Extension 02.Dl Allocation type = “min max share”

L2-PS increments M55332C00003 by one

L2-PS increments M55332C00002 by one

#### 2.5.4.7.0-2 EN DSS DL CELL RESOURCE AREA ALLOCATION REQUEST Handling of  'EN DSS Overload State' IE from CRM (ID: 11181316)

**2.5.4.7.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11181322`)

EN DSS DL CELL RESOURCE AREA ALLOCATION REQUEST If superFastOvlHandlEnh is enabled (5G_UP_ALG_28981_replaced([11172330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuLdcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

If 'Extension_03' (CRM_4352) IE is present in 'DL PRB Allocation Info' (CRM_1768):

L2_PS stores received value 'DL PRB Allocation Info'.'Extension_03'.'EN DSS Overload State'

If 'Extension_03' (CRM_4352) IE is not present in 'DL PRB Allocation Info' (CRM_1768):

L2-PS does nothing (latest value received from CRM Overload state kept)

Note: At cell setup, the default value for CRM overload state in L2-PS in 'normal load state'

If superFastOvlHandlEnh is disabled (5G_UP_ALG_28981_replaced([11172330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuLdcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

L2-PS does not check the presence of 'Extension_03' in 'DL PRB Allocation Info' (ignored by L2-PS if present)

### 2.5.4.10 EN DSS DL LOAD INDICATION

### 2.5.4.11 EN DSS DL QoS LOAD INDICATION

#### 2.5.4.11.0-1 EN DSS DL QoS LOAD INDICATION Available PRBs calculation for PDSCH GBR load (ID: 11181354)

**2.5.4.11.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12983552`)

EN DSS DL QoS LOAD INDICATION When explicit GBR Load reporting for DSS is enabled

  * Definitions: 



\- avgGbrPrbLoad(t) =Floor[ nPrb_used(t) * 100 / nPrb_usable(t)] ; where:

\- nPrb_used(t) = number of PRBs assigned for PDSCH GBR bearers only, up to time instant t

\- nPrb_usable (t) = number of PRBs usable by L2-PS for PDSCH for any DRB, up to time instant t

\- t refers to end of LoadIndicationDuration as defined in 5G_L2_100_replaced([11143404](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_230G2fvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

In FDD with PRBPooling enabled, nPrb_usable is determined as:

\- PRBs allocated by the BBRM which are available for DataTransmission are considered as usable (i.e. PRBS used by SIB1, SSB, TRS are excluded).

\- In SF 5 and 9 if allocated to NR, the min (BBRM allocated PRBs, CRM allocated PRBs) shall be considered as usable PRBs.

[CB007372-AA]

If actAsymmetricDss is set to "true', the usable PRBs are the sum of NR dedicated PRBs and PRBs from the LTE shared area which are allocated to NR. And refer to [11172138: DSS DL Load Indication](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuJoUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) [11172167: DSS DL VoNR PRB Load Indicator](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuKPQPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) [11172186: DSS DL GBR PRB Load Indicator](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuKPRPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for specific load computation description.

[End CB007372-AA]

Associated CP2 Requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4729_replaced([11172138](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuJoUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

---

#### 2.5.4.11.0-2 EN DSS DL QoS LOAD INDICATION Available PRBs calculation for PDSCH nGBR nNBR load (ID: 11181363)

**2.5.4.11.0-2.0-2**  (ID: `12983572`)

EN DSS DL QoS LOAD INDICATION The measured nGBR and nNBR load reported to CRM is as below:

Measured nGBR nNBR load = floor(PRBs assigned for PDSCH * 100/total number of usable PRBs )

If actSlowPrbPooling = TRUE, the total number of usable PRBs is calculated as below

  * PRBs allocated by the BBRM which are available for DataTransmission are considered as usable (i.e. PRBS used by SIB1, SSB, TRS are excluded).

  * In SF 5 and 9 if allocated to NR, the min (BBRM allocated PRBs, CRM allocated PRBs) shall be considered as usable PRBs.




[CB007372-AA]

If actAsymmetricDss is set to "true', the usable PRBs are the sum of NR dedicated PRBs and PRBs from the LTE shared area which are allocated to NR. And refer to [11172138: DSS DL Load Indication](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuJoUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for specific load computation description.

**[End CB007372-AA]**

Associated CP2 Requirement 5G_UP_ALG_4729_replaced([11172138](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuJoUPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

#### 2.5.4.11.0-4 EN DSS DL QoS LOAD INDICATION Test mode to generate fake Dl Qos load indication (ID: 11181392)

**2.5.4.11.0-4.0-1**  (ID: `11181401`)

EN DSS DL QoS LOAD INDICATION [image-0][image_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating a timeline with different events and states. The timeline is marked with numbers from 0 to 11, representing "SFN % X". Above each number, there is an upward arrow and the text "measurement period". Below the timeline, there are several rectangular boxes indicating different states or events. From SFN 0 to 1, there is a box labeled "OffsetStartFakeLoad". Below this, a darker blue rectangle spans from SFN 0 to SFN 2. From SFN 2 to SFN 3, there is a box labeled "NbDlloadIndicAt100%". Below this, a lighter blue rectangle spans from SFN 2 to SFN 4, labeled "Fake load 100%". From SFN 4 to SFN 5, there is no specific label in the top row. From SFN 5 to SFN 7, there is a box labeled "NbDlloadIndicAt0%". Below this, a darker blue rectangle spans from SFN 5 to SFN 8, labeled "Fake load 0%". A longer, lighter blue rectangle labeled "Fake loadIndic pattern" spans from SFN 4 to SFN 9. From SFN 8 to SFN 10, there is a box labeled "NbDlloadIndicAt100%". The DL fake load consist of to send periodily EN DSS DL QOS LOAD INDICATION with alternately 100% and 0% load.

The DL fake load start when rdOffsetSartDlFakeLoad (5G_L2_7731_replaced([11188322](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28HYDvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) != 0XFFFF and current SFN mod rdModuloX (5G_L2_7737_replaced([11188353](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28H_HPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = rdOffsetSartDlFakeLoad

Then there is a pattern of:

 rdNbDlLoadIndicAt100Percent (5G_L2_7732_replaced([11188333](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28H_GPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) frame with load set to 100%, follow by,

 rdNbDlLoadIndicAt0Percent (5G_L2_7733_replaced([11188343](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28H_GvvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) frame with load set to 0%,

This pattern is sent until gNB is restarted.

### 2.5.4.12 EN DSS UL QOS LOAD INDICATION

#### 2.5.4.12.0-1 EN DSS UL QOS LOAD INDICATION Available PRBs calculation for PUSCH GBR load (ID: 11181410)

**2.5.4.12.0-1.0-4**  (ID: `12981803`)

EN DSS UL QOS LOAD INDICATION When explicit GBR Load reporting for DSS is enabled

Definitions: 

\- avgGbrPrbLoad(t) =Floor[ nPrb_used(t) * 100/ nPrb_usable(t)] ; where:

**if NIDD:actUlAdaptReTxEnhDss=false**

\- nPrb_used(t) = number of PRBs assigned by L2-PS for initial HARQ Tx PUSCH and GBR bearers only, up to time instant t

\- nPrb_usable(t) = number of PRBs usable by L2-PS for PUSCH for any DRB, up to time instant t

**if NIDD:actUlAdaptReTxEnhDss=true**

\- nPrb_used(t) = sum(i=0...t) (min(nPrbGbr_used(i), nPrb_usableForNewTx(i))

\- nPrb_usable(t) = sum(i=0...t) nPrb_usableForNewTx(i)

\- nPrbGbr_used(i) = number of PRBs assigned by L2-PS for initial HARQ Tx PUSCH and GBR bearers only, in slot i

\- nPrb_usableForNewTx(i) = number of PRBs usable by L2-PS for PUSCH for any DRB for an initial Tx in slot i. The number of usable Prb for initial transmission is considered as specified in 5G_UP_ALG_5173_replaced([11172400](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuMEd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). 

\- t refers to end of LoadIndicationDuration as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_5173_replaced([11172400](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuMEd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If actSlowPrbPooling = TRUE, then min (BBRM allocated PRBs after long PUCCH PRBs removal, CRM allocated PRBs) shall be considered as nPrb_usable.

Associated CP2 Requirement [11172429](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuMEfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9)

[CB007372-AA]

If actAsymmetricDss is set to "true', the usable PRBs are the sum of NR dedicated PRBs and PRBs from the LTE shared area which are allocated to NR. And refer to [11172400: DSS UL Load Indication](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuMEd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) [11172422: DSS UL VoNR PRB Load Indicator](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuMEevvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) [11172429: DSS UL GBR PRB Load Indicator](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuMEfPvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for specific load computation description.

[End CB007372-AA]

---

#### 2.5.4.12.0-2 EN DSS UL QOS LOAD INDICATION Available PRBs calculation for PUSCH nGBR nNBR load (ID: 11181425)

**2.5.4.12.0-2.0-4**  (ID: `12981337`)

EN DSS UL QOS LOAD INDICATION Measured nGBR nNBR load is the ratio between the number of PRBs assigned for PUSCH and the total number of usable PRBs for PUSCH.

If NIDD:actUlAdaptReTxEnhDss=false the number of usable PRBs refers to the current pattern, but the number of PRB used is aligned to the next pattern. Example (current pattern 10 PRBs, next pattern 5 PRBs UL load 50% except if there is some retransmission during transition phase.

if NIDD:actUlAdaptReTxEnhDss=true, the number of usable PRBs and the number of used PRBs are aligned to the next pattern according to requirement 5G_UP_ALG_5173_replaced([11172400](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuMEd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)). Example (current pattern 10 PRBs, next pattern 5 PRBs: UL load is 100% with 5 PRBs transmitted in initial transmissions.)

nGBRnNBRPrbLoad ==Floor[ nPrb_used(t) * 100/ nPrb_usable(t)] ; where:

\- nPrb_used(t) = sum(i=0...t) (min(nPrb_usedInSlot(i), nPrb_usableForNewTx(i)- nPrbGbr_used(i) )

if explicit Gbr Report is requested

\- nPrbGbr_used(i) is defined in 5G_L2_5961_replaced([11181410](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_27Tfu_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

else

-nPrbGbr_used(i) = 0

endif

\- nPrb_usable(t) = sum(i=0...t) nPrb_usableForNewTx(i)

\- nPrb_usedInSlot(i) = number of PRBs assigned by L2-PS in slot i

\- nPrb_usableForNewTx(i) = number of PRBs usable by L2-PS for PUSCH for any DRB for an initial Tx in slot i, as specified 5G_UP_ALG_5173_replaced([11172400](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuMEd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ)).

\- t refers to end of LoadIndicationDuration as defined in 5G_UP_ALG_5173_replaced([11172400](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuMEd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

[CB007372-AA]

If actAsymmetricDss is set to "true', the usable PRBs are the sum of NR dedicated PRBs and PRBs from the LTE shared area which are allocated to NR. And refer to [11172400: DSS UL Load Indication](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuMEd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ?oslc_config.context=https%3A%2F%2Fdn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com%2Fgc%2Fconfiguration%2F9) for specific load computation description.

[End CB007372-AA]

If actSlowPrbPooling = TRUE, then min (BBRM allocated PRBs after long PUCCH PRBs removal, CRM allocated PRBs) is considered as available PRBs.

Associated CP2 Requirement 5G_UP_ALG_5173_replaced([11172400](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuMEd_vSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))

If actPartialSlotUlCceCountDss(5G_L2_IF_122_replaced([10969219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UbPTPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = true

For slot 5 and 9, L2-PS computes the minimum UL CCE needed to have at least one DCI.

If aggregationLevelSelection(5G_L2_IF_122_replaced([10969219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UbPTPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = static

The minimum CCE is defined by dciDedicatedAggregationLevel(5G_L2_IF_122_replaced([10969219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UbPTPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

Else

The minimum CCE is defined by the min value of aggregation level in aggregationLevelList(5G_L2_IF_122_replaced([10969219](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_2UbPTPu6Ee-AqvopbP1qhQ)))

endif

If there is not enough CCE for UL transmission,

The PRB of the UL slot are not considered as available.

Endif 

Endif

---

#### 2.5.4.12.0-3 EN DSS UL QOS LOAD INDICATION Test mode to generate fake Ul Qos load indication (ID: 11181445)

**2.5.4.12.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11181452`)

EN DSS UL QOS LOAD INDICATION [image-0][image_desc]The image is a timeline diagram illustrating different events and states over time, marked by "SFN % X" on the left vertical axis. The horizontal axis represents time, with numerical markers from 0 to 11, each indicating a "measurement period." The diagram shows three main horizontal bands representing different states or indicators. The top band, starting from SFN 1, shows events labeled "OffsetStartFakeLoad" and "NbDlloadIndicAt100%" and "NbDiLoadIndicAt0%". These labels appear at specific measurement periods. The middle band, which spans from SFN 0 to SFN 11, is divided into segments indicating "Fake load 100%" and "Fake load 0%". There's also a longer segment labeled "Fake loadIndic pattern" that overlaps with some of the "Fake load 0%" and "Fake load 100%" segments. The bottom band is a solid blue bar that starts at SFN 0 and extends to SFN 2, labeled "OffsetStartFakeLoad". It then transitions to a lighter blue segment from SFN 2 to SFN 4, labeled "Fake load 100%". From SFN 5 to SFN 7, it's a darker blue segment labeled "Fake load 0%". Finally, from SFN 9 to SFN 11, it's a lighter blue segment labeled "Fake load 100%". The diagram visually represents a sequence of operations or states related to fake load management and load indication over successive measurement periods.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_6164.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

The UL fake load consist of to send periodily EN DSS UL QOS LOAD INDICATION with alternately 100% and 0% load.

The UL fake load start when rdOffsetSartUlFakeLoad (5G_L2_7734_replaced([11188371](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28H_H_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) != 0XFFFF and current SFN mod rdModuloX (5G_L2_7737_replaced([11188353](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28H_HPvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) = rdOffsetSartUlFakeLoad

Then there is a pattern of:

 rdNbUlLoadIndicAt100Percent (5G_L2_7735_replaced([11188382](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28H_K_vTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) frame with load set to 100%, follow by,

 rdNbUlLoadIndicAt0Percent (5G_L2_7736_replaced([11188394](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_28H_LfvTEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) frame with load set to 0%,

This pattern is sent until gNB is restarted.

### 2.5.4.13 EN DSS UL SUBCARRIER RESOURCE ALLOCATION REQUEST

#### 2.5.4.13.0-1 EN DSS UL SUBCARRIER RESOURCE ALLOCATION REQUEST Handling EN DSS UL Subcarrier Resource Allocation Request message with fast allocation (ID: 11181460)

**2.5.4.13.0-1.0-1**  (ID: `11181469`)

EN DSS UL SUBCARRIER RESOURCE ALLOCATION REQUEST When fast allocation is activated (actLteNrDssFastAlloc=true), it might happen that a new UL Subcarrier Resource Allocation Request message comes before the activation time of the previous request message. In this case, the L2PS needs to store the associated information of Ul resource allocation requests (max 3) and erase them once the corresponding Activation Time passes.

Note: with the current definition, the transition phase lasts one radio frame before the activation time, there should be no overlapping between 2 DSS UL allocation transition phases but we could rather have several consecutive transition phases in time, as illustrated in the below example.

[image-0][image_desc]The image is a diagram illustrating a communication protocol between CRM and L2-PS, likely in a wireless communication system. The diagram uses a timeline on the left, with values ranging from 0 to 3.9. Two vertical columns represent CRM and L2-PS. The CRM column shows a sequence of events: \- At time 0, an "UL SUBCARRIER RESOURCE ALLOCATION Request" for "Pattern B" is sent. \- At time 0.5, an "UL SUBCARRIER RESOURCE ALLOCATION Response" is received. \- At time 1.1, another "UL SUBCARRIER RESOURCE ALLOCATION Request" for "Pattern C" is sent. \- At time 1.6, an "UL SUBCARRIER RESOURCE ALLOCATION Response" is received. The L2-PS column shows different patterns and transition phases over time: \- From time 0 to approximately 0.9, "Pattern A" is active. \- From approximately 0.9 to 1.9, a "Transition Phase A->B" occurs. An arrow points from this phase to the text "ACTIVATION TIME For Pattern B". \- From approximately 1.9 to 2.9, a "Transition Phase B->C" occurs, followed by "Pattern B" from approximately 2.9 to 3.9. An arrow points from the start of "Pattern B" to the text "ACTIVATION TIME For Pattern C". \- Below "Pattern B", "Pattern C" is shown starting from approximately 3.9. The diagram visually represents the timing and sequence of resource allocation requests and responses, as well as the activation of different patterns and transition phases within the L2-PS system.[/image_desc][image_path]https://storage.googleapis.com/dng_files/images/HTML_m24dng_5G_L2_Entity_Level_file_6167.001.png[/image_path][/image-0]

The example in .xlsx can be found here: [https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:x:/r/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/FS1TAs-CFAMs/CB/CB007600%20-%20CB007999/CFAM/CB007738%20NR-LTE%20DSS%20Superfast%20coordination/CP3/Figure%20for%20DOORS/7738_A_UlResourceAllocation.xlsx?d=w0d9ecf97afb244aa96f48ecad7d0d041&csf=1&web=1&e=FfZG1E](https://nokia.sharepoint.com/:x:/r/sites/ASCOP/AS%20Documents/FS1TAs-CFAMs/CB/CB007600%20-%20CB007999/CFAM/CB007738%20NR-LTE%20DSS%20Superfast%20coordination/CP3/Figure%20for%20DOORS/7738_A_UlResourceAllocation.xlsx?d=w0d9ecf97afb244aa96f48ecad7d0d041&csf=1&web=1&e=FfZG1E)

---

#### 2.5.4.13.0-2 EN DSS UL SUBCARRIER RESOURCE ALLOCATION REQUEST Handling EN DSS UL Subcarrier Resource Allocation Request message for M55332C01002 and M55332C01003 counters (ID: 11181476)

**2.5.4.13.0-2.0-1**  (ID: `11181481`)

EN DSS UL SUBCARRIER RESOURCE ALLOCATION REQUEST If UL SC Allocation Info (CRM_1119) includes Extension 01 (CRM_3690) (5G_UP_ALG_8379_replaced([11172457](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuMrgfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))) then counters M55332C01002 and M55332C01003 shall be incremented at each UL usable slot allowed as follow:

If Extension 01.Ul Allocation type = “min share”

L2-PS increments M55332C01003 by Nb PRB allocated to NR inside LTE grid( PUSCH and PUCCH PRB)

Else if Extension 01.Ul Allocation type = “max share”

L2-PS increments M55332C01002 by Nb PRB allocated to NR inside LTE grid( PUSCH and PUCCH PRB)

Else if Extension 01.Ul Allocation type = “min max share”

L2-PS increments M55332C01003 by Nb PRB allocated to NR inside LTE grid( PUSCH and PUCCH PRB)

L2-PS increments M55332C01002 by Nb PRB allocated to NR inside LTE grid( PUSCH and PUCCH PRB)

---

#### 2.5.4.13.0-3 EN DSS UL SUBCARRIER RESOURCE ALLOCATION REQUEST Handling of  'EN DSS Overload State' IE from CRM (ID: 11181488)

**2.5.4.13.0-3.0-1**  (ID: `11181494`)

EN DSS UL SUBCARRIER RESOURCE ALLOCATION REQUEST If superFastOvlHandlEnh is enabled (5G_UP_ALG_28981_replaced([11172330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuLdcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

If 'Extension_02' (CRM_4351) IE is present in 'UL SC Allocation Info' (CRM_1119):

L2_PS stores received value 'UL SC Allocation Info'.'Extension_02'.'EN DSS Overload State'

If 'Extension_02' (CRM_4351) IE is not present in 'UL SC Allocation Info' (CRM_1119):

L2-PS does nothing (latest value received from CRM Overload state kept)

Note: At cell setup, the default value for CRM overload state in L2-PS in 'normal load state'

If superFastOvlHandlEnh is disabled (5G_UP_ALG_28981_replaced([11172330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuLdcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):

L2-PS does not check the presence of 'Extension_02' in 'UL SC Allocation Info' (ignored by L2-PS if present)

---

### 2.5.4.14 EN DSS UL SUBCARRIER RESOURCE ALLOCATION RESPONSE

#### 2.5.4.14.0-1 EN DSS UL SUBCARRIER RESOURCE ALLOCATION RESPONSE Filling of 'EN DSS Overload State' IE (ID: 11181505)

**2.5.4.14.0-1.0-2**  (ID: `12817109`)

EN DSS UL SUBCARRIER RESOURCE ALLOCATION RESPONSE If _superFastOvlHandlEnh is enabled (5G_UP_ALG_28981_replaced([11172330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuLdcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):_

L2-PS sets 'Extension_02' (CRM_4351) IE to present in 'UL SC Allocation Info' (CRM_1119)

and L2-PS fills its own overload state [CB014088-B](\[12688465\]\(https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_REod0lXNEfC45IKMrv0u7Q?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9 "https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/bi_reod0lxnefc45ikmrv0u7q?oslc_config.context=https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/gc/configuration/9"))[End CB014088-B] in

'UL SC Allocation Info'.'Extension_02'.'EN DSS Overload State' (independantly from 'EN DSS OVerload State' reception from CRM)

If _superFastOvlHandlEnh is disabled (5G_UP_ALG_28981_replaced([11172330](https://dn-prod.ext.net.nokia.com/rm/resources/BI_kuLdcfvSEe-AqvopbP1qhQ))):_

L2-PS **does not set 'Extension_02' (CRM_4351) IE to present in 'UL SC Allocation Info' (CRM_1119)**

---
